## Psalms 1:1 (id: 919001001)

1Happy is the man who walks not in the advice of the wicked {ones}, and stands not in the pathway of sinners, and sits not in the seat of scoffers,


## Psalms 1:2 (id: 919001002)

2but in the instruction of Yahweh {is} his delight, and in his instruction he meditates day and night.


## Psalms 1:3 (id: 919001003)

3And he is like a tree set to grow on streams of water, which gives its fruit in its season, and its leaf does not wither, and he makes successful all that he does.


## Psalms 1:4 (id: 919001004)

4Not so the wicked {ones}! But {they are} like the chaff that wind chases away.


## Psalms 1:5 (id: 919001005)

5Thus the wicked {ones} will not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous {ones}.


## Psalms 1:6 (id: 919001006)

6For Yahweh knows the way of the righteous {ones}, but the way of the wicked {ones} will perish.


## Psalms 2:1 (id: 919002001)

1Why do nations conspire and peoples plot futilely?


## Psalms 2:2 (id: 919002002)

2The kings of the earth take their stand, and the rulers conspire together against Yahweh and against his anointed,


## Psalms 2:3 (id: 919002003)

3“Let us tear apart their bonds and cast their cords away from us.”


## Psalms 2:4 (id: 919002004)

4He who is sitting in the heavens laughs; the Lord mocks them.


## Psalms 2:5 (id: 919002005)

5Then he will speak to them in his anger and terrify them in his fury,


## Psalms 2:6 (id: 919002006)

6“I myself have poured out my king on Zion, the mountain of my holiness.”


## Psalms 2:7 (id: 919002007)

7I will describe a decree of Yahweh. He said to me, “You are my son! Today I have begotten you.


## Psalms 2:8 (id: 919002008)

8Ask from me, and I will give nations {as} your inheritance and the extremities of the earth {as} your possession.


## Psalms 2:9 (id: 919002009)

9You will break them with an iron rod; like a jar of a potter, you will smash them to pieces.”


## Psalms 2:10 (id: 919002010)

10And now kings, act prudently; be admonished, rulers of the earth.


## Psalms 2:11 (id: 919002011)

11Serve Yahweh with fear and rejoice with trembling.


## Psalms 2:12 (id: 919002012)

12Kiss the son, lest he be angry and you perish in the way, for his anger burns for just a moment. Happy are all seekers of refuge in him.


## Psalms 3:1 (id: 919003001)

1Yahweh, how many my oppressors have become! The risers against me are many.


## Psalms 3:2 (id: 919003002)

2{There are} many sayers about me, “There is no salvation for him in God.” Selah


## Psalms 3:3 (id: 919003003)

3But you, Yahweh, are a shield behind me, my glory, and the lifter up of my head.


## Psalms 3:4 (id: 919003004)

4{With} my voice I call to Yahweh, and he answered me from the hill of his holiness. Selah


## Psalms 3:5 (id: 919003005)

5I laid myself down and slept. I awoke, for Yahweh protects me.


## Psalms 3:6 (id: 919003006)

6I will not fear the multitudes of people who stand against me round about.


## Psalms 3:7 (id: 919003007)

7Rise up, Yahweh! Save me, my God! For you hit all my enemies on the cheek; the teeth of the wicked you break.


## Psalms 3:8 (id: 919003008)

8Salvation {is} of Yahweh. Your blessing {is} on your people. Selah


## Psalms 4:1 (id: 919004001)

1Answer me when I call, God of my righteousness, in distress you relieve me. Be gracious {to} me and hear my prayer.


## Psalms 4:2 (id: 919004002)

2Son of man, until when {will} my glory become shame? {Until when} will you love futility, {until when} will you seek falsehood? Selah


## Psalms 4:3 (id: 919004003)

3But know that Yahweh has set apart the covenantally faithful for himself. Yahweh hears when I call to him.


## Psalms 4:4 (id: 919004004)

4Tremble and do not sin! Meditate in your heart on your bed and be silent. Selah


## Psalms 4:5 (id: 919004005)

5Sacrifice sacrifices of righteousness and trust in Yahweh.


## Psalms 4:6 (id: 919004006)

6Many say, “Who will show us good?” Lift up the light of your face on us Yahweh!


## Psalms 4:7 (id: 919004007)

7You have put joy in my heart more than the time {when} their grain and their new wine abound.


## Psalms 4:8 (id: 919004008)

8In peace I will both lie down and sleep, for you alone, Yahweh, cause me to dwell securely.


## Psalms 5:1 (id: 919005001)

1{To} my words give ear, Yahweh! Understand my murmuring!


## Psalms 5:2 (id: 919005002)

2Listen attentively to the sound of my cry for help, my king and my God, for to you I pray!


## Psalms 5:3 (id: 919005003)

3Yahweh, in the morning you hear my voice. In the morning I prepare for you and watch.


## Psalms 5:4 (id: 919005004)

4For you are not a god pleased with wickedness; evil ones will not sojourn with you.


## Psalms 5:5 (id: 919005005)

5The arrogant will not stand in front of your eyes; you hate all doers of iniquity.


## Psalms 5:6 (id: 919005006)

6You will destroy speakers of falsehood; the man of blood and deceit Yahweh abhors.


## Psalms 5:7 (id: 919005007)

7But I, in the greatness of your covenant faithfulness, I will come into your house; I will bow down toward your temple of holiness in fear.


## Psalms 5:8 (id: 919005008)

8Yahweh, guide me in your righteousness because of my watchers; straighten before my face your path.


## Psalms 5:9 (id: 919005009)

9For there is no firmness in his mouth; their inward being is destruction. An open tomb is their throat; their tongue they make smooth.


## Psalms 5:10 (id: 919005010)

10Make them guilty, God; may they fall due to their schemes! Because of their many transgressions, drive them out, for they rebel against you!


## Psalms 5:11 (id: 919005011)

11But may all refuge seekers in you rejoice; may they shout joyfully to eternity; and may you cover over them; and may lovers of your name exult in you.


## Psalms 5:12 (id: 919005012)

12For you, Yahweh, you bless the righteous, you surround him {with} favor as a shield.


## Psalms 6:1 (id: 919006001)

1Yahweh, not in your nose, rebuke me, and not in your rage, discipline me.


## Psalms 6:2 (id: 919006002)

2Be gracious {to} me, Yahweh, for I am frail! Heal me, Yahweh, for my bones are shaking!


## Psalms 6:3 (id: 919006003)

3And my soul is very disturbed. And you, Yahweh, until when?


## Psalms 6:4 (id: 919006004)

4Turn back, Yahweh! Rescue my soul! Save me for the sake of your covenant faithfulness!


## Psalms 6:5 (id: 919006005)

5For in death, there is no remembrance of you. In Sheol, who will thank you?


## Psalms 6:6 (id: 919006006)

6I am weary with my groaning. During every night, I cause my bed to swim, With my tears, my couch I melt.


## Psalms 6:7 (id: 919006007)

7My eye has wasted away from grief, it advances because of all my adversaries.


## Psalms 6:8 (id: 919006008)

8Turn away from me, all you doers of iniquity, for Yahweh has heard the sound of my sobbing!


## Psalms 6:9 (id: 919006009)

9Yahweh has heard my appeal for mercy, Yahweh accepts my prayer.


## Psalms 6:10 (id: 919006010)

10Let all my enemies be shamed and greatly disturbed. Let them turn back. Let them be shamed {in} an instant.


## Psalms 7:1 (id: 919007001)

1A musical composition of David, which he sang to Yahweh concerning the words of Cush the Benjamite. Yahweh my God, in you I have taken refuge; save me from all my pursuers, and rescue me!


## Psalms 7:2 (id: 919007002)

2Lest he rip my life apart like a lion, tearing apart, and there is no one to rescue.


## Psalms 7:3 (id: 919007003)

3Yahweh my God, if I have done this, if there is wrong on my hands,


## Psalms 7:4 (id: 919007004)

4if I have repaid evil {to} one {who was at} peace with me, or senselessly rescued my adversary,


## Psalms 7:5 (id: 919007005)

5let my enemy pursue my soul and overtake {it}, and let him trample my life to the ground and cause my honor to live in the dust.


## Psalms 7:6 (id: 919007006)

6Arise, Yahweh! In your nose, be lifted with the rage of my adversaries! And wake up for me! You have ordered judgment.


## Psalms 7:7 (id: 919007007)

7And an assembly of peoples surround you, and over it return on high!


## Psalms 7:8 (id: 919007008)

8Yahweh, adjudicate the peoples! Judge me, Yahweh, according to my righteousness and according to my integrity, Most High!


## Psalms 7:9 (id: 919007009)

9May the evil of wicked ones end, and {would} you establish righteous ones. The righteous God examines hearts and kidneys.


## Psalms 7:10 (id: 919007010)

10My shield is with God, the savior of the upright of heart.


## Psalms 7:11 (id: 919007011)

11God is a righteous judge, and a God {who is} indignant on every day.


## Psalms 7:12 (id: 919007012)

12If he does not repent, his sword he will sharpen, his bow he has bent and prepared.


## Psalms 7:13 (id: 919007013)

13and for him he has prepared implements of death, he has made his arrows into burning {arrows}.


## Psalms 7:14 (id: 919007014)

14Behold he is pregnant with wickedness, and he conceives trouble, and he births lies.


## Psalms 7:15 (id: 919007015)

15He digs a pit and hollows it out and falls into the hole he has made.


## Psalms 7:16 (id: 919007016)

16His trouble returns on his head, and his violence comes down on the top of his head.


## Psalms 7:17 (id: 919007017)

17I will thank Yahweh according to his righteousness, and sing praise to the name of Yahweh, the Most High.


## Psalms 8:1 (id: 919008001)

1For the chief musician; set to the gittith {style}. A psalm of David. Yahweh, our Lord, how magnificent is your name in all the earth, {you} whose splendor is bestowed on the heavens.


## Psalms 8:2 (id: 919008002)

2Out of the mouth of children and nursing ones you have established strength because of your adversaries, to cause the enemy and avenger to end.


## Psalms 8:3 (id: 919008003)

3When I look at your heavens, the work of your fingers, the moon and the stars, which you have set in place,


## Psalms 8:4 (id: 919008004)

4what is mankind that you remember him, or the son of man that you pay attention to him?


## Psalms 8:5 (id: 919008005)

5Yet you have made him to lack little from the heavenly beings, and {with} glory and majesty you have crowned him.


## Psalms 8:6 (id: 919008006)

6You made him rule over the works of your hands, everything you have put under his feet:


## Psalms 8:7 (id: 919008007)

7sheep and oxen—all of them, and also the animals of the field,


## Psalms 8:8 (id: 919008008)

8birds of the sky, and the fish of the sea, the passers {on} the paths of the seas.


## Psalms 8:9 (id: 919008009)

9Yahweh, our Lord, how magnificent is your name in all the earth!


## Psalms 9:1 (id: 919009001)

1For the chief musician; set to Muth Labben style. A psalm of David. I will thank Yahweh with all my heart, I will recount all your wonders.


## Psalms 9:2 (id: 919009002)

2I will rejoice and exult in you, I will sing praise to your name, Most High!


## Psalms 9:3 (id: 919009003)

3When my enemies turn back, they stumble and perish from your face.


## Psalms 9:4 (id: 919009004)

4For you have done my justice and my claim; you have sat on your throne, a judge of righteousness!


## Psalms 9:5 (id: 919009005)

5You rebuked nations; you destroyed the wicked; you blotted out their name forever and ever.


## Psalms 9:6 (id: 919009006)

6The enemy are finished—desolation forever, and you pulled up cities. {As for} them, their remembrance perished,


## Psalms 9:7 (id: 919009007)

7but Yahweh will sit forever. He has established his throne for justice,


## Psalms 9:8 (id: 919009008)

8as for him, he will judge the world with righteousness, and he will adjudicate for the peoples with fairness.


## Psalms 9:9 (id: 919009009)

9And may Yahweh be a secure height for the oppressed, a secure height for times with distress.


## Psalms 9:10 (id: 919009010)

10And may the knowers of your name trust in you, because you have not abandoned the seekers of you, Yahweh.


## Psalms 9:11 (id: 919009011)

11Sing praises to Yahweh, the sitter {in} Zion! Declare his deeds among the peoples


## Psalms 9:12 (id: 919009012)

12for the seeker of {vengeance for} bloodshed remembered them, he does not forget the cry of the afflicted ones.


## Psalms 9:13 (id: 919009013)

13Have mercy on me, Yahweh! See my affliction from my haters, O lifter of me from the gates of death,


## Psalms 9:14 (id: 919009014)

14in order that I might recount all your praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion. I will rejoice in your salvation!


## Psalms 9:15 (id: 919009015)

15The nations have sunk down into the pit they made; their foot is caught in the net that they hid.


## Psalms 9:16 (id: 919009016)

16Yahweh has revealed himself, he has done justice; the wicked is ensnared by the work of his hands. 


## Psalms 9:17 (id: 919009017)

17Wicked ones will turn back to Sheol, all nations are forgetful of God.


## Psalms 9:18 (id: 919009018)

18But the needy will not be forgotten eternally, {nor} will the hope of the afflicted perish forever.


## Psalms 9:19 (id: 919009019)

19Arise, Yahweh! Let not humanity prevail! On your face let nations be judged.


## Psalms 9:20 (id: 919009020)

20Put terror to them, Yahweh! May nations know they are human. 


## Psalms 10:1 (id: 919010001)

1Why, Yahweh, do you stand far\-off? {Why} do you hide in times of trouble?


## Psalms 10:2 (id: 919010002)

2In arrogance, the wicked hotly pursue the afflicted; may they be caught by the schemes that they have planned.


## Psalms 10:3 (id: 919010003)

3Indeed, the wicked boasts about the desires of his soul and he blesses the robber; he despises Yahweh.


## Psalms 10:4 (id: 919010004)

4According to the haughtiness of his nose the wicked seeks not; All his thoughts {are}, “{There is} no God.”


## Psalms 10:5 (id: 919010005)

5His ways endure at every time; your judgements are high from in front of him; {as for} all his enemies, he snorts at them.


## Psalms 10:6 (id: 919010006)

6He says in his heart, “I will not be shaken; to generation and generation {it is I} who {will} not {be} in distress.”


## Psalms 10:7 (id: 919010007)

7His mouth is full of curses and lies and oppression; under his tongue are mischief and evil.


## Psalms 10:8 (id: 919010008)

8He sits in ambush near the villages; in the secret places he murders the innocent; his eyes stealthily watch for a helpless person.


## Psalms 10:9 (id: 919010009)

9He ambushes in a secret place like a lion in cover; he ambushes to seize the afflicted. He seizes the afflicted by pulling in his net.


## Psalms 10:10 (id: 919010010)

10He stoops, crouches, and unfortunate people fall by his power.


## Psalms 10:11 (id: 919010011)

11He says in his heart, “God has forgotten; he has hidden his face; to perpetuity he sees not.”


## Psalms 10:12 (id: 919010012)

12Arise, Yahweh! God, lift up your hand! Do not forget the afflicted ones.


## Psalms 10:13 (id: 919010013)

13Why does the wicked despise God? He says in his heart, “You will not seek.”


## Psalms 10:14 (id: 919010014)

14You have seen! Indeed, you notice mischief and vexation to take {it} in your hand. The helpless person entrusts {himself} to you; as for the orphan you, {even} you, are {his} helper.


## Psalms 10:15 (id: 919010015)

15Break the arm of wicked and evil {people}. May it seek his wickedness, {but} not find {it}.


## Psalms 10:16 (id: 919010016)

16Yahweh is king forever and ever; the nations have perished from his land.


## Psalms 10:17 (id: 919010017)

17The desire of afflicted ones, you have heard, Yahweh; you strengthen their heart, you cause your ear to attend:


## Psalms 10:18 (id: 919010018)

18to judge the orphan and oppressed; {that} mankind {who is} from the earth will never again terrify.


## Psalms 11:1 (id: 919011001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. To the director. Of David. In Yahweh I have taken refuge. How will you say to myself, “Flutter {away like} a bird to your mountain”?


## Psalms 11:2 (id: 919011002)

2For see! The wicked prepare their bows. They make ready their arrows on the strings to shoot in the darkness at the upright in heart.


## Psalms 11:3 (id: 919011003)

3For if the foundations are ruined, what can the righteous do?


## Psalms 11:4 (id: 919011004)

4Yahweh is in his holy temple; his eyes watch, his eyes examine the children of mankind.


## Psalms 11:5 (id: 919011005)

5Yahweh examines both the righteous and the wicked, but he hates those who love to do violence.


## Psalms 11:6 (id: 919011006)

6He rains burning coals and brimstone upon the wicked; a scorching wind will be their portion from his cup!


## Psalms 11:7 (id: 919011007)

7For Yahweh is righteous, and he loves righteousness; the upright will see his face.


## Psalms 12:1 (id: 919012001)

1For the chief musician; set to the Sheminith. A psalm of David. Help, Yahweh, for the faithful ones have disappeared; those who have integrity have vanished from the children of men.


## Psalms 12:2 (id: 919012002)

2Everyone says empty words to his neighbor; everyone speaks with flattering lips and a double heart.


## Psalms 12:3 (id: 919012003)

3Yahweh, cut off all flattering lips, every tongue declaring great things.


## Psalms 12:4 (id: 919012004)

4These are those who have said, “With our tongues will we prevail. When our lips speak, who can be master over us?”


## Psalms 12:5 (id: 919012005)

5“Because of violence against the poor, because of the groans of the needy, I will arise,” says Yahweh. “I will provide the safety for which they long.”


## Psalms 12:6 (id: 919012006)

6The words of Yahweh are pure words, like silver purified in a furnace on the earth, refined seven times.


## Psalms 12:7 (id: 919012007)

7You are Yahweh! You keep them. You preserve the godly people from this wicked generation and forever.


## Psalms 12:8 (id: 919012008)

8The wicked walk on every side when evil is exalted among the children of mankind.


## Psalms 13:1 (id: 919013001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. How long, Yahweh, will you keep forgetting about me? How long will you hide your face from me?


## Psalms 13:2 (id: 919013002)

2How long must I worry and have grief in my heart all day? How long will my enemy triumph over me?


## Psalms 13:3 (id: 919013003)

3Look at me and answer me, Yahweh my God! Give light to my eyes, or I will sleep in death.


## Psalms 13:4 (id: 919013004)

4Do not let my enemy say, “I have defeated him,” so that my enemy may not say, “I have prevailed over my adversary”; otherwise, my enemies will rejoice when I am brought down.


## Psalms 13:5 (id: 919013005)

5But I have trusted in your covenant faithfulness; my heart rejoices in your salvation.


## Psalms 13:6 (id: 919013006)

6I will sing to Yahweh because he has treated me very generously.


## Psalms 14:1 (id: 919014001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. To the chief musician A psalm of DavidA A fool says in his heart, “There is no God.” They are corrupt and have done abominable iniquity; there is no one who does good.


## Psalms 14:2 (id: 919014002)

2Yahweh looks down from heaven on the children of mankind to see if there are any who understand, who seek after him.


## Psalms 14:3 (id: 919014003)

3They have all turned away. Together they have become corrupt. There is no one who does good, no, not one.


## Psalms 14:4 (id: 919014004)

4Do they not know anything, those who commit iniquity, those who eat up my people as they eat bread, but who do not call on Yahweh?


## Psalms 14:5 (id: 919014005)

5They tremble with dread, for God is with the righteous assembly!


## Psalms 14:6 (id: 919014006)

6You want to humiliate the poor person even though Yahweh is his refuge.


## Psalms 14:7 (id: 919014007)

7Oh, that the salvation of Israel would come from Zion! When Yahweh brings back his people from the captivity, then Jacob will rejoice and Israel will be glad!


## Psalms 15:1 (id: 919015001)

1A psalm of David. To the chief musician A psalm of David Yahweh, who may stay in your tabernacle? Who may live on your holy hill?


## Psalms 15:2 (id: 919015002)

2Whoever walks blamelessly, does what is right and speaks truth from his heart.


## Psalms 15:3 (id: 919015003)

3He does not slander with his tongue, he does not harm others, and he does not insult his neighbor.


## Psalms 15:4 (id: 919015004)

4The worthless person is despised in his eyes, but he honors those who fear Yahweh. He swears to his own disadvantage and does not take back his promises.


## Psalms 15:5 (id: 919015005)

5He does not charge interest when he lends money. He does not take bribes to testify against the innocent. He who does these things will never be shaken.


## Psalms 16:1 (id: 919016001)

1A michtam of David. A song of David Protect me, God, for I take refuge in you.


## Psalms 16:2 (id: 919016002)

2You say to Yahweh, “You are my Lord; my goodness is nothing apart from you.


## Psalms 16:3 (id: 919016003)

3As for the holy ones who are in the land, they are noble people; all my delight is in them.


## Psalms 16:4 (id: 919016004)

4Their troubles will increase, those who seek out other gods. I will not pour out their drink offerings of blood or lift up their names with my lips.


## Psalms 16:5 (id: 919016005)

5Yahweh is the portion of my inheritance and my cup. You hold onto my lot.


## Psalms 16:6 (id: 919016006)

6Measuring lines have been laid for me in pleasant places; surely a pleasing inheritance is mine.


## Psalms 16:7 (id: 919016007)

7I will bless Yahweh, who counsels me; even at night my mind instructs me.


## Psalms 16:8 (id: 919016008)

8I set Yahweh before me continually, for he is at my right hand, I will not be shaken.


## Psalms 16:9 (id: 919016009)

9Therefore my heart rejoices, and my glory is joyful. Surely my flesh will dwell in security.


## Psalms 16:10 (id: 919016010)

10For you will not abandon my soul to Sheol. You will not let your faithful one see the pit.


## Psalms 16:11 (id: 919016011)

11You teach me the path of life; abundant joy is in your face; pleasures are at your right hand forever!”


## Psalms 17:1 (id: 919017001)

1A prayer of David. A prayer of David Listen to my plea for justice, Yahweh; pay attention to my call for help! Give ear to my prayer from lips without deceit.


## Psalms 17:2 (id: 919017002)

2Let my vindication come from your presence; let your eyes see what is right!


## Psalms 17:3 (id: 919017003)

3If you test my heart, if you come to me in the night, you will purify me and will not find any evil plans; my mouth will not transgress.


## Psalms 17:4 (id: 919017004)

4As for the deeds of mankind, it is at the word of your lips that I have kept myself from the ways of the lawless.


## Psalms 17:5 (id: 919017005)

5My steps have held firmly to your tracks; my feet have not slipped.


## Psalms 17:6 (id: 919017006)

6I call to you, for you answer me, God; turn your ear to me and listen when I speak.


## Psalms 17:7 (id: 919017007)

7Show your covenant faithfulness in a wonderful way, you who save by your right hand those who take refuge in you from their enemies!


## Psalms 17:8 (id: 919017008)

8Protect me like the apple of your eye; hide me under the shadow of your wings


## Psalms 17:9 (id: 919017009)

9from the presence of the wicked ones who assault me, my enemies who surround me.


## Psalms 17:10 (id: 919017010)

10They have no mercy on anyone; their mouths speak with pride.


## Psalms 17:11 (id: 919017011)

11They have surrounded my steps. They set their eyes to strike me to the ground.


## Psalms 17:12 (id: 919017012)

12They are like a lion eager for a victim, like a young lion crouching in hidden places.


## Psalms 17:13 (id: 919017013)

13Arise, Yahweh! Attack them! Throw them down on their faces! Rescue my life from the wicked by your sword!


## Psalms 17:14 (id: 919017014)

14Rescue me from men by your hand, Yahweh, from men of this world whose prosperity is in this life alone! You will fill the bellies of your treasured ones with riches; they will have many children and will leave their wealth to their children.


## Psalms 17:15 (id: 919017015)

15As for me, I will see your face in righteousness; I will be satisfied, when I awake, with a sight of you.


## Psalms 18:1 (id: 919018001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David, the servant of Yahweh, when he sang to Yahweh the words of this song on the day that Yahweh rescued him from the hand of all his enemies and from the hand of Saul. He sang: I love you, Yahweh, my strength.


## Psalms 18:2 (id: 919018002)

2Yahweh is my rock, my fortress, the one who brings me to safety; he is my God, my rock; I take refuge in him. He is my shield, the horn of my salvation, and my stronghold.


## Psalms 18:3 (id: 919018003)

3I will call on Yahweh who is worthy to be praised, and I will be saved from my enemies.


## Psalms 18:4 (id: 919018004)

4The cords of death surrounded me, and the rushing waters of worthlessness overwhelmed me.


## Psalms 18:5 (id: 919018005)

5The cords of Sheol surrounded me; the snares of death trapped me.


## Psalms 18:6 (id: 919018006)

6In my distress I called to Yahweh; I called for help to my God. He heard my voice from his temple; my call for help went into his presence; it went into his ears.


## Psalms 18:7 (id: 919018007)

7Then the earth shook and trembled; the foundations of the mountains also trembled and were shaken because God was angry.


## Psalms 18:8 (id: 919018008)

8Smoke went up from out of his nostrils, and blazing fire came out of his mouth. Coals were ignited by it.


## Psalms 18:9 (id: 919018009)

9He opened the heavens and came down, and thick darkness was under his feet.


## Psalms 18:10 (id: 919018010)

10He rode on a cherub and flew; he glided on the wings of the wind.


## Psalms 18:11 (id: 919018011)

11He made darkness a tent around him, heavy rainclouds in the skies.


## Psalms 18:12 (id: 919018012)

12Hailstones and coals of fire fell from the lightning before him.


## Psalms 18:13 (id: 919018013)

13Yahweh thundered in the heavens! The voice of the Most High shouted hailstones and coals of fire


## Psalms 18:14 (id: 919018014)

14He shot his arrows and scattered his enemies; many lightning bolts dispersed them.


## Psalms 18:15 (id: 919018015)

15Then the water channels appeared; the foundations of the world were laid bare at your rebuke, Yahweh, at the blast of the breath of your nostrils.


## Psalms 18:16 (id: 919018016)

16He reached down from above; he took hold of me! He pulled me out of the surging water.


## Psalms 18:17 (id: 919018017)

17He rescued me from my strong enemy, from those who hated me, for they were too strong for me.


## Psalms 18:18 (id: 919018018)

18They came against me on the day of my distress but Yahweh was my support!


## Psalms 18:19 (id: 919018019)

19He set me free in a wide open place; he saved me because he was pleased with me.


## Psalms 18:20 (id: 919018020)

20Yahweh has rewarded me because of my righteousness; he has restored me because my hands were clean.


## Psalms 18:21 (id: 919018021)

21For I have kept the ways of Yahweh and have not wickedly turned away from my God.


## Psalms 18:22 (id: 919018022)

22For all his righteous decrees have been before me; as for his statutes, I have not turned away from them.


## Psalms 18:23 (id: 919018023)

23I have also been innocent before him, and I have kept myself from sin.


## Psalms 18:24 (id: 919018024)

24Therefore Yahweh has restored me because of my righteousness, because my hands were clean before his eyes.


## Psalms 18:25 (id: 919018025)

25To the one who is faithful, you show yourself to be faithful; to a man who is blameless, you show yourself to be blameless.


## Psalms 18:26 (id: 919018026)

26To anyone who is pure, you show yourself pure; but you are clever toward anyone who is twisted.


## Psalms 18:27 (id: 919018027)

27For you save afflicted people, but you bring down those with proud, uplifted eyes!


## Psalms 18:28 (id: 919018028)

28For you give light to my lamp; Yahweh my God lights up my darkness.


## Psalms 18:29 (id: 919018029)

29For by you I can run over a barricade; by my God I can leap over a wall.


## Psalms 18:30 (id: 919018030)

30As for God—his way is perfect! The word of Yahweh is pure! He is a shield to everyone who takes refuge in him.


## Psalms 18:31 (id: 919018031)

31For who is God except Yahweh? Who is a rock except our God?


## Psalms 18:32 (id: 919018032)

32It is God who puts strength on me like a belt, who places the blameless person on his path.


## Psalms 18:33 (id: 919018033)

33He makes my feet swift like a deer and places me on the heights!


## Psalms 18:34 (id: 919018034)

34He trains my hands for war and my arms to bend a bow of bronze.


## Psalms 18:35 (id: 919018035)

35You have given me the shield of your salvation. Your right hand has supported me, and your favor has made me great.


## Psalms 18:36 (id: 919018036)

36You have made a wide place for my feet beneath me so that my feet have not slipped.


## Psalms 18:37 (id: 919018037)

37I pursued my enemies and caught them; I did not turn back until they were destroyed.


## Psalms 18:38 (id: 919018038)

38I smashed them so that they were unable to rise; they have fallen under my feet.


## Psalms 18:39 (id: 919018039)

39For you put strength on me like a belt for battle; you put under me those who rise up against me.


## Psalms 18:40 (id: 919018040)

40You gave me the back of my enemies’ necks; I annihilated those who hated me.


## Psalms 18:41 (id: 919018041)

41They called for help, but no one saved them; they called out to Yahweh, but he did not answer them.


## Psalms 18:42 (id: 919018042)

42I beat them into fine pieces like dust before the wind; I threw them out like mud in the streets.


## Psalms 18:43 (id: 919018043)

43You rescued me from the disputes of people. You have made me the head over nations. People that I have not known serve me.


## Psalms 18:44 (id: 919018044)

44As soon as they heard of me, they obeyed me; foreigners were forced to bow to me.


## Psalms 18:45 (id: 919018045)

45The foreigners came trembling out of their strongholds.


## Psalms 18:46 (id: 919018046)

46Yahweh lives; may my rock be praised. May the God of my salvation be exalted.


## Psalms 18:47 (id: 919018047)

47He is the God who executes vengeance for me, who subdues the nations under me.


## Psalms 18:48 (id: 919018048)

48I am set free from my enemies! Indeed, you lifted me above the ones who rose against me! You rescued me from violent men.


## Psalms 18:49 (id: 919018049)

49Therefore I will give thanks to you, Yahweh, among the nations; I will sing praises to your name!


## Psalms 18:50 (id: 919018050)

50God gives great victory to his king, and he shows his covenant loyalty to his anointed one, to David and to his descendants forever.


## Psalms 19:1 (id: 919019001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. The heavens declare the glory of God, and the skies make his handiwork known!


## Psalms 19:2 (id: 919019002)

2Day after day speech pours out; night after night it reveals knowledge.


## Psalms 19:3 (id: 919019003)

3There is no speech or spoken words; their voice is not heard.


## Psalms 19:4 (id: 919019004)

4Yet their words go out over all the earth, and their speech to the end of the world. He has pitched a tent for the sun among them.


## Psalms 19:5 (id: 919019005)

5The sun is like a bridegroom coming out of his chamber and like a strong man who rejoices when he runs his race.


## Psalms 19:6 (id: 919019006)

6The sun rises from the one horizon and crosses the sky to the other; nothing escapes its heat.


## Psalms 19:7 (id: 919019007)

7The law of Yahweh is perfect, restoring the soul; the testimony of Yahweh is reliable, making the simple wise.


## Psalms 19:8 (id: 919019008)

8The instructions of Yahweh are right, making the heart glad; the commandment of Yahweh is pure, bringing light to the eyes.


## Psalms 19:9 (id: 919019009)

9The fear of Yahweh is pure, enduring forever; the righteous decrees of Yahweh are true and altogether right!


## Psalms 19:10 (id: 919019010)

10They are of greater value than gold, even more than much fine gold; they are sweeter than honey and the dripping honey from the honeycomb.


## Psalms 19:11 (id: 919019011)

11Yes, by them your servant is warned; in obeying them there is great reward.


## Psalms 19:12 (id: 919019012)

12Who can discern all his own errors? Cleanse me from hidden faults.


## Psalms 19:13 (id: 919019013)

13Keep your servant also from arrogant sins; let them not rule over me. Then I will be perfect, and I will be innocent from many transgressions.


## Psalms 19:14 (id: 919019014)

14May the words of my mouth and the thoughts of my heart be acceptable in your sight, Yahweh, my rock and my redeemer.


## Psalms 20:1 (id: 919020001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. May Yahweh help you in the day of trouble; may the name of the God of Jacob protect you


## Psalms 20:2 (id: 919020002)

2and send help from the holy place to support you from Zion.


## Psalms 20:3 (id: 919020003)

3May he call to mind all your offerings and accept your burnt sacrifice. 


## Psalms 20:4 (id: 919020004)

4May he grant you your heart’s desire and fulfill all your plans.


## Psalms 20:5 (id: 919020005)

5Then we will rejoice in your victory, and, in the name of our God, we will raise banners. May Yahweh grant all your petitions.


## Psalms 20:6 (id: 919020006)

6Now I know that Yahweh will rescue his anointed one; he will answer him from his holy heaven with the strength of his right hand that can rescue him.


## Psalms 20:7 (id: 919020007)

7These trust in chariots and others in horses, but we will remember the name of Yahweh our God.


## Psalms 20:8 (id: 919020008)

8They will be brought down and fall, but we will rise and stand upright!


## Psalms 20:9 (id: 919020009)

9Yahweh, rescue the king; help us when we call.


## Psalms 21:1 (id: 919021001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. The king rejoices in your strength, Yahweh! How greatly he rejoices in the salvation you provide!


## Psalms 21:2 (id: 919021002)

2You have given him his heart’s desire and have not held back the request of his lips. Selah


## Psalms 21:3 (id: 919021003)

3For you bring him rich blessings; you placed on his head a crown of purest gold.


## Psalms 21:4 (id: 919021004)

4He asked you for life; you gave it to him; you gave him the length of his days forever and ever.


## Psalms 21:5 (id: 919021005)

5His glory is great because of your victory; you have bestowed on him splendor and majesty.


## Psalms 21:6 (id: 919021006)

6For you grant him lasting blessings; you make him glad with the joy of your presence.


## Psalms 21:7 (id: 919021007)

7For the king trusts in Yahweh; through the covenant faithfulness of the Most High he will not be moved.


## Psalms 21:8 (id: 919021008)

8Your hand will seize all your enemies; your right hand will seize those who hate you.


## Psalms 21:9 (id: 919021009)

9At the time of your anger, you will burn them up as in a fiery furnace. Yahweh will consume them in his wrath, and the fire will devour them.


## Psalms 21:10 (id: 919021010)

10You will destroy their offspring from the earth and their descendants from among the human race.


## Psalms 21:11 (id: 919021011)

11For they intended evil against you; they conceived a plot with which they will not succeed!


## Psalms 21:12 (id: 919021012)

12For you will turn them back; you will draw your bow before them.


## Psalms 21:13 (id: 919021013)

13Be exalted, Yahweh, in your strength; we will sing and praise your power.


## Psalms 22:1 (id: 919022001)

1For the chief musician; set to “The rhythm of the deer.” A psalm of David. My God, my God, why have you abandoned me? Why are you so far from saving me and far from the words of my anguish?


## Psalms 22:2 (id: 919022002)

2My God, I cry out in the daytime, but you do not answer, and at night I am not silent!


## Psalms 22:3 (id: 919022003)

3Yet you are holy; you sit as king with the praises of Israel.


## Psalms 22:4 (id: 919022004)

4Our ancestors trusted in you; they trusted in you, and you rescued them.


## Psalms 22:5 (id: 919022005)

5They cried to you and they were rescued. They trusted in you and were not disappointed.


## Psalms 22:6 (id: 919022006)

6But I am a worm and not a man, a disgrace to humanity and despised by the people.


## Psalms 22:7 (id: 919022007)

7All those who see me taunt me; they mock me; they shake their heads at me.


## Psalms 22:8 (id: 919022008)

8They say, “He trusts in Yahweh; let Yahweh rescue him. Let him rescue him, for he delights in him.”


## Psalms 22:9 (id: 919022009)

9For you brought me from the womb; you made me trust you when I was on my mother’s breasts.


## Psalms 22:10 (id: 919022010)

10I have been thrown on you from the womb; you are my God since I was in my mother’s womb!


## Psalms 22:11 (id: 919022011)

11Do not be far away from me, for trouble is near; there is no one to help.


## Psalms 22:12 (id: 919022012)

12Many bulls surround me; strong bulls of Bashan surround me.


## Psalms 22:13 (id: 919022013)

13They open their mouths wide against me like a roaring lion ripping its victim.


## Psalms 22:14 (id: 919022014)

14I am being poured out like water, and all my bones are dislocated. My heart is like wax; it melts away within my inner parts.


## Psalms 22:15 (id: 919022015)

15My strength has dried up like a piece of pottery; my tongue sticks to the roof of my mouth. You have laid me in the dust of death.


## Psalms 22:16 (id: 919022016)

16For dogs have surrounded me; a company of evildoers has encircled me; they have pierced my hands and my feet.


## Psalms 22:17 (id: 919022017)

17I can count all my bones. They look and stare at me.


## Psalms 22:18 (id: 919022018)

18They divide my garments among themselves, they cast lots for my clothes.


## Psalms 22:19 (id: 919022019)

19Do not be far away, Yahweh; please hurry to help me, my strength!


## Psalms 22:20 (id: 919022020)

20Rescue my soul from the sword, my only life from the claws of wild dogs.


## Psalms 22:21 (id: 919022021)

21Save me from the lion’s mouth; rescue me from the horns of the wild oxen.


## Psalms 22:22 (id: 919022022)

22I will declare your name to my brothers; in the midst of the assembly I will praise you.


## Psalms 22:23 (id: 919022023)

23You who fear Yahweh, praise him! All you descendants of Jacob, honor him! Stand in awe of him, all you descendants of Israel!


## Psalms 22:24 (id: 919022024)

24For he has not despised or abhorred the suffering of the afflicted one; Yahweh has not hidden his face from him; when the afflicted one cried to him, he heard.


## Psalms 22:25 (id: 919022025)

25My praise will be because of you in the great assembly; I will fulfill my vows before those who fear him.


## Psalms 22:26 (id: 919022026)

26The oppressed will eat and be satisfied; those who seek Yahweh will praise him. May your hearts live forever.


## Psalms 22:27 (id: 919022027)

27All the peoples of the earth will remember and turn to Yahweh; all the families of the nations will bow down before you.


## Psalms 22:28 (id: 919022028)

28For the kingdom is Yahweh’s; he is the ruler over the nations.


## Psalms 22:29 (id: 919022029)

29All the prosperous people of the earth will feast and will worship; all those who are descending into the dust will bow before him, those who cannot preserve their own lives.


## Psalms 22:30 (id: 919022030)

30A generation to come will serve him; they will tell the next generation of the Lord.


## Psalms 22:31 (id: 919022031)

31They will come and tell of his righteousness; they will tell to a people not yet born what he has done!


## Psalms 23:1 (id: 919023001)

1A psalm of David. \[A Psalm of David] Yahweh is my shepherd; I will lack nothing.


## Psalms 23:2 (id: 919023002)

2He makes me to lie down in green pastures; he leads me beside tranquil water.


## Psalms 23:3 (id: 919023003)

3He brings back my life; he guides me along right paths for the sake of his name.


## Psalms 23:4 (id: 919023004)

4Even though I walk through a valley of darkest shadow, I will not fear harm since you are with me; your rod and your staff, they comfort me.


## Psalms 23:5 (id: 919023005)

5You prepare a table before me in the presence of my enemies; you have anointed my head with oil; my cup runs over.


## Psalms 23:6 (id: 919023006)

6Surely goodness and covenant faithfulness will pursue me all the days of my life; and I will live in the house of Yahweh for the length of my days!


## Psalms 24:1 (id: 919024001)

1A psalm of David. The earth is Yahweh’s, and its fullness, the world, and all who live in it.


## Psalms 24:2 (id: 919024002)

2For he has founded it upon the seas and established it on the rivers.


## Psalms 24:3 (id: 919024003)

3Who will ascend the mountain of Yahweh? Who will stand in his holy place?


## Psalms 24:4 (id: 919024004)

4The one with clean hands and a pure heart; who has not lifted up my life as a falsehood, and has not sworn an oath in order to deceive.


## Psalms 24:5 (id: 919024005)

5He will receive a blessing from Yahweh and righteousness from the God of his salvation.


## Psalms 24:6 (id: 919024006)

6Such is the generation of those who seek him, those who seek the face of Jacob. 


## Psalms 24:7 (id: 919024007)

7Lift up your heads, you gates; be lifted up, everlasting doors, so that the King of glory may come in!


## Psalms 24:8 (id: 919024008)

8Who is this King of glory? Yahweh, strong and mighty; Yahweh, mighty in battle.


## Psalms 24:9 (id: 919024009)

9Lift up your heads, you gates; be lifted up, everlasting doors, so that the King of glory may come in!


## Psalms 24:10 (id: 919024010)

10Who is this King of glory? Yahweh of hosts, he is the King of glory. 


## Psalms 25:1 (id: 919025001)

1David To you, Yahweh, I lift up my life!


## Psalms 25:2 (id: 919025002)

2My God, I trust in you. Do not let me be humiliated; do not let my enemies rejoice triumphantly over me.


## Psalms 25:3 (id: 919025003)

3May no one who hopes in you be disgraced may those who act treacherously without cause be ashamed!


## Psalms 25:4 (id: 919025004)

4Make known to me your ways, Yahweh; teach me your paths.


## Psalms 25:5 (id: 919025005)

5Guide me into your truth and teach me, for you are the God of my salvation; I hope in you all day long.


## Psalms 25:6 (id: 919025006)

6Call to mind, Yahweh, your acts of compassion and of covenant faithfulness; for they have always existed.


## Psalms 25:7 (id: 919025007)

7Do not think about the sins of my youth or my rebelliousness; Call me to mind with covenant faithfulness because of your goodness, Yahweh!


## Psalms 25:8 (id: 919025008)

8Yahweh is good and upright; therefore he teaches sinners the way.


## Psalms 25:9 (id: 919025009)

9He guides the humble in what is right and he teaches them his way.


## Psalms 25:10 (id: 919025010)

10All the paths of Yahweh are steadfast love and faithfulness to those who keep his covenant and his solemn commands.


## Psalms 25:11 (id: 919025011)

11For your name’s sake, Yahweh, pardon my sin, for it is great.


## Psalms 25:12 (id: 919025012)

12Who is the man who fears Yahweh? The Lord will instruct him in the way that he should choose.


## Psalms 25:13 (id: 919025013)

13His life will go along in goodness; and his descendants will inherit the land.


## Psalms 25:14 (id: 919025014)

14The friendship of Yahweh is for those who honor him, and he makes his covenant known to them.


## Psalms 25:15 (id: 919025015)

15My eyes are always on Yahweh, for he will free my feet from the net.


## Psalms 25:16 (id: 919025016)

16Turn toward me and have mercy on me; for I am alone and afflicted.


## Psalms 25:17 (id: 919025017)

17The troubles of my heart are enlarged; draw me out from my distress!


## Psalms 25:18 (id: 919025018)

18See my affliction and my toils; forgive all my sins.


## Psalms 25:19 (id: 919025019)

19See my enemies, for they are many; they hate me with cruel hatred.


## Psalms 25:20 (id: 919025020)

20Protect my life and rescue me; do not let me be humiliated, for I take refuge in you!


## Psalms 25:21 (id: 919025021)

21May integrity and uprightness preserve me, for I hope in you.


## Psalms 25:22 (id: 919025022)

22Rescue Israel, God, from all of his troubles!


## Psalms 26:1 (id: 919026001)

1A psalm of David. David Judge me, Yahweh, for I have walked with integrity; I have trusted in Yahweh without wavering.


## Psalms 26:2 (id: 919026002)

2Examine me, Yahweh, and test me; test the purity of my inner parts and my heart!


## Psalms 26:3 (id: 919026003)

3For your covenant faithfulness is before my eyes, and I walk about in your faithfulness.


## Psalms 26:4 (id: 919026004)

4I do not associate with deceitful people, nor do I mingle with dishonest people.


## Psalms 26:5 (id: 919026005)

5I hate the assembly of evildoers, and I do not live with the wicked.


## Psalms 26:6 (id: 919026006)

6I wash my hands in innocence, and I go around your altar, Yahweh,


## Psalms 26:7 (id: 919026007)

7to sing a loud song of praise and report all your wonderful deeds.


## Psalms 26:8 (id: 919026008)

8Yahweh, I love the house where you live, the place where your glory lives!


## Psalms 26:9 (id: 919026009)

9Do not sweep me away with sinners, or my life with people who are bloodthirsty,


## Psalms 26:10 (id: 919026010)

10in whose hands there is a plot, and whose right hand is full of bribes.


## Psalms 26:11 (id: 919026011)

11But as for me, I will walk in integrity; redeem me and have mercy on me.


## Psalms 26:12 (id: 919026012)

12My foot stands on level ground; in the assemblies will I bless Yahweh!


## Psalms 27:1 (id: 919027001)

1A psalm of David. David Yahweh is my light and my salvation; whom should I fear? Yahweh is my life’s refuge; whom should I dread?


## Psalms 27:2 (id: 919027002)

2When evildoers approached me to devour my flesh, my adversaries and my enemies stumbled and fell.


## Psalms 27:3 (id: 919027003)

3Though an army encamps against me, my heart will not fear; though war rises up against me, even then I will remain confident.


## Psalms 27:4 (id: 919027004)

4One thing have I asked of Yahweh, and I will seek that: that I may live in the house of Yahweh all the days of my life, to see the beauty of Yahweh and to meditate in his temple.


## Psalms 27:5 (id: 919027005)

5For in the day of trouble he will hide me in his shelter; in the cover of his tent he will conceal me. He will lift me high on a rock!


## Psalms 27:6 (id: 919027006)

6Then my head will be lifted up above my enemies all around me, and I will offer sacrifices of joy in his tent! I will sing and make songs to Yahweh!


## Psalms 27:7 (id: 919027007)

7Hear, Yahweh, my voice when I cry out! Have mercy on me, and answer me!


## Psalms 27:8 (id: 919027008)

8My heart says about you, “Seek his face!” I seek your face, Yahweh!


## Psalms 27:9 (id: 919027009)

9Do not hide your face from me; do not turn your servant away in anger! You have been my helper; do not forsake me or abandon me, God of my salvation!


## Psalms 27:10 (id: 919027010)

10Even if my father and my mother forsake me, Yahweh will take me in.


## Psalms 27:11 (id: 919027011)

11Teach me your way, Yahweh! Lead me on a level path because of my enemies.


## Psalms 27:12 (id: 919027012)

12Do not give me up to the desires of my enemies, for false witnesses have risen up against me, and they breathe out violence!


## Psalms 27:13 (id: 919027013)

13What would have happened to me if I had not believed that I would see the goodness of Yahweh in the land of the living?


## Psalms 27:14 (id: 919027014)

14Wait for Yahweh; be strong, and let your heart be courageous! Wait for Yahweh!


## Psalms 28:1 (id: 919028001)

1A psalm of David. David To you, Yahweh, I cry out; my rock, do not ignore me. If you do not respond to me, I will join those who go down to the grave.


## Psalms 28:2 (id: 919028002)

2Hear the sound of my pleading when I call for help from you, when I lift up my hands toward your most holy place!


## Psalms 28:3 (id: 919028003)

3Do not drag me away with the wicked, those who do iniquity, who speak peace with their neighbors but have evil in their hearts.


## Psalms 28:4 (id: 919028004)

4Give them what their deeds deserve and repay them what their wickedness demands, repay them for the work of their hands and render to them their due.


## Psalms 28:5 (id: 919028005)

5Because they do not understand the deeds of Yahweh or the work of his hands, he will tear them down and never rebuild them.


## Psalms 28:6 (id: 919028006)

6Blessed be Yahweh because he has heard the sound of my pleading!


## Psalms 28:7 (id: 919028007)

7Yahweh is my strength and my shield; my heart trusts in him, and I am helped. Therefore my heart greatly rejoices, and I will praise him with singing.


## Psalms 28:8 (id: 919028008)

8Yahweh is the strength of his people, and he is the saving refuge of his anointed one.


## Psalms 28:9 (id: 919028009)

9Save your people and bless your inheritance. Be their shepherd and carry them forever.


## Psalms 29:1 (id: 919029001)

1A psalm of David. A Psalm of David Ascribe to Yahweh, you sons of God, ascribe to Yahweh glory and strength!


## Psalms 29:2 (id: 919029002)

2Ascribe to Yahweh the glory his name deserves. Bow down to Yahweh in the splendor of holiness!


## Psalms 29:3 (id: 919029003)

3The voice of Yahweh is heard over the waters; the God of glory thunders, Yahweh thunders over many waters.


## Psalms 29:4 (id: 919029004)

4The voice of Yahweh is powerful; the voice of Yahweh is majestic.


## Psalms 29:5 (id: 919029005)

5The voice of Yahweh breaks the cedars; Yahweh breaks in pieces the cedars of Lebanon.


## Psalms 29:6 (id: 919029006)

6He makes Lebanon skip like a calf and Sirion like a young ox.


## Psalms 29:7 (id: 919029007)

7The voice of Yahweh sends out flames of fire.


## Psalms 29:8 (id: 919029008)

8The voice of Yahweh shakes the wilderness; Yahweh shakes the wilderness of Kadesh.


## Psalms 29:9 (id: 919029009)

9The voice of Yahweh causes the oaks to twist and strips the forests bare. Everyone in his temple says, “Glory!”


## Psalms 29:10 (id: 919029010)

10Yahweh sits as king over the flood; Yahweh sits as king forever.


## Psalms 29:11 (id: 919029011)

11Yahweh gives strength to his people; Yahweh blesses his people with peace.


## Psalms 30:1 (id: 919030001)

1A psalm; a song at the dedication of the temple. A psalm of David. I will exalt you, Yahweh, for you have raised me up and have not allowed my enemies to rejoice over me.


## Psalms 30:2 (id: 919030002)

2Yahweh my God, I cried to you for help, and you healed me.


## Psalms 30:3 (id: 919030003)

3Yahweh, you have brought up my soul from Sheol; you have kept me alive from going down to the grave.


## Psalms 30:4 (id: 919030004)

4Sing praises to Yahweh, you his faithful ones! Give thanks when you remember his holiness.


## Psalms 30:5 (id: 919030005)

5For his anger is only for a moment; but his favor is for a lifetime. Weeping comes for a night, but joy comes in the morning.


## Psalms 30:6 (id: 919030006)

6In confidence I said, “I will never be shaken.”


## Psalms 30:7 (id: 919030007)

7Yahweh, by your favor you established me as a strong mountain; but when you hid your face, I was troubled.


## Psalms 30:8 (id: 919030008)

8I cried to you, Yahweh, and sought favor from my Lord!


## Psalms 30:9 (id: 919030009)

9What advantage is there in my death, if I go down to the grave? Will the dust praise you? Will it declare your trustworthiness?


## Psalms 30:10 (id: 919030010)

10Hear, Yahweh, and have mercy on me! Yahweh, be my helper.


## Psalms 30:11 (id: 919030011)

11You have turned my mourning into dancing; you have removed my sackcloth and clothed me with gladness.


## Psalms 30:12 (id: 919030012)

12So now my glory will sing praise to you and not be silent; Yahweh my God, I will give thanks to you forever!


## Psalms 31:1 (id: 919031001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. In you, Yahweh, I take refuge; never let me be humiliated. Rescue me in your righteousness.


## Psalms 31:2 (id: 919031002)

2Listen to me; rescue me quickly; be my rock of refuge, a stronghold to save me.


## Psalms 31:3 (id: 919031003)

3For you are my rock and my fortress; therefore for your name’s sake, lead and guide me.


## Psalms 31:4 (id: 919031004)

4Pluck me out of the net that they have hidden for me, for you are my refuge.


## Psalms 31:5 (id: 919031005)

5Into your hands I entrust my spirit; you will redeem me, Yahweh, God of trustworthiness.


## Psalms 31:6 (id: 919031006)

6I hate those who serve worthless idols, but I trust in Yahweh.


## Psalms 31:7 (id: 919031007)

7I will be glad and rejoice in your covenant faithfulness, for you saw my affliction; you knew the distress of my soul.


## Psalms 31:8 (id: 919031008)

8You have not given me into the hand of my enemy. You have set my feet in a wide open place.


## Psalms 31:9 (id: 919031009)

9Have mercy upon me, Yahweh, for I am in distress; my eyes grow weary with grief with my soul and my body.


## Psalms 31:10 (id: 919031010)

10For my life is weary with sorrow and my years with groaning. My strength fails because of my sin, and my bones are wasting away.


## Psalms 31:11 (id: 919031011)

11Because of all my enemies, people disdain me; my neighbors are appalled at my situation, and those who know me are horrified. Those who see me in the street run from me.


## Psalms 31:12 (id: 919031012)

12I am forgotten as a dead man whom no one thinks about. I am like a broken pot.


## Psalms 31:13 (id: 919031013)

13For I have heard the whispering of many, terrifying news from every side as they plot together against me. They plot to take away my life.


## Psalms 31:14 (id: 919031014)

14But I trust in you, Yahweh; I say, “You are my God.”


## Psalms 31:15 (id: 919031015)

15My times are in your hand. Rescue me from the hands of my enemies and from those who pursue me.


## Psalms 31:16 (id: 919031016)

16Make your face shine on your servant; save me in your covenant faithfulness.


## Psalms 31:17 (id: 919031017)

17Do not let me be humiliated, Yahweh; for I call out to you! May the wicked be humiliated! May they be silent in Sheol.


## Psalms 31:18 (id: 919031018)

18May lying lips be silenced that speak against the righteous defiantly with arrogance and contempt.


## Psalms 31:19 (id: 919031019)

19How great is your goodness that you have stored up for those who revere you, that you perform for those who take refuge in you before all the children of mankind!


## Psalms 31:20 (id: 919031020)

20In the shelter of your presence, you hide them from the plots of men. You hide them in a shelter from the violence of tongues.


## Psalms 31:21 (id: 919031021)

21Blessed be Yahweh, for he showed me his marvelous covenant faithfulness when I was in a besieged city.


## Psalms 31:22 (id: 919031022)

22Though I said in my haste, “I am cut off from your eyes,” yet you heard my plea for help when I cried to you.


## Psalms 31:23 (id: 919031023)

23Love Yahweh, all you faithful ones. Yahweh protects the faithful, but he pays back the arrogant in full.


## Psalms 31:24 (id: 919031024)

24Be strong and confident, all you who trust in Yahweh for help.


## Psalms 32:1 (id: 919032001)

1A psalm of David. A maschil. A writing of David Blessed is the person whose transgression is forgiven, whose sin is covered.


## Psalms 32:2 (id: 919032002)

2Blessed is the man to whom Yahweh reckons no guilt and in whose spirit there is no deceit.


## Psalms 32:3 (id: 919032003)

3When I remained silent, my bones were wasting away while I groaned all day long.


## Psalms 32:4 (id: 919032004)

4For day and night your hand was heavy upon me. My strength withered as in summer drought. 


## Psalms 32:5 (id: 919032005)

5Then I acknowledged my sin to you, and I no longer hid my iniquity. I said, “I will confess my transgressions to Yahweh,” and you forgave the guilt of my sin. 


## Psalms 32:6 (id: 919032006)

6For this reason every one of your faithful followers should pray to you at a time of great distress. When the surging waters overflow, the waters will not reach them.


## Psalms 32:7 (id: 919032007)

7You are my hiding place; you will guard me from trouble. You will surround me with the songs of victory. 


## Psalms 32:8 (id: 919032008)

8I will instruct you and teach you in the way which you should go. I will instruct you with my eye upon you.


## Psalms 32:9 (id: 919032009)

9Do not be like a horse or like a mule, which have no understanding; it is only with bridle and bit to control them that they will go where you want them to.


## Psalms 32:10 (id: 919032010)

10The wicked have many sorrows, but Yahweh’s covenant faithfulness will surround the one who trusts in him.


## Psalms 32:11 (id: 919032011)

11Be glad in Yahweh, and rejoice, you righteous; shout for joy, all you who are upright in heart.


## Psalms 33:1 (id: 919033001)

1Rejoice in Yahweh, you righteous; praise is appropriate for the upright.


## Psalms 33:2 (id: 919033002)

2Give thanks to Yahweh with the harp; sing praises to him with the harp of ten strings.


## Psalms 33:3 (id: 919033003)

3Sing to him a new song; play skillfully and sing with joy.


## Psalms 33:4 (id: 919033004)

4For Yahweh’s word is upright, and everything he does is fair.


## Psalms 33:5 (id: 919033005)

5He loves righteousness and justice. The earth is full of Yahweh’s covenant faithfulness.


## Psalms 33:6 (id: 919033006)

6By the word of Yahweh the heavens were made, and all the stars were made by the breath of his mouth.


## Psalms 33:7 (id: 919033007)

7He gathers the waters of the sea together like a heap; he puts the oceans in storehouses.


## Psalms 33:8 (id: 919033008)

8Let the whole earth fear Yahweh; let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.


## Psalms 33:9 (id: 919033009)

9For he spoke, and it was done; he commanded, and it stood in place.


## Psalms 33:10 (id: 919033010)

10Yahweh frustrates the alliances of nations; he overrules the plans of the peoples.


## Psalms 33:11 (id: 919033011)

11The plans of Yahweh stand forever, the plans of his heart for all generations.


## Psalms 33:12 (id: 919033012)

12Blessed is the nation whose God is Yahweh, the people whom he has chosen as his own inheritance.


## Psalms 33:13 (id: 919033013)

13Yahweh looks from heaven; he sees all the people.


## Psalms 33:14 (id: 919033014)

14From the place where he lives, he looks down on all who live on the earth.


## Psalms 33:15 (id: 919033015)

15He who shapes the hearts of them all observes all their deeds.


## Psalms 33:16 (id: 919033016)

16No king is saved by a vast army; a warrior is not saved by his great strength.


## Psalms 33:17 (id: 919033017)

17A horse is a false hope for victory; in spite of his great strength, he cannot rescue.


## Psalms 33:18 (id: 919033018)

18See, Yahweh’s eye is on those who fear him, on those who hope in his covenant faithfulness


## Psalms 33:19 (id: 919033019)

19to deliver their lives from death and to keep them alive in times of famine.


## Psalms 33:20 (id: 919033020)

20We wait for Yahweh; he is our help and our shield.


## Psalms 33:21 (id: 919033021)

21Our hearts rejoice in him, for we trust in his holy name.


## Psalms 33:22 (id: 919033022)

22Let your covenant faithfulness, Yahweh, be with us as we put our hope in you.


## Psalms 34:1 (id: 919034001)

1A psalm of David; when he pretended to be insane before Abimelech, who drove him out. I will praise Yahweh at all times, his praise will always be in my mouth.


## Psalms 34:2 (id: 919034002)

2I will praise Yahweh! May the oppressed hear and rejoice.


## Psalms 34:3 (id: 919034003)

3Praise Yahweh with me, let us lift up his name together.


## Psalms 34:4 (id: 919034004)

4I sought Yahweh and he answered me, and he gave me victory over all my fears.


## Psalms 34:5 (id: 919034005)

5Those who look to him are radiant, and their faces are not ashamed.


## Psalms 34:6 (id: 919034006)

6This oppressed man cried and Yahweh heard him and saved him from all his troubles.


## Psalms 34:7 (id: 919034007)

7The angel of Yahweh camps around those who fear him and rescues them.


## Psalms 34:8 (id: 919034008)

8Taste and see that Yahweh is good. Blessed is the man who takes refuge in him.


## Psalms 34:9 (id: 919034009)

9Fear Yahweh, you his holy people. There is no lack for those who fear him.


## Psalms 34:10 (id: 919034010)

10The young lions sometimes lack food and suffer hunger, but those who seek Yahweh will not lack anything good.


## Psalms 34:11 (id: 919034011)

11Come, sons, listen to me. I will teach you the fear of Yahweh.


## Psalms 34:12 (id: 919034012)

12What man is there who desires life and loves many days, that he may see good?


## Psalms 34:13 (id: 919034013)

13Then keep your tongue from evil and keep your lips from speaking lies.


## Psalms 34:14 (id: 919034014)

14Turn away from evil and do good. Seek peace and go after it.


## Psalms 34:15 (id: 919034015)

15The eyes of Yahweh are on the righteous and his ears are directed toward their cry.


## Psalms 34:16 (id: 919034016)

16The face of Yahweh is against those who do evil, to cut off the memory of them from the earth.


## Psalms 34:17 (id: 919034017)

17The righteous cry out and Yahweh hears and he rescues them from all their troubles.


## Psalms 34:18 (id: 919034018)

18Yahweh is close to the brokenhearted, and he saves those who are crushed in spirit.


## Psalms 34:19 (id: 919034019)

19Many are the troubles of the righteous, but Yahweh delivers them out of them all.


## Psalms 34:20 (id: 919034020)

20He keeps all his bones, not one of them will be broken.


## Psalms 34:21 (id: 919034021)

21Evil will kill the wicked. Those who hate the righteous will be condemned.


## Psalms 34:22 (id: 919034022)

22Yahweh rescues the lives of his servants. None of those who take refuge in him will be condemned.


## Psalms 35:1 (id: 919035001)

1A psalm of David. David Yahweh, work against those who work against me; fight against those who fight against me.


## Psalms 35:2 (id: 919035002)

2Grab your small shield and large shield; rise up and help me.


## Psalms 35:3 (id: 919035003)

3Use your spear and battle ax against those who chase me; say to my soul, “I am your salvation.”


## Psalms 35:4 (id: 919035004)

4May those who seek my life be shamed and dishonored. May those who plan to harm me be turned back and confounded.


## Psalms 35:5 (id: 919035005)

5May they be as chaff before the wind, as the angel of Yahweh drives them away.


## Psalms 35:6 (id: 919035006)

6May their way be dark and slippery, as the angel of Yahweh chases them.


## Psalms 35:7 (id: 919035007)

7Without cause they set their net for me; without cause they dug a pit for my life.


## Psalms 35:8 (id: 919035008)

8Let destruction overtake them by surprise. Let the net that they have set catch them. Let them fall into it, to their destruction.


## Psalms 35:9 (id: 919035009)

9But I will be joyful in Yahweh and rejoice in his salvation.


## Psalms 35:10 (id: 919035010)

10All my bones will say, “Yahweh, who is like you, who rescues the oppressed from those who are too strong for them and the poor and needy from those who try to rob them?”


## Psalms 35:11 (id: 919035011)

11Unrighteous witnesses rise up; they accuse me falsely.


## Psalms 35:12 (id: 919035012)

12They repay me evil for good. I am sorrowful.


## Psalms 35:13 (id: 919035013)

13But, when they were sick, I wore sackcloth; I fasted for them with my head bowed on my chest.


## Psalms 35:14 (id: 919035014)

14I went about in grief as for my brother; I bent down in mourning as for my mother.


## Psalms 35:15 (id: 919035015)

15But when I stumbled, they rejoiced and gathered together; they gathered together against me, and I was surprised by them. They tore at me without stopping.


## Psalms 35:16 (id: 919035016)

16With no respect at all they mocked me; they grind their teeth at me in rage.


## Psalms 35:17 (id: 919035017)

17Lord, how long will you look on? Rescue my soul from their destructive attacks, my life from the lions.


## Psalms 35:18 (id: 919035018)

18Then I will thank you in the great assembly; I will praise you among many people.


## Psalms 35:19 (id: 919035019)

19Do not let my deceitful enemies rejoice over me; do not let them carry out their wicked schemes.


## Psalms 35:20 (id: 919035020)

20For they do not speak peace, but they devise deceitful words against those in our land who live in peace.


## Psalms 35:21 (id: 919035021)

21They open their mouths wide against me; they said, “Aha, Aha, our eyes have seen it.”


## Psalms 35:22 (id: 919035022)

22You have seen it, Yahweh, do not be silent; Lord, do not be far from me.


## Psalms 35:23 (id: 919035023)

23Arouse yourself and awake to my defense; My God and my Lord, defend my cause.


## Psalms 35:24 (id: 919035024)

24Defend me, Yahweh my God, because of your righteousness; do not let them rejoice over me.


## Psalms 35:25 (id: 919035025)

25Do not let them say in their heart, “Aha, we have what we wanted.” Do not let them say, “We have devoured him.”


## Psalms 35:26 (id: 919035026)

26May they be put to shame and may they be confounded who rejoice at my distress. May those who exalt themselves over me be clothed with shame and dishonor.


## Psalms 35:27 (id: 919035027)

27Let those who desire my vindication shout for joy and be glad; may they say continually, “Yahweh be praised, he who delights in the welfare of his servant.”


## Psalms 35:28 (id: 919035028)

28Then I will tell of your justice and praise you all day long.


## Psalms 36:1 (id: 919036001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David the servant of Yahweh. An evil man speaks of his transgression from deep in his heart, there is no fear of God before his eyes.


## Psalms 36:2 (id: 919036002)

2For he comforts himself, thinking that his sin will not be discovered and be hated.


## Psalms 36:3 (id: 919036003)

3His words are sinful and deceitful; he does not want to be wise and do good.


## Psalms 36:4 (id: 919036004)

4While he lies in bed, he plans ways to sin; he sets out on an evil way; he does not reject evil.


## Psalms 36:5 (id: 919036005)

5Your covenant faithfulness, Yahweh, reaches to the heavens; your loyalty reaches to the clouds.


## Psalms 36:6 (id: 919036006)

6Your righteousness is like the mountains of God; your judgments are like the great deep. Yahweh, you preserve both mankind and the animals.


## Psalms 36:7 (id: 919036007)

7How precious is your covenant faithfulness, God! Humanity takes refuge under the shadow of your wings.


## Psalms 36:8 (id: 919036008)

8They feast upon the abundance of your house; you let them drink from the river of your delights.


## Psalms 36:9 (id: 919036009)

9For with you is the fountain of life; in your light we will see light.


## Psalms 36:10 (id: 919036010)

10Extend your covenant faithfulness fully to those who know you, your defense to the upright of heart.


## Psalms 36:11 (id: 919036011)

11Do not let the foot of the arrogant man come near to me. Do not let the hand of the wicked drive me away.


## Psalms 36:12 (id: 919036012)

12Over there the evildoers have fallen; they are knocked down and are not able to get up.


## Psalms 37:1 (id: 919037001)

1A psalm of David. David Do not be irritated because of evildoers; do not be envious of those who act unrighteously.


## Psalms 37:2 (id: 919037002)

2For they will soon dry up as the grass and wither as the green plants.


## Psalms 37:3 (id: 919037003)

3Trust in Yahweh and do what is good; settle in the land and graze in faithfulness.


## Psalms 37:4 (id: 919037004)

4Then delight yourself in Yahweh, and he will give you the desires of your heart.


## Psalms 37:5 (id: 919037005)

5Give your ways to Yahweh; trust in him, and he will act on your behalf.


## Psalms 37:6 (id: 919037006)

6He will display your justice like the daylight and your innocence like the day at noon.


## Psalms 37:7 (id: 919037007)

7Be still before Yahweh and wait patiently for him. Do not be angry if someone succeeds in what he does, or when he makes evil plots.


## Psalms 37:8 (id: 919037008)

8Do not be angry and frustrated. Do not worry. This only makes trouble.


## Psalms 37:9 (id: 919037009)

9Evildoers will be cut off, but those who wait for Yahweh will inherit the land.


## Psalms 37:10 (id: 919037010)

10In a little while the evil man will disappear; you will look at his place, but he will be gone.


## Psalms 37:11 (id: 919037011)

11But the meek will inherit the land and will delight in great prosperity.


## Psalms 37:12 (id: 919037012)

12The wicked man plots against the righteous and he grinds his teeth in rage against him.


## Psalms 37:13 (id: 919037013)

13The Lord laughs at him, for he sees that his day is coming.


## Psalms 37:14 (id: 919037014)

14The wicked have drawn out their swords and have bent their bows to cast down the oppressed and needy, to kill those who are upright.


## Psalms 37:15 (id: 919037015)

15Their swords will pierce their own hearts, and their bows will be broken.


## Psalms 37:16 (id: 919037016)

16Better is the little that the righteous has than the abundance of many wicked people.


## Psalms 37:17 (id: 919037017)

17For the arms of the wicked people will be broken, but Yahweh supports the righteous people.


## Psalms 37:18 (id: 919037018)

18Yahweh watches over the blameless day by day, and their heritage will be forever.


## Psalms 37:19 (id: 919037019)

19They will not be ashamed when times are bad. When famine comes, they will have enough to eat.


## Psalms 37:20 (id: 919037020)

20But evil men will perish. Yahweh’s enemies will be like the glory of the pastures; they will be consumed and disappear in the smoke.


## Psalms 37:21 (id: 919037021)

21The wicked person borrows but does not repay, but the righteous person is generous and gives.


## Psalms 37:22 (id: 919037022)

22Those who are blessed by God will inherit the land; those who are cursed by him will be cut off.


## Psalms 37:23 (id: 919037023)

23It is by Yahweh that a man’s steps are established, the man whose way is commendable in God’s sight.


## Psalms 37:24 (id: 919037024)

24Though he stumbles, he will not fall down, for Yahweh is holding him with his hand.


## Psalms 37:25 (id: 919037025)

25I was young and now am old; I have never seen the righteous person abandoned or his children begging for bread.


## Psalms 37:26 (id: 919037026)

26All the day long he is gracious and lends, and his children become a blessing.


## Psalms 37:27 (id: 919037027)

27Turn away from evil and do what is right; then you will be safe forever.


## Psalms 37:28 (id: 919037028)

28For Yahweh loves justice and does not abandon his faithful ones. They are preserved forever, but the descendants of the wicked will be cut off.


## Psalms 37:29 (id: 919037029)

29The righteous will inherit the land and live there forever.


## Psalms 37:30 (id: 919037030)

30The mouth of the righteous person speaks wisdom and increases justice.


## Psalms 37:31 (id: 919037031)

31The law of his God is in his heart; his feet will not slip.


## Psalms 37:32 (id: 919037032)

32The wicked person watches the righteous person and seeks to kill him.


## Psalms 37:33 (id: 919037033)

33Yahweh will not abandon him into the evil person’s hand or condemn him when he is judged.


## Psalms 37:34 (id: 919037034)

34Wait for Yahweh and keep his way, and he will raise you up to possess the land. You will see when the wicked are cut off.


## Psalms 37:35 (id: 919037035)

35I have seen the wicked and terrifying person spread out like a green tree in its native soil.


## Psalms 37:36 (id: 919037036)

36But when I passed by again, he was not there. I looked for him, but he could not be found.


## Psalms 37:37 (id: 919037037)

37Observe the man of integrity, and mark the upright; there is a good future for a man of peace.


## Psalms 37:38 (id: 919037038)

38Sinners will be totally destroyed; the future for the wicked man is cut off.


## Psalms 37:39 (id: 919037039)

39Salvation of the righteous comes from Yahweh; he protects them in the times of trouble.


## Psalms 37:40 (id: 919037040)

40Yahweh helps them and rescues them. He rescues them from evil men and saves them because they have taken refuge in him.


## Psalms 38:1 (id: 919038001)

1A psalm of David, to bring to remembrance. Yahweh, do not rebuke me in your anger; do not punish me in your wrath.


## Psalms 38:2 (id: 919038002)

2For your arrows pierce me, and your hand presses me down.


## Psalms 38:3 (id: 919038003)

3My whole body is sick because of your anger; there is no health in my bones because of my sin.


## Psalms 38:4 (id: 919038004)

4For my iniquities overwhelm me; they are a burden too heavy for me.


## Psalms 38:5 (id: 919038005)

5My wounds are infected and smell because of my foolish sins.


## Psalms 38:6 (id: 919038006)

6I am stooped over and humiliated every day; I go about mourning all day long.


## Psalms 38:7 (id: 919038007)

7For within me, I am filled with burning; there is no health in my flesh.


## Psalms 38:8 (id: 919038008)

8I am numb and utterly crushed; I groan because of the anguish of my heart.


## Psalms 38:9 (id: 919038009)

9Lord, you understand my heart’s deepest yearnings, and my groanings are not hidden from you.


## Psalms 38:10 (id: 919038010)

10My heart pounds, my strength fades, and my eyesight dims.


## Psalms 38:11 (id: 919038011)

11My friends and companions shun me because of my condition; my neighbors stand far off.


## Psalms 38:12 (id: 919038012)

12Those who seek my life lay snares for me. They who seek my harm speak destructive words and say deceitful words all day long.


## Psalms 38:13 (id: 919038013)

13But I, I am like a deaf man and hear nothing; I am like a mute man who says nothing.


## Psalms 38:14 (id: 919038014)

14I am like a man who does not hear and who has no reply.


## Psalms 38:15 (id: 919038015)

15Surely I wait for you, Yahweh; you will answer, Lord my God.


## Psalms 38:16 (id: 919038016)

16For I said "Hear me, so that they will not gloat over me. If my foot slips, they will do terrible things to me.


## Psalms 38:17 (id: 919038017)

17For I am about to stumble, and I am in constant pain.


## Psalms 38:18 (id: 919038018)

18I confess my guilt; I am concerned about my sin.


## Psalms 38:19 (id: 919038019)

19But my enemies are numerous; those who hate me wrongfully are many.


## Psalms 38:20 (id: 919038020)

20They repay me evil for good; they hurl accusations at me although I have pursued what is good.


## Psalms 38:21 (id: 919038021)

21Do not abandon me, Yahweh; my God, do not stay far away from me.


## Psalms 38:22 (id: 919038022)

22Come quickly to help me, Lord, my salvation.


## Psalms 39:1 (id: 919039001)

1For the chief musician, for Jeduthun. A psalm of David. I decided, “I will watch what I say so that I do not sin with my tongue. I will muzzle my mouth while in the presence of an evil man.”


## Psalms 39:2 (id: 919039002)

2I kept silent; I kept back my words even from saying anything good, and my pain grew worse.


## Psalms 39:3 (id: 919039003)

3My heart became hot; when I thought about these things, it burned like a fire. Then finally I spoke.


## Psalms 39:4 (id: 919039004)

4“Yahweh, make me know when will be the end of my life and the extent of my days. Show me how transient I am.


## Psalms 39:5 (id: 919039005)

5See, you have made my days only the width of my hand, and my lifetime is like nothing before you. Surely every man is a single breath. 


## Psalms 39:6 (id: 919039006)

6Surely every man walks about like a shadow. Surely everyone hurries about to accumulate riches although they do not know who will receive them.


## Psalms 39:7 (id: 919039007)

7Now, Lord, for what am I waiting? You are my only hope.


## Psalms 39:8 (id: 919039008)

8Rescue me from my sins; do not make me the reproach of fools.


## Psalms 39:9 (id: 919039009)

9I am silent and cannot open my mouth, because it is you who has done it.


## Psalms 39:10 (id: 919039010)

10Stop wounding me; I am overwhelmed by the blow of your hand.


## Psalms 39:11 (id: 919039011)

11When you discipline people for sin, you consume the things they desire like a moth; surely all people are nothing but vapor. 


## Psalms 39:12 (id: 919039012)

12Hear my prayer, Yahweh, and listen to me; listen to my weeping! Do not be deaf to me, for I am like a foreigner with you, a refugee like all my ancestors were.


## Psalms 39:13 (id: 919039013)

13Turn your gaze from me so that I may smile again before I die.”


## Psalms 40:1 (id: 919040001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. I waited patiently for Yahweh; he listened to me and heard my cry.


## Psalms 40:2 (id: 919040002)

2He brought me up out of a horrible pit, out of the miry clay, and he set my feet on a rock and made my steps secure.


## Psalms 40:3 (id: 919040003)

3He has put a new song in my mouth, praise to our God. Many will see it and honor him and will trust in Yahweh.


## Psalms 40:4 (id: 919040004)

4Blessed is the man who makes Yahweh his trust and does not honor the proud or those who turn away from him to lies.


## Psalms 40:5 (id: 919040005)

5Many, Yahweh my God, are the wonderful deeds that you have done, and your thoughts which are about us cannot be numbered; if I declared and spoke of them, they would be more than could be counted.


## Psalms 40:6 (id: 919040006)

6You have no delight in sacrifice or offering, but you have opened my ears; you have not required burnt offerings or sin offerings.


## Psalms 40:7 (id: 919040007)

7Then said I, “See, I have come; it is written about me in the scroll of the document.


## Psalms 40:8 (id: 919040008)

8I delight to do your will, my God; your laws are in my heart.”


## Psalms 40:9 (id: 919040009)

9I have proclaimed good news of your righteousness in the great assembly; Yahweh, you know that my lips have not kept back from doing this.


## Psalms 40:10 (id: 919040010)

10I have not concealed your righteousness in my heart; I have declared your faithfulness and your salvation; I have not concealed your covenant faithfulness or your trustworthiness from the great assembly.


## Psalms 40:11 (id: 919040011)

11Do not keep back your acts of mercy from me, Yahweh; let your covenant faithfulness and your trustworthiness always preserve me.


## Psalms 40:12 (id: 919040012)

12Troubles that cannot be numbered surround me; my iniquities have caught up with me so that I am no longer able to see anything; they are more than the hairs on my head, and my heart has failed me.


## Psalms 40:13 (id: 919040013)

13Be pleased, Yahweh, to rescue me; hurry to help me, Yahweh.


## Psalms 40:14 (id: 919040014)

14Let them be ashamed and completely disappointed who pursue my life to take it away. Let them be turned back and brought to dishonor, those who delight in hurting me.


## Psalms 40:15 (id: 919040015)

15Let them be shocked because of their shame, those who say to me, “Aha, aha!”


## Psalms 40:16 (id: 919040016)

16But may all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you; let everyone who loves your salvation say continually, “May Yahweh be praised.”


## Psalms 40:17 (id: 919040017)

17I am poor and needy; yet the Lord thinks about me. You are my help and you come to my rescue; do not delay, my God.


## Psalms 41:1 (id: 919041001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. Blessed is he who is concerned for the weak; in the day of trouble, Yahweh will rescue him.


## Psalms 41:2 (id: 919041002)
