2Yahweh will preserve him and keep him alive, and he will be blessed on the earth; Yahweh will not turn him over to the will of his enemies.


## Psalms 41:3 (id: 919041003)

3Yahweh will support him on the bed of suffering; you will make his bed of sickness into a bed of healing.


## Psalms 41:4 (id: 919041004)

4I said, “Yahweh, have mercy on me! Heal me, for I have sinned against you.”


## Psalms 41:5 (id: 919041005)

5My enemies speak evil against me, saying, ‘When will he die and his name perish?’


## Psalms 41:6 (id: 919041006)

6If my enemy comes to see me, he says worthless things; his heart gathers up my disaster for itself; when he goes away from me, he tells others about it.


## Psalms 41:7 (id: 919041007)

7All who hate me whisper together against me; against me they hope for my hurt.


## Psalms 41:8 (id: 919041008)

8They say, “An evil disease holds on tightly to him; now that he is lying down, he will rise up no more.”


## Psalms 41:9 (id: 919041009)

9Indeed, even my own close friend, in whom I trusted, who ate my bread, has lifted up his heel against me.


## Psalms 41:10 (id: 919041010)

10But you, Yahweh, have mercy on me and raise me up so that I may pay them back.


## Psalms 41:11 (id: 919041011)

11By this I know that you delight in me, for my enemy does not triumph over me.


## Psalms 41:12 (id: 919041012)

12As for me, you support me in my integrity and will keep me before your face forever.


## Psalms 41:13 (id: 919041013)

13May Yahweh, the God of Israel be praised from everlasting to everlasting. Amen and Amen.


## Psalms 42:1 (id: 919042001)

1For the chief musician. A maschil of the sons of Korah. As a deer longs for streams of water, so my soul longs for you, God.


## Psalms 42:2 (id: 919042002)

2My soul thirsts for God, for the living God. When will I come and appear before the face of God?


## Psalms 42:3 (id: 919042003)

3My tears are my food day and night, as {people are} saying to me every day, “Where is your God?”


## Psalms 42:4 (id: 919042004)

4These things I remember, and I pour out my soul within myself: I traveled with the crowd and accompanied them to the house of God with a voice of joy and praise, a multitude celebrating a festival.


## Psalms 42:5 (id: 919042005)

5Why are you bowed down, O my soul, and upset within me? Hope in God, for again I will praise him, the salvation of my face


## Psalms 42:6 (id: 919042006)

6and my God. My soul is bowed down within me, therefore I remember you from the land of the Jordan and the Hermons, and from Mount Mizar.


## Psalms 42:7 (id: 919042007)

7Deep is calling to deep at the sound of your waterfalls; All of your waves and your billows flow over me.


## Psalms 42:8 (id: 919042008)

8During the day, Yahweh commands his covenant faithfulness, and in the night, his song is with me— a prayer to the God of my life.


## Psalms 42:9 (id: 919042009)

9I will say to God, my rock, “Why have you forgotten me? Why do I walk around mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?”


## Psalms 42:10 (id: 919042010)

10In the crushing of my bones, those who are hostile to me rebuke me when they are saying to me all day long, “Where is your God?”


## Psalms 42:11 (id: 919042011)

11Why are you bowed down, O my soul? And why are you upset within me? Hope in God, for again I will give him thanks, the salvation of my face is my God.


## Psalms 43:1 (id: 919043001)

1Declare me righteous, O God, and defend my case against a nation that is not faithful. Deliver me from a deceitful and evil man.


## Psalms 43:2 (id: 919043002)

2For you are the God of my fortification. Why have you rejected me? Why do I walk around mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?


## Psalms 43:3 (id: 919043003)

3Send out your light and your truth, let them lead me. Let them bring me to your holy mountain and to your dwelling place.


## Psalms 43:4 (id: 919043004)

4I will go to the altar of God, to the God of the joy of my gladness. I will praise you with the lyre, O God, my God.


## Psalms 43:5 (id: 919043005)

5Why are you bowed down, O my soul? And why are you upset within me? Hope in God, for again I will give him thanks, the salvation of my face is my God.


## Psalms 44:1 (id: 919044001)

1For the chief musician. Of the sons of Korah. A maschil. O God, we have listened with our ears, our fathers have told us the work you did in their days, in the days of old.


## Psalms 44:2 (id: 919044002)

2You drove out the nations {by} your hand, but you planted them. You afflicted the peoples, but you sent them.


## Psalms 44:3 (id: 919044003)

3For with their sword they did not possess the land, and their arm did not save them, but your right hand, and your arm, and the light of your face, because you were pleased with them.


## Psalms 44:4 (id: 919044004)

4You are my king, O God. Appoint salvation for Jacob.


## Psalms 44:5 (id: 919044005)

5Through you we will gore our adversaries, by your name we will trample those who rise up against us.


## Psalms 44:6 (id: 919044006)

6For I will not trust in my bow, and my sword will not save me.


## Psalms 44:7 (id: 919044007)

7For you have saved us from our adversaries, and have put to shame those who hate us.


## Psalms 44:8 (id: 919044008)

8In God we have boasted every day, and we will praise your name forever. 


## Psalms 44:9 (id: 919044009)

9Yet, you have rejected and humiliated us, and you do not go out with our armies.


## Psalms 44:10 (id: 919044010)

10You made us turn back from the adversary, and those who hate us plunder for themselves.


## Psalms 44:11 (id: 919044011)

11You have appoint us {to be} like sheep for food, and you have scattered us among the nations.


## Psalms 44:12 (id: 919044012)

12You have sold your people for what is not valuable, you have not increased their price.


## Psalms 44:13 (id: 919044013)

13You have made us a reproach to our neighbors, a contempt and a scorn to those around us.


## Psalms 44:14 (id: 919044014)

14You made us an insult among the nations, a shaking of the head among the peoples.


## Psalms 44:15 (id: 919044015)

15All day my dishonor is before me, and the shame of my face has covered me


## Psalms 44:16 (id: 919044016)

16from of the voice of reproaching and insulting, and from the face of an enemy and a vengeful one.


## Psalms 44:17 (id: 919044017)

17All of this has come {against} us, and we have not forgotten you, and we have not dealt falsely with your covenant.


## Psalms 44:18 (id: 919044018)

18Our heart has not turned back, our steps bent from your way.


## Psalms 44:19 (id: 919044019)

19But you have crushed us in the place of jackals, and you have covered over us with extreme darkness.


## Psalms 44:20 (id: 919044020)

20If we had forgotten the name of our God and spread out our hands to a foreign god,


## Psalms 44:21 (id: 919044021)

21would God not have discovered this? For he knows the secrets of the heart.


## Psalms 44:22 (id: 919044022)

22Indeed, because of you we are killed all the day, we are considered {to be} like sheep of slaughtering.


## Psalms 44:23 (id: 919044023)

23Awake! Why do you sleep, Lord? Arise! Do not reject {us} forever!


## Psalms 44:24 (id: 919044024)

24Why do you hide your face and forget our affliction and our oppression?


## Psalms 44:25 (id: 919044025)

25For our life has sunk down into the dust, our belly has clung to the earth.


## Psalms 44:26 (id: 919044026)

26Rise up {as) our helper and redeem us because of your covenant faithfulness.


## Psalms 45:1 (id: 919045001)

1For the chief musician; set to Shoshannim. A psalm of the sons of Korah. A maschil. A song of loves. My heart overflows on a good subject; I will read aloud the words I have composed about the king; my tongue is the pen of a ready writer.


## Psalms 45:2 (id: 919045002)

2You are fairer than the children of mankind; grace is poured onto your lips; therefore we know that God has blessed you forever.


## Psalms 45:3 (id: 919045003)

3Put your sword on your side, mighty one, in your glory and your majesty.


## Psalms 45:4 (id: 919045004)

4In your majesty ride on triumphantly because of trustworthiness, meekness, and righteousness; your right hand will teach you fearful things.


## Psalms 45:5 (id: 919045005)

5Your arrows are sharp; the peoples fall under you; your arrows are in the hearts of the king’s enemies.


## Psalms 45:6 (id: 919045006)

6Your throne, God, is forever and ever; a scepter of justice is the scepter of your kingdom.


## Psalms 45:7 (id: 919045007)

7You have loved righteousness and hated wickedness; therefore God, your God, has anointed you with the oil of gladness more than your companions.


## Psalms 45:8 (id: 919045008)

8All your garments smell of myrrh, aloes, and cassia; out of ivory palaces stringed instruments have made you glad.


## Psalms 45:9 (id: 919045009)

9Kings’ daughters are among your honorable women; at your right hand stands the queen clothed in gold of Ophir.


## Psalms 45:10 (id: 919045010)

10Listen, daughter, consider and incline your ear; forget your own people and your father’s house.


## Psalms 45:11 (id: 919045011)

11In this way the king will desire your beauty; he is your master; revere him.


## Psalms 45:12 (id: 919045012)

12The daughter of Tyre will be there with a gift; the rich among the people will beg for your favor.


## Psalms 45:13 (id: 919045013)

13The royal daughter in the palace is all glorious; her clothing is worked with gold.


## Psalms 45:14 (id: 919045014)

14She will be led to the king in embroidered dress; the virgins, her companions who follow her, will be brought to you.


## Psalms 45:15 (id: 919045015)

15They will be led by gladness and rejoicing; they will enter into the king’s palace.


## Psalms 45:16 (id: 919045016)

16In the place of your fathers will be your children, whom you will make princes in all the earth.


## Psalms 45:17 (id: 919045017)

17I will make your name to be remembered in all generations; therefore the peoples will give you thanks forever and ever.


## Psalms 46:1 (id: 919046001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of the sons of Korah; set to Alamoth. A song. God is our refuge and strength, a very present help in trouble.


## Psalms 46:2 (id: 919046002)

2Therefore we will not fear, though the earth should change, though the mountains should be shaken into the heart of the seas,


## Psalms 46:3 (id: 919046003)

3though its waters roar and rage, and though the mountains tremble with their swelling. Selah


## Psalms 46:4 (id: 919046004)

4There is a river whose streams make the city of God happy, the holy place where the Most High dwells.


## Psalms 46:5 (id: 919046005)

5God is in the middle of her; she will not be moved; God will help her, and he will do so at the dawn of morning.


## Psalms 46:6 (id: 919046006)

6The nations raged and the kingdoms were shaken; he lifted up his voice, and the earth melted.


## Psalms 46:7 (id: 919046007)

7Yahweh of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our refuge. 


## Psalms 46:8 (id: 919046008)

8Come, behold the deeds of Yahweh, the destruction he has caused on earth.


## Psalms 46:9 (id: 919046009)

9He makes wars cease to the ends of the earth; he breaks the bow and cuts the spear into pieces; he burns up the shields.


## Psalms 46:10 (id: 919046010)

10Be quiet and know that I am God; I will be exalted among the nations; I will be exalted on the earth.


## Psalms 46:11 (id: 919046011)

11Yahweh of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our refuge. 


## Psalms 47:1 (id: 919047001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of the sons of Korah. Clap your hands, all you peoples; shout to God with the sound of triumph.


## Psalms 47:2 (id: 919047002)

2For Yahweh Most High is terrifying; he is a great King over all the earth.


## Psalms 47:3 (id: 919047003)

3He subdues peoples under us and nations under our feet.


## Psalms 47:4 (id: 919047004)

4He chooses our inheritance for us, the glory of Jacob whom he loved. 


## Psalms 47:5 (id: 919047005)

5God has gone up with a shout, Yahweh with the sound of a trumpet.


## Psalms 47:6 (id: 919047006)

6Sing praises to God, sing praises; sing praises to our King, sing praises.


## Psalms 47:7 (id: 919047007)

7For God is the King over all the earth; sing praises with understanding.


## Psalms 47:8 (id: 919047008)

8God reigns over the nations; God sits on his holy throne.


## Psalms 47:9 (id: 919047009)

9The princes of the peoples have gathered together to the people of the God of Abraham; for the shields of the earth belong to God; he is greatly exalted.


## Psalms 48:1 (id: 919048001)

1A song; a psalm of the sons of Korah. Great is Yahweh and greatly to be praised, in the city of our God on his holy mountain.


## Psalms 48:2 (id: 919048002)

2Beautiful in elevation, the joy of the whole earth, is Mount Zion, on the sides of the north, the city of the great King.


## Psalms 48:3 (id: 919048003)

3God has made himself known in her palaces as a refuge.


## Psalms 48:4 (id: 919048004)

4For, see, the kings assembled themselves; they passed by together.


## Psalms 48:5 (id: 919048005)

5They saw it, then they were amazed; they were dismayed, and they hurried away.


## Psalms 48:6 (id: 919048006)

6Trembling took hold of them there, pain as when a woman is in labor.


## Psalms 48:7 (id: 919048007)

7With the east wind you break the ships of Tarshish.


## Psalms 48:8 (id: 919048008)

8As we have heard, so have we seen in the city of Yahweh of hosts, in the city of our God; God will establish it forever. 


## Psalms 48:9 (id: 919048009)

9We have thought about your covenant faithfulness, God, in the middle of your temple.


## Psalms 48:10 (id: 919048010)

10As your name is, God, so is your praise to the ends of the earth; your right hand is full of righteousness.


## Psalms 48:11 (id: 919048011)

11Let Mount Zion be glad, let the daughters of Judah rejoice because of your righteous decrees.


## Psalms 48:12 (id: 919048012)

12Walk around Mount Zion, go round about her; count her towers,


## Psalms 48:13 (id: 919048013)

13notice well her walls, and look at her palaces so that you may tell it to the next generation.


## Psalms 48:14 (id: 919048014)

14For this God is our God forever and ever; he will be our guide to death.


## Psalms 49:1 (id: 919049001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of the sons of Korah. Hear this, all you peoples; give ear, all you inhabitants of the world,


## Psalms 49:2 (id: 919049002)

2both low and high, rich and poor together.


## Psalms 49:3 (id: 919049003)

3My mouth will speak wisdom and the meditation of my heart will be of understanding.


## Psalms 49:4 (id: 919049004)

4I will incline my ear to a parable; I will begin my parable with the harp.


## Psalms 49:5 (id: 919049005)

5Why should I fear the days of evil, when iniquity surrounds me at my heels?


## Psalms 49:6 (id: 919049006)

6Why should I fear those who trust in their wealth and boast about the amount of their riches?


## Psalms 49:7 (id: 919049007)

7It is certain that no one can redeem his brother or give God a ransom for him,


## Psalms 49:8 (id: 919049008)

8For the redemption of one’s life is costly, and no one can pay what we owe.


## Psalms 49:9 (id: 919049009)

9No one can live forever so that his body should not decay.


## Psalms 49:10 (id: 919049010)

10For he will see decay. Wise men die; the fool and the brute alike perish and leave their wealth to others.


## Psalms 49:11 (id: 919049011)

11Their inner thought is that their families will continue forever, and the places where they live, to all generations; they call their lands after their own names.


## Psalms 49:12 (id: 919049012)

12But man, having wealth, does not remain alive; he is like the beasts that perish.


## Psalms 49:13 (id: 919049013)

13This, their way, is their folly; yet after them, men approve of their sayings. 


## Psalms 49:14 (id: 919049014)

14Like sheep they are appointed for Sheol, and death will be their shepherd. The upright will rule over them in the morning, and their bodies will be consumed in Sheol, with no place for them to live.


## Psalms 49:15 (id: 919049015)

15But God will redeem my life from the power of Sheol; he will receive me. 


## Psalms 49:16 (id: 919049016)

16Do not be afraid when one becomes rich, and the glory of his house increases.


## Psalms 49:17 (id: 919049017)

17For when he dies he will take nothing away; his glory will not go down after him.


## Psalms 49:18 (id: 919049018)

18He blessed his soul while he lived— and men praise you when you live for yourself—


## Psalms 49:19 (id: 919049019)

19he will go to the generation of his fathers and they will never see the light again.


## Psalms 49:20 (id: 919049020)

20One who has wealth but no understanding is like the beasts, which perish.


## Psalms 50:1 (id: 919050001)

1A psalm of Asaph. A Psalm of Asaph The Mighty One, God, Yahweh, has spoken and called the earth from the rising of the sun to its setting.


## Psalms 50:2 (id: 919050002)

2Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God has shone.


## Psalms 50:3 (id: 919050003)

3Our God comes and does not stay silent; a fire devours before him, and it is very stormy around him.


## Psalms 50:4 (id: 919050004)

4He calls to the heavens above and to the earth so that he may judge his people:


## Psalms 50:5 (id: 919050005)

5“Gather my faithful ones together to me, those who have made a covenant with me by sacrifice.”


## Psalms 50:6 (id: 919050006)

6The heavens will declare his righteousness, for God himself is judge. 


## Psalms 50:7 (id: 919050007)

7“Israel, I will testify against you. Hear, my people, and I will speak; I am God, your God.


## Psalms 50:8 (id: 919050008)

8I will not reprove you for your sacrifices; your burnt offerings are always before me.


## Psalms 50:9 (id: 919050009)

9I will take no bull out of your house, or male goats out of your folds.


## Psalms 50:10 (id: 919050010)

10For every beast of the forest is mine, and the cattle on a thousand hills.


## Psalms 50:11 (id: 919050011)

11I know all the birds of the mountains, and the wild beasts of the field are mine.


## Psalms 50:12 (id: 919050012)

12If I were hungry, I would not tell you; for the world is mine, and everything in it.


## Psalms 50:13 (id: 919050013)

13Will I eat the flesh of bulls or drink the blood of goats?


## Psalms 50:14 (id: 919050014)

14Offer to God the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and pay your vows to the Most High.


## Psalms 50:15 (id: 919050015)

15Call on me in the day of trouble; I will rescue you, and you will glorify me.”


## Psalms 50:16 (id: 919050016)

16But to the wicked God says, “What have you to do with declaring my statutes, that you have taken my covenant in your mouth,


## Psalms 50:17 (id: 919050017)

17since you hate instruction and throw my words away?


## Psalms 50:18 (id: 919050018)

18When you see a thief, you agree with him; you participate with those who commit adultery.


## Psalms 50:19 (id: 919050019)

19You give your mouth to evil, and your tongue expresses deceit.


## Psalms 50:20 (id: 919050020)

20You sit and speak against your brother; you slander your own mother’s son.


## Psalms 50:21 (id: 919050021)

21You have done these things, but I have kept silent, so you thought that I was someone just like yourself. But I will reprove you and bring up, right before your eyes, all the things you have done.


## Psalms 50:22 (id: 919050022)

22Give this careful consideration, you who forget God, otherwise I will tear you to pieces, and there will be no one to come to help you!


## Psalms 50:23 (id: 919050023)

23The one who offers a sacrifice of thanksgiving praises me, and to anyone who plans his path in the right way I will show God’s salvation.”


## Psalms 51:1 (id: 919051001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David; when Nathan the prophet came to him after he had gone in to Bathsheba. Have mercy on me, God, because of your covenant faithfulness; for the sake of the multitude of your merciful actions, blot out my transgressions.


## Psalms 51:2 (id: 919051002)

2Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity and cleanse me from my sin.


## Psalms 51:3 (id: 919051003)

3For I know my transgressions, and my sin is always before me.


## Psalms 51:4 (id: 919051004)

4Against you, you only, I have sinned and done what is evil in your sight; you are right when you speak; you are correct when you judge.


## Psalms 51:5 (id: 919051005)

5See, I was born in iniquity; as soon as my mother conceived me, I was in sin.


## Psalms 51:6 (id: 919051006)

6See, you desire trustworthiness in my inner self; and you teach me wisdom in the secret place within.


## Psalms 51:7 (id: 919051007)

7Purify me with hyssop, and I will be clean; wash me, and I will be whiter than snow.


## Psalms 51:8 (id: 919051008)

8Make me hear joy and gladness so that the bones that you have broken may rejoice.


## Psalms 51:9 (id: 919051009)

9Hide your face from my sins and blot out all my iniquities.


## Psalms 51:10 (id: 919051010)

10Create in me a clean heart, God, and renew a right spirit within me.


## Psalms 51:11 (id: 919051011)

11Do not drive me away from your presence, and do not take your holy Spirit from me.


## Psalms 51:12 (id: 919051012)

12Restore to me the joy of your salvation, and sustain me with a willing spirit.


## Psalms 51:13 (id: 919051013)

13Then will I teach transgressors your ways, and sinners will be converted to you.


## Psalms 51:14 (id: 919051014)

14Forgive me for shedding blood, God of my salvation, and I will shout for the joy of your righteousness.


## Psalms 51:15 (id: 919051015)

15Lord, open my lips, and my mouth will express your praise.


## Psalms 51:16 (id: 919051016)

16For you do not delight in sacrifice, or I would give it; you have no pleasure in burnt offerings.


## Psalms 51:17 (id: 919051017)

17The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit. You, God, will not despise a broken and a contrite heart.


## Psalms 51:18 (id: 919051018)

18Do good in your good pleasure to Zion; rebuild the walls of Jerusalem.


## Psalms 51:19 (id: 919051019)

19Then will you delight in the sacrifices of righteousness, in burnt offerings and whole burnt offerings; then our people will offer bulls on your altar.


## Psalms 52:1 (id: 919052001)

1For the chief musician. A maschil of David; when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, and said to him, “David has come to the house of Ahimelech.” Why are you proud of making trouble, you mighty man? The covenant faithfulness of God comes every day.


## Psalms 52:2 (id: 919052002)

2Your tongue plans destruction like a sharp razor, working deceitfully.


## Psalms 52:3 (id: 919052003)

3You love evil more than good and lying rather than speaking righteousness. 


## Psalms 52:4 (id: 919052004)

4You love all words that devour others, you deceitful tongue.


## Psalms 52:5 (id: 919052005)

5God will likewise destroy you forever; he will take you up and pluck you out of your tent and root you out of the land of the living. 


## Psalms 52:6 (id: 919052006)

6The righteous will also see it and fear; they will laugh at him and say,


## Psalms 52:7 (id: 919052007)

7“See, this is a man who did not make God his refuge, but he trusted in the abundance of his wealth, and he was strong when he destroyed others.”


## Psalms 52:8 (id: 919052008)

8But as for me, I am like a green olive tree in God’s house; I will trust in the covenant faithfulness of God forever and ever.


## Psalms 52:9 (id: 919052009)

9I will give you thanks forever for what you have done. I will wait for your name, because it is good, in the presence of your faithful ones.


## Psalms 53:1 (id: 919053001)

1For the chief musician; set to Mahalath. A maschil of David. A fool says in his heart, “There is no God.” They are corrupt and have done abominable iniquity; there is no one who does good.


## Psalms 53:2 (id: 919053002)

2God looks down from heaven on the children of mankind to see if there are any who understand, who seek after him.


## Psalms 53:3 (id: 919053003)

3They have all turned away. Together they have become corrupt. There is not one who does good, not even one.


## Psalms 53:4 (id: 919053004)

4Do those who commit iniquity have no understanding— those who devour my people as if they were eating bread and they do not call on God?


## Psalms 53:5 (id: 919053005)

5They were in great fear, although no reason to fear was there; for God will scatter the bones of whoever will camp against you; such people will be put to shame because God has rejected them.


## Psalms 53:6 (id: 919053006)

6Oh, that the salvation of Israel would come from Zion! When God brings back his people from the captivity, then Jacob will rejoice and Israel will be glad!


## Psalms 54:1 (id: 919054001)

1For the chief musician; on stringed instruments. A maschil of David; when the Ziphites came and said to Saul, “Does David not hide himself with us?” Save me, God, by your name, and judge me in your might.


## Psalms 54:2 (id: 919054002)

2Hear my prayer, God; give ear to the words of my mouth.


## Psalms 54:3 (id: 919054003)

3For strangers have risen up against me, and pitiless men have sought after my life; they have not set God before them. Selah


## Psalms 54:4 (id: 919054004)

4See, God is my helper; the Lord is the one who upholds me.


## Psalms 54:5 (id: 919054005)

5He will repay my enemies with evil; in your faithfulness, destroy them!


## Psalms 54:6 (id: 919054006)

6I will sacrifice to you with a freewill offering; I will give thanks to your name, Yahweh, for it is good.


## Psalms 54:7 (id: 919054007)

7For he has rescued me from every trouble; my eye has looked in triumph on my enemies.


## Psalms 55:1 (id: 919055001)

1For the chief musician; on stringed instruments. A maschil of David. Give ear to my prayer, God; and do not hide yourself from my plea.


## Psalms 55:2 (id: 919055002)

2Pay attention to me and answer me; I have no rest in my troubles


## Psalms 55:3 (id: 919055003)

3because of the voice of my enemies, because of the oppression of the wicked; for they bring trouble on me and persecute me in anger.


## Psalms 55:4 (id: 919055004)

4My heart trembles within me, and the terrors of death have fallen on me.


## Psalms 55:5 (id: 919055005)

5Fearfulness and trembling have come on me, and horror has overwhelmed me.


## Psalms 55:6 (id: 919055006)

6I said, “Oh, if only I had wings like a dove! Then would I fly away and be at rest.


## Psalms 55:7 (id: 919055007)

7See, then I would wander far away; I would stay in the wilderness. 


## Psalms 55:8 (id: 919055008)

8I would hurry to a shelter from the stormy wind and tempest.”


## Psalms 55:9 (id: 919055009)

9Devour them, Lord, confuse their language! For I have seen violence and strife in the city.


## Psalms 55:10 (id: 919055010)

10Day and night they go about on its walls; wickedness and trouble are in the middle of it.


## Psalms 55:11 (id: 919055011)

11Wickedness is in the middle of it; oppression and deceit do not leave its streets.


## Psalms 55:12 (id: 919055012)

12For it was not an enemy who rebuked me, then I could have borne it; neither was it he who hated me who raised himself up against me, then I would have hidden myself from him.


## Psalms 55:13 (id: 919055013)

13But it was you, a man equal to myself, my companion and my close friend.


## Psalms 55:14 (id: 919055014)

14We had sweet fellowship together; we walked in the house of God with the throng.


## Psalms 55:15 (id: 919055015)

15Let death come suddenly on them; let them go down alive to Sheol, for wickedness is where they live, right among them.


## Psalms 55:16 (id: 919055016)

16As for me, I will call on God, and Yahweh will save me.


## Psalms 55:17 (id: 919055017)

17In the evening, morning and at noonday I complain and moan; he will hear my voice.


## Psalms 55:18 (id: 919055018)

18He will safely rescue my life from the battle that was against me, for those who fought against me were many.


## Psalms 55:19 (id: 919055019)

19God, the one who rules from eternity, will hear them and humiliate them. They never change, and they do not fear God.


## Psalms 55:20 (id: 919055020)

20My friend has raised his hands against those who were at peace with him; he has not respected the covenant that he had.


## Psalms 55:21 (id: 919055021)

21His mouth was smooth as butter, but his heart was hostile; his words were softer than oil, yet they were actually drawn swords.


## Psalms 55:22 (id: 919055022)

22Place your burdens on Yahweh, and he will sustain you; he will never allow a righteous person to totter.


## Psalms 55:23 (id: 919055023)

23But you, God, will bring the wicked down into the pit of destruction; bloodthirsty and deceitful men will not live even half as long as others, but I will trust in you.


## Psalms 56:1 (id: 919056001)

1For the chief musician; set to Jonath elem rehokim. A psalm of David. A michtam; when the Philistines took him in Gath. Be merciful to me, God, for men are attacking me! All the day long those who fight me press their assault.


## Psalms 56:2 (id: 919056002)

2My enemies trample me all day long; for there are many who arrogantly fight against me.


## Psalms 56:3 (id: 919056003)

3When I am afraid, I will put my trust in you.


## Psalms 56:4 (id: 919056004)

4In God, whose word I praise— in God I have put my trust; I will not be afraid; what can mere man do to me?


## Psalms 56:5 (id: 919056005)

5All the day long they twist my words; all their thoughts are against me for evil.


## Psalms 56:6 (id: 919056006)

6They gather themselves together, they hide themselves, and they mark my steps, just as they have waited for my life.


## Psalms 56:7 (id: 919056007)

7Do not let them escape doing iniquity. Bring down the peoples in your anger, God.


## Psalms 56:8 (id: 919056008)

8You number my wanderings and put my tears into your bottle; are they not in your book?


## Psalms 56:9 (id: 919056009)

9Then my enemies will turn back on the day that I call to you; this I know, that God is for me.


## Psalms 56:10 (id: 919056010)

10In God—whose word I praise, in Yahweh—whose word I praise,


## Psalms 56:11 (id: 919056011)

11in God I trust, I will not be afraid. What can anyone do to me?


## Psalms 56:12 (id: 919056012)

12The duty to fulfill my vows to you is on me, God; I will give thank offerings to you.


## Psalms 56:13 (id: 919056013)

13For you have rescued my life from death; you have kept my feet from falling, so that I may walk before God in the light of the living.


## Psalms 57:1 (id: 919057001)

1For the chief musician; set to Al Tashheth. A psalm of David. A michtam; when he fled from Saul, in the cave. Be merciful to me, God, be merciful to me, for I take refuge in you until these troubles are over. I stay under your wings for protection until this destruction is over.


## Psalms 57:2 (id: 919057002)

2I will cry to God Most High, to God, who does all things for me.


## Psalms 57:3 (id: 919057003)

3He will send help from heaven and save me, he is angry with those who crush me. God will send me his loving kindness and his faithfulness.


## Psalms 57:4 (id: 919057004)

4My life is among lions; I am among those who are ready to devour me. I am among people whose teeth are spears and arrows, and whose tongues are sharp swords.


## Psalms 57:5 (id: 919057005)

5Be exalted, God, above the heavens; let your glory be above all the earth.


## Psalms 57:6 (id: 919057006)

6They spread out a net for my feet; I was distressed. They dug a pit in front of me. They themselves have fallen into the middle of it! 


## Psalms 57:7 (id: 919057007)

7My heart is fixed, God, my heart is fixed; I will sing, yes, I will sing praises.


## Psalms 57:8 (id: 919057008)

8Wake up, my honored heart; wake up, lute and harp; I will wake up the dawn.


## Psalms 57:9 (id: 919057009)

9I will give thanks to you, Lord, among the peoples; I will sing praises to you among the nations.


## Psalms 57:10 (id: 919057010)

10For great is your unfailing love, reaching to the heavens; and your faithfulness to the clouds.


## Psalms 57:11 (id: 919057011)

11Be exalted, God, above the heavens; may your glory be exalted over all the earth.


## Psalms 58:1 (id: 919058001)

1For the chief musician; set to Al Tashheth. A psalm of David. A michtam. Do you indeed rulers speak righteousness you silent ones? Do you judge uprightly, you people?


## Psalms 58:2 (id: 919058002)

2No, you commit wickedness in your heart; you distribute violence throughout the land with your hands.


## Psalms 58:3 (id: 919058003)

3The wicked go astray even when they are in the womb; they go astray from birth, speaking lies.


## Psalms 58:4 (id: 919058004)

4Their poison is like a snake’s poison; they are like a deaf adder that stops up its ears,


## Psalms 58:5 (id: 919058005)

5that pays no attention to the voice of charmers, no matter how skillful they are.


## Psalms 58:6 (id: 919058006)

6Break their teeth in their mouths, God; break out the great teeth of the young lions, Yahweh.


## Psalms 58:7 (id: 919058007)

7Let them melt away as water that runs off; when they shoot their arrows, let them be as though they had no points.


## Psalms 58:8 (id: 919058008)

8Let them be like a snail that melts and passes away, like the untimely\-born child of a woman that never sees the sunlight.


## Psalms 58:9 (id: 919058009)

9Before your pots can feel the thorn’s burning heat, he will take them away with a whirlwind, the green thorns and the burning thorns alike.


## Psalms 58:10 (id: 919058010)

10The righteous will rejoice when he sees God’s vengeance; he will wash his feet in the blood of the wicked,


## Psalms 58:11 (id: 919058011)

11so that men will say, “Truly, there is a reward for the righteous person; truly there is a God who judges the earth.”


## Psalms 59:1 (id: 919059001)

1For the chief musician; set to Al Tashheth. A psalm of David. A michtam; when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him. Rescue me from my enemies, my God; set me on high away from those who rise up against me.


## Psalms 59:2 (id: 919059002)

2Keep me safe from the workers of iniquity, and save me from the bloodthirsty men.


## Psalms 59:3 (id: 919059003)

3For, see, they wait in ambush to take my life. The powerful men gather themselves together against me, but not because of my transgression or my sin, Yahweh.


## Psalms 59:4 (id: 919059004)

4They prepare to run at me although I am without fault; awake and help me and see.


## Psalms 59:5 (id: 919059005)

5You, Yahweh God of hosts, the God of Israel, arise and punish all the nations; do not be merciful to any wicked transgressors. 


## Psalms 59:6 (id: 919059006)

6They return at evening, they howl like dogs and go around the city.


## Psalms 59:7 (id: 919059007)

7See, they belch out with their mouths; swords are in their lips, for they say, “Who hears us?”


## Psalms 59:8 (id: 919059008)

8But you, Yahweh, laugh at them; you hold all the nations in derision.


## Psalms 59:9 (id: 919059009)

9God, my strength, I will pay attention to you; you are my high tower.


## Psalms 59:10 (id: 919059010)

10My God will meet me with his covenant faithfulness; God will let me see my desire on my enemies.


## Psalms 59:11 (id: 919059011)

11Do not kill them, or my people will forget. Scatter them by your power and make them fall, Lord our shield.


## Psalms 59:12 (id: 919059012)

12For the sins of their mouths and the words of their lips, let them be captured in their pride, and for the curses and lies that they express.


## Psalms 59:13 (id: 919059013)

13Consume them in wrath, consume them so that they will be no more; let them know that God rules in Jacob and to the ends of the earth. 


## Psalms 59:14 (id: 919059014)

14At evening they return, howling like dogs going around the city.


## Psalms 59:15 (id: 919059015)

15They wander about looking for food and they growl like a dog if they are not satisfied.


## Psalms 59:16 (id: 919059016)

16But I will sing about your strength, and in the morning I will sing about your steadfast love! For you have been my high tower and a refuge in the day of my distress.


## Psalms 59:17 (id: 919059017)

17To you, my strength, I will sing praises; for God is my high tower, the God of covenant faithfulness.


## Psalms 60:1 (id: 919060001)

1For the chief musician; set to Shushan Eduth. A michtam of David, for teaching. When he fought with Aram Naharaim and with Aram Zobah, and Joab returned and killed twelve thousand Edomites in the Valley of Salt. God, you have cast us off; you have broken through our defenses; you have been angry; restore us again.


## Psalms 60:2 (id: 919060002)

2You have made the land tremble; you have torn it apart; heal its fissures, for it is shaking.


## Psalms 60:3 (id: 919060003)

3You have made your people see difficult things; you have made us drink the wine of staggering.


## Psalms 60:4 (id: 919060004)

4For those who honor you, you have set up a banner to be displayed against those who carry the bow. 


## Psalms 60:5 (id: 919060005)

5So that those you love may be rescued, rescue us with your right hand and answer me.


## Psalms 60:6 (id: 919060006)

6God has spoken in his holiness, “I will rejoice; I will divide Shechem and apportion out the Valley of Succoth.


## Psalms 60:7 (id: 919060007)

7Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is my helmet; Judah is my scepter.


## Psalms 60:8 (id: 919060008)

8Moab is my washbasin; over Edom I will throw my shoe; I will shout in triumph because of Philistia.”


## Psalms 60:9 (id: 919060009)

9Who will bring me into the strong city? Who will lead me to Edom?


## Psalms 60:10 (id: 919060010)

10But you, God, have you not rejected us? You do not go into battle with our army.


## Psalms 60:11 (id: 919060011)

11Give us help against the enemy, for man’s help is futile.


## Psalms 60:12 (id: 919060012)

12We will triumph with God’s help; he will trample down our enemies.


## Psalms 61:1 (id: 919061001)

1For the chief musician; on a stringed instrument. A psalm of David. Hear my cry, God; attend to my prayer.


## Psalms 61:2 (id: 919061002)

2From the ends of the earth will I call to you when my heart is faint; lead me to the rock that is higher than I.


## Psalms 61:3 (id: 919061003)

3For you have been a refuge for me, a strong tower from the enemy.


## Psalms 61:4 (id: 919061004)

4Let me live in your tabernacle forever! Let me take refuge under the shelter of your wings. 


## Psalms 61:5 (id: 919061005)

5For you, God, have heard my vows, you have given me the inheritance of those who honor your name.


## Psalms 61:6 (id: 919061006)

6You will prolong the king’s life; his years will be like many generations.


## Psalms 61:7 (id: 919061007)

7Oh prepare mercy and truth which may preserve him. He will remain before God forever.


## Psalms 61:8 (id: 919061008)

8I will sing praise to your name forever so that I may perform my vows every day.


## Psalms 62:1 (id: 919062001)

1For the chief musician; after the manner of Jeduthun. A psalm of David. I wait in silence for God alone; my salvation comes from him.


## Psalms 62:2 (id: 919062002)

2He alone is my rock and my salvation; he is my high tower; I will not be greatly moved.


## Psalms 62:3 (id: 919062003)

3How long, all of you, will you attack a man, that you may tip him over like a leaning wall or a shaky fence?


## Psalms 62:4 (id: 919062004)

4They consult with him only to bring him down from his honorable position; they love to tell lies; they bless him with their mouths, but in their hearts they curse him. 


## Psalms 62:5 (id: 919062005)

5I wait in silence for God alone; for my hope is set on him.


## Psalms 62:6 (id: 919062006)

6He alone is my rock and my salvation; he is my high tower; I will not be moved.


## Psalms 62:7 (id: 919062007)

7With God is my salvation and my glory; the rock of my strength and my refuge are in God.


## Psalms 62:8 (id: 919062008)

8Trust in him at all times, you people; pour out your heart before him; God is a refuge for us. 


## Psalms 62:9 (id: 919062009)

9Surely men of low standing are vanity, and men of high standing are a lie; they will weigh lightly in the scales; weighed together, they are lighter than nothing.


## Psalms 62:10 (id: 919062010)

10Do not trust in oppression or robbery; and do not hope uselessly in riches, for they will bear no fruit; do not fix your heart on them.


## Psalms 62:11 (id: 919062011)

11God has spoken once, twice have I heard this: power belongs to God.


## Psalms 62:12 (id: 919062012)

12Also to you, Lord, belongs covenant faithfulness, for you pay back every person for what he has done.


## Psalms 63:1 (id: 919063001)

1A psalm of David, when he was in the wilderness of Judah. God, you are my God! I earnestly search for you, my soul thirsts for you, and my flesh longs for you, in a dry and weary land where there is no water.


## Psalms 63:2 (id: 919063002)

2So I have looked on you in the sanctuary, to see your power and your glory.


## Psalms 63:3 (id: 919063003)

3Because your covenant faithfulness is better than life, my lips will praise you.


## Psalms 63:4 (id: 919063004)

4So I will bless you with my life; I will lift up my hands in your name.


## Psalms 63:5 (id: 919063005)

5It will be like when my throat is satisfied with fatty meats and rich foods; with joyful lips my mouth will praise you,


## Psalms 63:6 (id: 919063006)

6when I remember you on my bed and meditate on you in the night hours.


## Psalms 63:7 (id: 919063007)

7For you have been my help, and in the shadow of your wings I rejoice.


## Psalms 63:8 (id: 919063008)

8My soul clings to you; your right hand supports me.


## Psalms 63:9 (id: 919063009)

9But those who seek to destroy my life will go down into the lowest parts of the earth;


## Psalms 63:10 (id: 919063010)

10they will be given over to the power of the sword, and they will become food for the jackals.


## Psalms 63:11 (id: 919063011)

11But the king will rejoice in God; everyone who swears by him will exult, but the mouth of those who speak lies will be shut.


## Psalms 64:1 (id: 919064001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. Hear my voice, God, listen to my complaint; preserve my life from fear of my enemies.


## Psalms 64:2 (id: 919064002)

2Hide me from the secret plotting of evildoers, from the commotion of the doers of iniquity.


## Psalms 64:3 (id: 919064003)

3They have sharpened their tongues like swords; they have aimed their arrows, bitter words,


## Psalms 64:4 (id: 919064004)

4so that they may shoot from secret places at someone who is innocent; suddenly they shoot at him and fear nothing.


## Psalms 64:5 (id: 919064005)

5They encourage themselves in an evil plan; they consult privately together in order to set traps; they say, “Who will see us?”


## Psalms 64:6 (id: 919064006)

6They invent sinful plans; “We have finished,” they say, “a careful plan.” The inner thoughts and hearts of man are deep.


## Psalms 64:7 (id: 919064007)

7But God will shoot them; suddenly they will be wounded with his arrows.


## Psalms 64:8 (id: 919064008)

8They will be made to stumble, since their own tongues are against them; all who see them will wag their heads.


## Psalms 64:9 (id: 919064009)

9All people will fear and will declare God’s deeds. They will wisely think about what he has done.


## Psalms 64:10 (id: 919064010)

10The righteous will be glad about Yahweh and will take refuge in him; all the upright in heart will take pride in him.


## Psalms 65:1 (id: 919065001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm. A song of David. For you, God in Zion, our praise waits; our vows will be carried out to you.


## Psalms 65:2 (id: 919065002)

2You who hear prayer, to you all flesh will come.


## Psalms 65:3 (id: 919065003)

3Iniquities prevail against us; as for our transgressions, you will forgive them.


## Psalms 65:4 (id: 919065004)

4Blessed is the man whom you choose to bring near to you so that he may live in your courts. We will be satisfied with the goodness of your house, your holy temple.


## Psalms 65:5 (id: 919065005)

5In righteousness you will answer us by doing amazing things, God of our salvation; you who are hope of all the ends of the earth and of those who are far across the sea.


## Psalms 65:6 (id: 919065006)

6For it is you who made the mountains firm, you who are belted with strength.


## Psalms 65:7 (id: 919065007)

7It is you who quiet the roaring of the seas, the roaring of their waves, and the commotion of the peoples.


## Psalms 65:8 (id: 919065008)

8Those who live in the uttermost parts of the earth are afraid of the evidence of your deeds; you make the east and the west rejoice.


## Psalms 65:9 (id: 919065009)

9You come to help the earth; you water it; you greatly enrich it; the river of God is full of water; you provide mankind grain when you have prepared the earth.


## Psalms 65:10 (id: 919065010)

10You water its furrows abundantly; you settle down the furrows’ ridges; you make them soft with rain showers; you bless the sprouts between them.


## Psalms 65:11 (id: 919065011)

11You crown the year with your goodness, and your wagon tracks overflow with abundance.


## Psalms 65:12 (id: 919065012)

12The pastures in the wilderness drip with dew, and the hills are clothed with joy.


## Psalms 65:13 (id: 919065013)

13The pastures are clothed with flocks; the valleys also are covered over with grain; they shout for joy, and they sing.


## Psalms 66:1 (id: 919066001)

1For the chief musician. A song, a psalm. To the chief musician. A song. A psalm. Make a joyful noise to God, all the earth;


## Psalms 66:2 (id: 919066002)

2Sing out the glory of his name; make his praise glorious.


## Psalms 66:3 (id: 919066003)

3Say to God, “How terrifying are your deeds! By the greatness of your power your enemies will submit to you.


## Psalms 66:4 (id: 919066004)

4All the earth will worship you and will sing to you; they will sing to your name.” 


## Psalms 66:5 (id: 919066005)

5Come and see the works of God; he is fearsome in his deeds toward the sons of mankind.


## Psalms 66:6 (id: 919066006)

6He turned the sea into dry land; they went through the river on foot; there we rejoiced in him.


## Psalms 66:7 (id: 919066007)

7He rules forever by his might; his eyes observe the nations; let not the rebellious exalt themselves. 


## Psalms 66:8 (id: 919066008)

8Give blessing to God, you people, let the sound of his praise be heard.


## Psalms 66:9 (id: 919066009)

9He keeps us among the living, and he does not permit our feet to slip.


## Psalms 66:10 (id: 919066010)

10For you, God, have tested us; you have tested us as silver is tested.


## Psalms 66:11 (id: 919066011)

11You brought us into a net; you laid a heavy burden on our backs.


## Psalms 66:12 (id: 919066012)

12You made people ride over our heads; we went through fire and water, but you brought us out into a spacious place.


## Psalms 66:13 (id: 919066013)

13I will come into your house with burnt offerings; I will pay you my vows


## Psalms 66:14 (id: 919066014)

14which my lips promised and my mouth spoke when I was in distress.


## Psalms 66:15 (id: 919066015)

15I will offer to you burnt offerings of fat animals with the sweet aroma of rams; I will offer bulls and goats. 


## Psalms 66:16 (id: 919066016)

16Come and listen, all you who fear God, and I will declare what he has done for my soul.


## Psalms 66:17 (id: 919066017)

17I cried to him with my mouth, and he was praised with my tongue.


## Psalms 66:18 (id: 919066018)

18If I had seen sin within my heart, the Lord would not have listened to me.


## Psalms 66:19 (id: 919066019)

19But God has truly heard; he has paid attention to the voice of my prayer.


## Psalms 66:20 (id: 919066020)

20Blessed be God, who has not turned away my prayer or his covenant faithfulness from me.


## Psalms 67:1 (id: 919067001)

## Psalms 67:2 (id: 919067002)

2so that your ways may be known on earth, your salvation among all nations.


## Psalms 67:3 (id: 919067003)

3Let the peoples praise you, God; let all the peoples praise you.


## Psalms 67:4 (id: 919067004)

4Let the nations be glad and sing for joy, for you will judge the peoples with uprightness and govern the nations on earth. 


## Psalms 67:5 (id: 919067005)

5Let the peoples praise you, God; let all the peoples praise you.


## Psalms 67:6 (id: 919067006)

6The earth has yielded its harvest; God, our God, will bless us.


## Psalms 67:7 (id: 919067007)

## Psalms 68:1 (id: 919068001)

1For the chief musician; A psalm of David, a song. Let God arise; let his enemies be scattered; let those also who hate him flee before him.


## Psalms 68:2 (id: 919068002)

2As smoke is driven away, so drive them away; as wax melts before the fire, so let the wicked perish in the presence of God.


## Psalms 68:3 (id: 919068003)

3But let the righteous be glad; let them exult before God; may they rejoice and be happy.


## Psalms 68:4 (id: 919068004)

4Sing to God! Sing praises to his name! Praise the one who rides through the plains of the Jordan River valley! Yahweh is his name! Rejoice before him!


## Psalms 68:5 (id: 919068005)

5A father of the fatherless, a judge of the widows, is God in the holy place where he lives.


## Psalms 68:6 (id: 919068006)

6God puts the lonely into families; he brings out the prisoners to live in prosperity; but the rebellious live in a parched land.


## Psalms 68:7 (id: 919068007)

7God, when you went out before your people, when you marched through the wilderness, 


## Psalms 68:8 (id: 919068008)

8The earth trembled; the heavens also dropped rain in God’s presence, in the presence of God when he came to Sinai, in the presence of God, the God of Israel.


## Psalms 68:9 (id: 919068009)

9You, God, sent a plentiful rain; you strengthened your inheritance when it was weary.


## Psalms 68:10 (id: 919068010)

10Your people lived in it; You, God, gave from your goodness to the poor.


## Psalms 68:11 (id: 919068011)

11The Lord gave the orders, and those who announced them were a great army.


## Psalms 68:12 (id: 919068012)

12Kings of armies flee, they flee, and the women waiting at home divide the plunder:


## Psalms 68:13 (id: 919068013)

13Though you lie down among the sheepfolds, You will be like the wings of a dove covered with silver, And her feathers with yellow gold


## Psalms 68:14 (id: 919068014)

14The Almighty scattered kings there, it was as when it snowed on Mount Zalmon.


## Psalms 68:15 (id: 919068015)

15A mighty mountain is the hill country of Bashan; a high mountain is the hill country of Bashan.


## Psalms 68:16 (id: 919068016)

16Why do you look in envy, you high hill country, at the mountain which God desires for the place he will live? Indeed, Yahweh will live in it forever.


## Psalms 68:17 (id: 919068017)

17The chariots of God are twenty thousand, thousands upon thousands; the Lord is among them in the holy place, as at Sinai.


## Psalms 68:18 (id: 919068018)

18You have ascended on high; you have led away captives; you have received gifts from among men, even from those who fought against you, so that you, Yahweh God, might live there.


## Psalms 68:19 (id: 919068019)

19Blessed be the Lord, who daily bears our burdens, the God who is our salvation. 


## Psalms 68:20 (id: 919068020)

20Our God is a God who saves; Yahweh the Lord is the one who is able to rescue us from death.


## Psalms 68:21 (id: 919068021)

21But God will strike through the heads of his enemies, through the hairy scalps of those who walk in offenses against him.


## Psalms 68:22 (id: 919068022)

22The Lord said, “I will bring my enemies back from Bashan; I will bring them back from the depths of the sea


## Psalms 68:23 (id: 919068023)

23so that you may crush your enemies, dipping your foot in blood, and so that the tongues of your dogs may have their share from your enemies.”


## Psalms 68:24 (id: 919068024)

24They have seen your processions, God, the processions of my God, my King, into the holy place.


## Psalms 68:25 (id: 919068025)

25The singers went first, the minstrels followed after, and in the middle were the unmarried girls playing tambourines.


## Psalms 68:26 (id: 919068026)

26Bless God in the assemblies; praise Yahweh, you who are from the fountain of Israel.


## Psalms 68:27 (id: 919068027)

27There is first Benjamin, the smallest tribe, then the leaders of Judah and their multitudes, the leaders of Zebulun and the leaders of Naphtali.


## Psalms 68:28 (id: 919068028)

28Your God, Israel, has decreed your strength; reveal to us your power, God, as you have revealed it in times past.


## Psalms 68:29 (id: 919068029)

29Reveal your power to us from your temple at Jerusalem, where kings bring gifts to you.


## Psalms 68:30 (id: 919068030)

30Shout in battle against the wild beasts in the reeds, against the peoples, that multitude of bulls and calves. Humiliate them and make them bring you gifts; scatter the peoples who love to wage war.


## Psalms 68:31 (id: 919068031)

31Princes will come out of Egypt; Cush will hurry to reach out with her hands to God.


## Psalms 68:32 (id: 919068032)

32Sing to God, you kingdoms of the earth; Selah Sing praises to Yahweh.


## Psalms 68:33 (id: 919068033)

33To him who rides on the heaven of heavens, which exist from ancient times; see, he lifts up his voice with power.


## Psalms 68:34 (id: 919068034)

34Ascribe strength to God; his majesty is over Israel, and his strength is in the skies.


## Psalms 68:35 (id: 919068035)

35God, you are fearsome in your holy place; the God of Israel—he gives strength and power to his people. Blessed be God.


## Psalms 69:1 (id: 919069001)

1For the chief musician; set to Shoshannim. A psalm of David. Save me, God; for the waters have put my life in danger.


## Psalms 69:2 (id: 919069002)

2I sink in deep mire, where there is no place to stand; I have come into deep waters, where the floods flow over me.


## Psalms 69:3 (id: 919069003)

3I am weary with my crying; my throat is dry; my eyes fail while I wait for my God.


## Psalms 69:4 (id: 919069004)

4Those who hate me without a cause are more than the hairs on my head; those who would cut me off, being my enemies for wrong reasons, are mighty; what I did not steal, I have to give back.


## Psalms 69:5 (id: 919069005)

5God, you know my foolishness, and my sins are not hidden from you.


## Psalms 69:6 (id: 919069006)

6Let not those who hope in you be put to shame because of me, Lord Yahweh of hosts; let not those who seek you be brought to dishonor because of me, God of Israel.


## Psalms 69:7 (id: 919069007)

7For your sake I have borne rebuke; shame has covered my face.


## Psalms 69:8 (id: 919069008)

8I have become a stranger to my brothers, an alien to my mother’s children.


## Psalms 69:9 (id: 919069009)

9For the zeal of your house has eaten me up, and the rebukes of those who rebuke you have fallen on me.


## Psalms 69:10 (id: 919069010)

10When I wept and did not eat food, they insulted me.


## Psalms 69:11 (id: 919069011)

11When I made sackcloth my clothing, I became the object of a proverb to them.


## Psalms 69:12 (id: 919069012)

12Those who sit in the city gate talk about me; I am a song of drunkards.


## Psalms 69:13 (id: 919069013)

13But as for me, my prayer is to you, Yahweh, in the acceptable time; in the multitude of your mercy, hear me in the truth of your salvation.


## Psalms 69:14 (id: 919069014)

14Pull me out of the mire, and do not let me sink; let me be taken away from those who hate me and rescued out of the deep waters.


## Psalms 69:15 (id: 919069015)

15Do not let the floods of water overwhelm me, neither let the deep swallow me up. Do not let the pit shut its mouth on me.


## Psalms 69:16 (id: 919069016)

16Answer me, Yahweh, for your covenant faithfulness is good; because your mercies for me are many, turn to me.


## Psalms 69:17 (id: 919069017)

17Do not hide your face from your servant, for I am in distress; answer me quickly.


## Psalms 69:18 (id: 919069018)

18Come to me and redeem me. Because of my enemies, ransom me.


## Psalms 69:19 (id: 919069019)

19You know my rebuke, my shame, and my dishonor; my adversaries are all before you.


## Psalms 69:20 (id: 919069020)

20Rebuke has broken my heart; I am full of heaviness; I looked for someone to take pity, but there was none; I looked for comforters, but I found none.


## Psalms 69:21 (id: 919069021)

21They gave me poison for my food; in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.


## Psalms 69:22 (id: 919069022)

22Let their table before them become a snare; when they think they are in safety, let it become a trap.


## Psalms 69:23 (id: 919069023)

23Let their eyes be darkened so that they cannot see; and always make their loins shake.


## Psalms 69:24 (id: 919069024)

24Pour out your indignation on them, and let the fierceness of your anger overtake them.


## Psalms 69:25 (id: 919069025)

25Let their place be a desolation; let no one live in their tents.


## Psalms 69:26 (id: 919069026)

26For they persecuted the one you struck down. They repeated the account of the pain of those you have wounded.


## Psalms 69:27 (id: 919069027)

27Accuse them of having committed iniquity after iniquity; do not let them come into your righteous victory.


## Psalms 69:28 (id: 919069028)

28Let them be blotted out of the Book of Life and not be written down along with the righteous.


## Psalms 69:29 (id: 919069029)

29But I am poor and sorrowful; let your salvation, God, set me up on high.


## Psalms 69:30 (id: 919069030)

30I will praise the name of God with a song and will exalt him with thanksgiving.


## Psalms 69:31 (id: 919069031)

31That will please Yahweh better than an ox or a bull that has horns and hooves.


## Psalms 69:32 (id: 919069032)

32The meek have seen it and are glad; you who seek after God, let your hearts live.


## Psalms 69:33 (id: 919069033)

33For Yahweh hears the needy and does not despise his prisoners.


## Psalms 69:34 (id: 919069034)

34Let heaven and earth praise him, the seas and everything that moves in them.


## Psalms 69:35 (id: 919069035)

35For God will save Zion and will rebuild the cities of Judah; the people will live there and have it as a possession.


## Psalms 69:36 (id: 919069036)

36His servants’ descendants will inherit it; and those who love his name will live there.


## Psalms 70:1 (id: 919070001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David; to bring to remembrance. Save me, God! Yahweh, come quickly and help me.


## Psalms 70:2 (id: 919070002)

2Let those who try to take my life be ashamed and humiliated; let them be turned back and brought to dishonor, those who take pleasure in my pain.


## Psalms 70:3 (id: 919070003)

3Let them be turned back because of their shame, those who say, “Aha, aha.”


## Psalms 70:4 (id: 919070004)

4Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you; let those who love your salvation always say, “May God be praised.”


## Psalms 70:5 (id: 919070005)

5But I am poor and needy; hurry to me, God; you are my help and you rescue me. Yahweh, do not delay.


## Psalms 71:1 (id: 919071001)

1In you, Yahweh, I take refuge; let me never be put to shame.


## Psalms 71:2 (id: 919071002)

2Rescue me and make me safe in your righteousness; turn your ear to me and save me.


## Psalms 71:3 (id: 919071003)

3Be to me a rock for refuge where I may always go; you have given a command to save me, for you are my rock and my fortress.


## Psalms 71:4 (id: 919071004)

4Rescue me, my God, out of the hand of the wicked, out of the hand of the unrighteous and cruel.


## Psalms 71:5 (id: 919071005)

5For you are my hope, Lord Yahweh. I have trusted in you ever since I was a child.


## Psalms 71:6 (id: 919071006)

6By you I have been supported from the womb; you are he who took me out of my mother’s belly; my praise will be always about you.


## Psalms 71:7 (id: 919071007)

7I am an example to many people; you are my strong refuge.


## Psalms 71:8 (id: 919071008)

8My mouth will be filled with your praise, all the day with your honor.


## Psalms 71:9 (id: 919071009)

9Do not throw me away in my time of old age; do not abandon me when my strength fails.


## Psalms 71:10 (id: 919071010)

10For my enemies are talking about me; those who watch for my life are plotting together.


## Psalms 71:11 (id: 919071011)

11They say, “God has forsaken him; pursue and take him, for there is no one to save him.”


## Psalms 71:12 (id: 919071012)

12God, do not be far from me; my God, hurry to help me.


## Psalms 71:13 (id: 919071013)

13Let them be put to shame and destroyed, those who are hostile to my life; let them be covered with rebuke and dishonor, those who seek my hurt.


## Psalms 71:14 (id: 919071014)

14But I will always hope in you and will praise you more and more.


## Psalms 71:15 (id: 919071015)

15My mouth will tell about your righteousness and your salvation all the day, although I cannot understand it.


## Psalms 71:16 (id: 919071016)

16I will come with the mighty acts of the Lord Yahweh; I will make mention of your righteousness, yours alone.


## Psalms 71:17 (id: 919071017)

17God, you have taught me from my youth; even now I declare your wonderful deeds.


## Psalms 71:18 (id: 919071018)

18Indeed, even when I am old and gray\-headed, God, do not forsake me, as I have been declaring your strength to the next generation, your power to everyone who is to come.


## Psalms 71:19 (id: 919071019)

19Your righteousness also, God, is very high; you who have done great things, God, who is like you?


## Psalms 71:20 (id: 919071020)

20You who made me see many troubles will revive us again and will bring us up again from the depths of the earth.


## Psalms 71:21 (id: 919071021)

21May you increase my honor; turn again and comfort me.


## Psalms 71:22 (id: 919071022)

22I will also give thanks to you with the harp for your trustworthiness, my God; to you I will sing praises with the harp, Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 71:23 (id: 919071023)

23My lips will shout for joy when I sing praises to you— even my soul, which you have redeemed.


## Psalms 71:24 (id: 919071024)

24My tongue will also talk about your righteousness all day long; for they have been put to shame and are confused, those who sought my hurt.


## Psalms 72:1 (id: 919072001)

1A psalm of Solomon. A Psalm of Solomon Give the king your righteous decrees, God, your righteousness to the king’s son.


## Psalms 72:2 (id: 919072002)

2May he judge your people with righteousness and your poor with justice.


## Psalms 72:3 (id: 919072003)

3May the mountains produce peace for the people; may the hills produce righteousness.


## Psalms 72:4 (id: 919072004)

4May he judge the poor of the people; may he save the children of the needy and break in pieces the oppressor.


## Psalms 72:5 (id: 919072005)

5May they honor you while the sun endures, and as long as the moon lasts throughout all generations.


## Psalms 72:6 (id: 919072006)

6May he come down like rain on the mown grass, like showers that water the earth.


## Psalms 72:7 (id: 919072007)

7May the righteous flourish in his days, and may there be an abundance of peace till the moon is no more.


## Psalms 72:8 (id: 919072008)

8May he have dominion from sea to sea, and from the River to the ends of the earth.


## Psalms 72:9 (id: 919072009)

9May those who live in the wilderness bow down before him; may his enemies lick the dust.


## Psalms 72:10 (id: 919072010)

10May the kings of Tarshish and of the islands render tribute; may the kings of Sheba and Seba offer gifts.


## Psalms 72:11 (id: 919072011)

11Indeed, may all kings fall down before him; may all nations serve him.


## Psalms 72:12 (id: 919072012)

12For he helps the needy person who cries out and the poor person who has no other helper.


## Psalms 72:13 (id: 919072013)

13He has pity on the poor and needy, and he saves the lives of needy people.


## Psalms 72:14 (id: 919072014)

14He redeems their lives from oppression and violence, and their blood is precious in his sight.


## Psalms 72:15 (id: 919072015)

15May he live! May the gold of Sheba be given to him. May people always pray for him; may God bless him all day long.


## Psalms 72:16 (id: 919072016)

16May there be abundance of grain in the land; on the mountaintops may their crops wave. May the fruit of it be like Lebanon; may the people flourish in the cities like the grass of the field.


## Psalms 72:17 (id: 919072017)

17May his name endure forever; may his name continue as long as the sun; may people be blessed in him; may all nations call him blessed.


## Psalms 72:18 (id: 919072018)

18May Yahweh God, the God of Israel, be blessed, who alone does wonderful things.


## Psalms 72:19 (id: 919072019)

19May his glorious name be blessed forever, and may the whole earth be filled with his glory. Amen and Amen.


## Psalms 72:20 (id: 919072020)

20The prayers of David son of Jesse are finished.


## Psalms 73:1 (id: 919073001)

1A psalm of Asaph. A Psalm of Asaph. Surely God is good to Israel, to those with a pure heart.


## Psalms 73:2 (id: 919073002)

2But as for me, my feet almost slipped; my steps almost were caused to slide out {from under me}


## Psalms 73:3 (id: 919073003)

3because I was envious of the arrogant {when} I saw the prosperity of the wicked.


## Psalms 73:4 (id: 919073004)

4For {they have} no ropes until their death, and their belly is fat.


## Psalms 73:5 (id: 919073005)

5They {are} free from the trouble of man; and with {the rest of} man they are not afflicted.


## Psalms 73:6 (id: 919073006)

6Therefore pride is a necklace for them; a garment of violence covers them.


## Psalms 73:7 (id: 919073007)

7Their eyes bulge out from fatness; the imaginations of {their} heart overflow.


## Psalms 73:8 (id: 919073008)

8They mock and speak with evil of oppression; they speak from an elevated place.


## Psalms 73:9 (id: 919073009)

9They set their mouth in the heavens, and their tongue goes through the earth.


## Psalms 73:10 (id: 919073010)

10Therefore his people turn here, and waters of a full {cup} are drained by them.


## Psalms 73:11 (id: 919073011)

11And they say, “How does God know? And is there knowledge in the Most High?”


## Psalms 73:12 (id: 919073012)

12Behold, these wicked; they are always at ease, they increase in wealth.


## Psalms 73:13 (id: 919073013)

13Surely in vain I have kept my heart clean and washed my hands in innocence.


## Psalms 73:14 (id: 919073014)

14For I have been stricken all of the day, and punished every morning.


## Psalms 73:15 (id: 919073015)

15If I had said, “I will recount such things,” Behold, I would have betrayed the generation of your children.


## Psalms 73:16 (id: 919073016)

16And {when} I thought {how} to understand this, it {was} troublesome in my eyes


## Psalms 73:17 (id: 919073017)

17until I went into the sanctuaries of God; {then} I discerned their end.


## Psalms 73:18 (id: 919073018)

18Surely you set them in slippery places; you make them fall to destruction.


## Psalms 73:19 (id: 919073019)

19How they are {brought} to desolation as in a moment! They come to an end, they perish, by terrors.


## Psalms 73:20 (id: 919073020)

20Like a dream after {one} awakes; Lord, when you rouse {yourself}, you will despise their image.

21When my heart was embittered, and I was pierced in my kidneys,


## Psalms 73:22 (id: 919073022)

## Psalms 73:23 (id: 919073023)

23Yet I {am} continuously with you; you hold {me} by my right hand.


## Psalms 73:24 (id: 919073024)

## Psalms 73:26 (id: 919073026)

## Psalms 73:27 (id: 919073027)

## Psalms 73:28 (id: 919073028)
