## Psalms 74:1 (id: 919074001)

1A maschil of Asaph. A Maskil of Asaph. Why God, have you rejected {us} forever? {Why} does your nose smoke against the sheep of your pasture?


## Psalms 74:2 (id: 919074002)

2Remember your congregation, {whom} you aquired in ancient times, {which} you have redeemed to be the tribe of your inheritance; This Mount Zion, where you have dwelt.


## Psalms 74:3 (id: 919074003)

3Lift up your feet to the perpetual ruins; all the evil that the enemy has done in the sanctuary.


## Psalms 74:4 (id: 919074004)

4Your adversaries have roared in the middle of your meeting place; they have set up their signs as signs.


## Psalms 74:5 (id: 919074005)

5It is perceived like one bringing on high, axes against a forest of trees.


## Psalms 74:6 (id: 919074006)

6And now, with axe and hammers, they break down all its engravings.


## Psalms 74:7 (id: 919074007)

7They have set your sanctuary on fire to the ground; they have profaned the dwelling place of your name.


## Psalms 74:8 (id: 919074008)

8They said in their hearts, “We will oppress them altogether.” They have burned all of the meeting places of God in the land.


## Psalms 74:9 (id: 919074009)

9We do not see signs for us; {there is} no longer {any} prophet, and {there is} no one among us knowing how long this will last.


## Psalms 74:10 (id: 919074010)

10Until when, God, will the adversary reproach? Will the enemy treat your name with contempt forever?


## Psalms 74:11 (id: 919074011)

11Why do you withdraw your hand, your right hand? {Take it} from within the fold {of your garment and} destroy {them}.


## Psalms 74:12 (id: 919074012)

12Yet God {is} my king from ancient times, working acts of salvation in the midst of the earth.


## Psalms 74:13 (id: 919074013)

13You divided the sea by your strength; you smashed the heads of the sea monsters in the waters.


## Psalms 74:14 (id: 919074014)

14You crushed the heads of leviathan; you fed him to those living in the wilderness.


## Psalms 74:15 (id: 919074015)

15You broke open springs and streams; you dried up flowing rivers.


## Psalms 74:16 (id: 919074016)

16The day is yours, and the night is yours also; you set the sun and moon in place.


## Psalms 74:17 (id: 919074017)

17You have set all the borders of the earth; you have made summer and winter.


## Psalms 74:18 (id: 919074018)

18Call to mind how the enemy hurled insults at you, Yahweh, and that a foolish people has blasphemed your name.


## Psalms 74:19 (id: 919074019)

19Do not give the life of your dove to a wild animal. Do not forget forever the life of your oppressed people.


## Psalms 74:20 (id: 919074020)

20Remember your covenant, for the dark regions of the land are full of places of violence.


## Psalms 74:21 (id: 919074021)

21Do not let the oppressed be turned back in shame; let the poor and oppressed praise your name.


## Psalms 74:22 (id: 919074022)

22Arise, God; defend your own honor; call to mind how fools insult you all day long.


## Psalms 74:23 (id: 919074023)

23Do not forget the voice of your adversaries or the uproar of those who continually defy you.


## Psalms 75:1 (id: 919075001)

1For the chief musician; set to Al Tashheth. A psalm of Asaph, a song. We give thanks to you, God; we give thanks, for you reveal your presence; people tell of your wondrous works.


## Psalms 75:2 (id: 919075002)

2At the appointed time I will judge fairly.


## Psalms 75:3 (id: 919075003)

3Though the earth and all the inhabitants shake in fear, I make steady the earth’s pillars. Selah


## Psalms 75:4 (id: 919075004)

4I said to the arrogant, “Do not be arrogant,” and to the wicked, “Do not lift up the horn.


## Psalms 75:5 (id: 919075005)

5Do not lift up your horn to the heights; do not speak with an insolent neck.”


## Psalms 75:6 (id: 919075006)

6It is not from the east or from the west, and it is not from the wilderness that lifting up comes.


## Psalms 75:7 (id: 919075007)

7But God is the judge; he brings down one and he lifts up another.


## Psalms 75:8 (id: 919075008)

8For Yahweh holds in his hand a cup full of foaming wine, which is mixed with spices, and pours it out. Surely all the wicked of the earth will drink it to the last drop.


## Psalms 75:9 (id: 919075009)

9But I will continually tell what you have done; I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 75:10 (id: 919075010)

10He says, “I will cut off all the horns of the wicked, but the horns of the righteous will be raised up.”


## Psalms 76:1 (id: 919076001)

1For the chief musician, on stringed instruments. A psalm of Asaph, a song. God has made himself known in Judah; his name is great in Israel.


## Psalms 76:2 (id: 919076002)

2His tent is in Salem; his dwelling place is in Zion.


## Psalms 76:3 (id: 919076003)

3There he broke the arrows of the bow, the shield, the sword, and the other weapons of war. Selah


## Psalms 76:4 (id: 919076004)

4You shine brightly and reveal your glory, as you descend from the mountains, where you killed your victims.


## Psalms 76:5 (id: 919076005)

5The bravehearted were plundered; they fell asleep. All the warriors were helpless.


## Psalms 76:6 (id: 919076006)

6At your rebuke, God of Jacob, both rider and horse fell asleep.


## Psalms 76:7 (id: 919076007)

7You, yes you, are to be feared; who can stand in your sight when you are angry?


## Psalms 76:8 (id: 919076008)

8From heaven you made your judgment heard; the earth was afraid and silent


## Psalms 76:9 (id: 919076009)

9when you, God, arose to execute judgment and to save all the oppressed of the earth. 


## Psalms 76:10 (id: 919076010)

10Surely your angry judgment against humanity will bring you praise; you gird yourself with what is left of your anger.


## Psalms 76:11 (id: 919076011)

11Make vows to Yahweh your God and keep them. May all who surround him bring gifts to him who is to be feared.


## Psalms 76:12 (id: 919076012)

12He cuts off the spirit of the princes; he is feared by the kings of the earth.


## Psalms 77:1 (id: 919077001)

1For the chief musician; after the manner of Jeduthun. A psalm of Asaph. I will call out with my voice to God; I will call with my voice to God, and my God will hear me.


## Psalms 77:2 (id: 919077002)

2In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord; at night I stretched my hands out, and they would not become tired. My soul refused to be comforted.


## Psalms 77:3 (id: 919077003)

3I thought of God as I groaned; I thought about him as I grew faint. 


## Psalms 77:4 (id: 919077004)

4You held my eyes open; I was too troubled to speak.


## Psalms 77:5 (id: 919077005)

5I thought about the days of old, about times long past.


## Psalms 77:6 (id: 919077006)

6I call to remembrance my song in the night; I meditate within my heart, And my spirit makes diligent search.


## Psalms 77:7 (id: 919077007)

7Will the Lord reject me forever? Will he never again show me favor?


## Psalms 77:8 (id: 919077008)

8Was his covenant faithfulness gone forever? Had his promise failed forever?


## Psalms 77:9 (id: 919077009)

9Had God forgotten to be gracious? Had his anger shut off his compassion? 


## Psalms 77:10 (id: 919077010)

10I said, “This is my sorrow: the changing of the right hand of the Most High toward us.”


## Psalms 77:11 (id: 919077011)

11But I will call to mind your deeds, Yahweh; I will think about your wonderful deeds of old.


## Psalms 77:12 (id: 919077012)

12I will ponder all your deeds and will reflect on them.


## Psalms 77:13 (id: 919077013)

13Your way, God, is holy; what god compares to our great God?


## Psalms 77:14 (id: 919077014)

14You are the God who does wonders; you have revealed your strength among the peoples.


## Psalms 77:15 (id: 919077015)

15You gave your people victory by your great power— the descendants of Jacob and Joseph. 


## Psalms 77:16 (id: 919077016)

16The waters saw you, God; the waters saw you, and they were afraid; the depths trembled.


## Psalms 77:17 (id: 919077017)

17The clouds poured down water; the cloudy skies also gave voice; your arrows flew about.


## Psalms 77:18 (id: 919077018)

18Your thunderous voice was heard in the wind; the lightning lit up the world; the earth trembled and shook.


## Psalms 77:19 (id: 919077019)

19Your path went through the sea and your way through the surging waters, but your footprints were not seen.


## Psalms 77:20 (id: 919077020)

20You led your people like a flock by the hand of Moses and Aaron.


## Psalms 78:1 (id: 919078001)

1A maschil of Asaph. A writing of Asaph Hear my teaching, my people, listen to the words of my mouth.


## Psalms 78:2 (id: 919078002)

2I will open my mouth in parables; I will sing about hidden things about the past.


## Psalms 78:3 (id: 919078003)

3These are things that we have heard and learned, things that our ancestors have told us.


## Psalms 78:4 (id: 919078004)

4We will not keep them from their descendants. We will tell the next generation about the praiseworthy deeds of Yahweh, his strength, and the wonders that he has done.


## Psalms 78:5 (id: 919078005)

5For he established covenant decrees in Jacob and appointed a law in Israel. He commanded our ancestors that they were to teach them to their children.


## Psalms 78:6 (id: 919078006)

6He commanded this so that the generation to come might know his decrees, the children not yet born, who should tell them in turn to their own children.


## Psalms 78:7 (id: 919078007)

7Then they would place their hope in God and not forget his deeds but keep his commandments.


## Psalms 78:8 (id: 919078008)

8Then they would not be like their ancestors, who were a stubborn and rebellious generation, a generation whose hearts were not right, and whose spirits were not committed and faithful to God.


## Psalms 78:9 (id: 919078009)

9The Ephraimites were armed with bows, but they turned back on the day of battle.


## Psalms 78:10 (id: 919078010)

10They did not keep the covenant with God, and they refused to obey his law.


## Psalms 78:11 (id: 919078011)

11They forgot his deeds, the wonderful things that he had shown them.


## Psalms 78:12 (id: 919078012)

12They forgot the marvelous things he did in the sight of their ancestors in the land of Egypt, in the land of Zoan.


## Psalms 78:13 (id: 919078013)

13He divided the sea and led them across it; he made the waters to stand like walls.


## Psalms 78:14 (id: 919078014)

14In the daytime he led them with a cloud and all the night with the light of fire.


## Psalms 78:15 (id: 919078015)

15He split the rocks in the wilderness, and he gave them water abundantly, enough to fill the depths of the sea.


## Psalms 78:16 (id: 919078016)

16He made streams flow out of the rock and made the water flow like rivers.


## Psalms 78:17 (id: 919078017)

17Yet they continued to sin against him, rebelling against the Most High in the wilderness.


## Psalms 78:18 (id: 919078018)

18They challenged God in their hearts by asking for food to satisfy their appetites.


## Psalms 78:19 (id: 919078019)

19They spoke against God; they said, “Can God really lay out a table for us in the wilderness?


## Psalms 78:20 (id: 919078020)

20See, when he struck the rock, waters gushed out and streams overflowed. But can he give bread also? Will he provide meat for his people?”


## Psalms 78:21 (id: 919078021)

21When Yahweh heard this, he was angry; so his fire burned against Jacob, and his anger attacked Israel,


## Psalms 78:22 (id: 919078022)

22because they did not believe in God and did not trust in his salvation.


## Psalms 78:23 (id: 919078023)

23Yet he commanded the skies above and opened the doors of the sky.


## Psalms 78:24 (id: 919078024)

24He rained down manna for them to eat, and gave them the grain from heaven.


## Psalms 78:25 (id: 919078025)

25People ate the bread of angels. He sent them food in abundance.


## Psalms 78:26 (id: 919078026)

26He caused the east wind to blow in the sky, and by his power he guided the south wind.


## Psalms 78:27 (id: 919078027)

27He rained down meat on them like dust, birds as numerous as the sands of the sea.


## Psalms 78:28 (id: 919078028)

28They fell in the middle of their camp, all around their tents.


## Psalms 78:29 (id: 919078029)

29So they ate and were full. He gave them what they craved.


## Psalms 78:30 (id: 919078030)

30But they had not yet filled up; their food was still in their mouths.


## Psalms 78:31 (id: 919078031)

31Then God’s anger attacked them and killed the strongest of them. He brought down the young men of Israel.


## Psalms 78:32 (id: 919078032)

32Despite this, they continued to sin and did not believe his wonderful deeds.


## Psalms 78:33 (id: 919078033)

33Therefore God cut short their days; their years were filled with terror.


## Psalms 78:34 (id: 919078034)

34Whenever God afflicted them, they would start to seek him, and they would return and look earnestly for him.


## Psalms 78:35 (id: 919078035)

35They would call to mind that God was their rock and that the Most High God was their rescuer.


## Psalms 78:36 (id: 919078036)

36But they would flatter him with their mouth and lie to him with their words.


## Psalms 78:37 (id: 919078037)

37For their hearts were not firmly fixed on him, and they were not faithful to his covenant.


## Psalms 78:38 (id: 919078038)

38Yet he, being merciful, forgave their iniquity and did not destroy them. Yes, many times he held back his anger and did not stir up all his wrath.


## Psalms 78:39 (id: 919078039)

39He called to mind that they were made of flesh, a wind that passes away and does not return.


## Psalms 78:40 (id: 919078040)

40How often they rebelled against him in the wilderness and grieved him in the barren regions!


## Psalms 78:41 (id: 919078041)

41Again and again they challenged God and offended the Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 78:42 (id: 919078042)

42They did not think about his power, how he had rescued them from the enemy


## Psalms 78:43 (id: 919078043)

43when he performed his terrifying signs in Egypt and his wonders in the region of Zoan.


## Psalms 78:44 (id: 919078044)

44He turned the Egyptians’ rivers to blood so that they could not drink from their streams.


## Psalms 78:45 (id: 919078045)

45He sent swarms of flies that devoured them and frogs that overran their land.


## Psalms 78:46 (id: 919078046)

46He gave their crops to the grasshopper and their labor to the locust.


## Psalms 78:47 (id: 919078047)

47He destroyed their vines with hail and their sycamore trees with more hail.


## Psalms 78:48 (id: 919078048)

48He rained hail on their cattle and hurled lightning bolts at their livestock.


## Psalms 78:49 (id: 919078049)

49The fierceness of his anger lashed out against them. He sent wrath, fury, and trouble like agents who bring disaster.


## Psalms 78:50 (id: 919078050)

50He leveled a path for his anger; he did not spare them from death but gave them over to the plague.


## Psalms 78:51 (id: 919078051)

51He killed all the firstborn in Egypt, the firstborn of their strength in the tents of Ham.


## Psalms 78:52 (id: 919078052)

52He led his own people out like sheep and guided them through the wilderness like a flock.


## Psalms 78:53 (id: 919078053)

53He led them secure and unafraid, but the sea overwhelmed their enemies.


## Psalms 78:54 (id: 919078054)

54Then he brought them to the border of his holy land, to this mountain that his right hand acquired.


## Psalms 78:55 (id: 919078055)

55He drove out the nations from before them and assigned them their inheritance. He settled the tribes of Israel in their tents.


## Psalms 78:56 (id: 919078056)

56Yet they challenged and defied the Most High God and did not keep his solemn commands.


## Psalms 78:57 (id: 919078057)

57They were unfaithful and acted treacherously like their fathers; they were as undependable as a faulty bow.


## Psalms 78:58 (id: 919078058)

58For they made him angry with their high places and provoked him to jealous anger with their idols.


## Psalms 78:59 (id: 919078059)

59When God heard this, he was angry and completely rejected Israel.


## Psalms 78:60 (id: 919078060)

60He abandoned the sanctuary of Shiloh, the tent where he had lived among people.


## Psalms 78:61 (id: 919078061)

61He allowed his strength to be captured and gave his glory into the enemy’s hand.


## Psalms 78:62 (id: 919078062)

62He handed his people over to the sword, and he was angry with his heritage.


## Psalms 78:63 (id: 919078063)

63Fire devoured their young men, and their young women had no wedding songs.


## Psalms 78:64 (id: 919078064)

64Their priests fell by the sword, and their widows could not weep.


## Psalms 78:65 (id: 919078065)

65Then the Lord awakened as one from sleep, like a warrior who shouts because of wine.


## Psalms 78:66 (id: 919078066)

66He drove his adversaries back; he put them to everlasting shame.


## Psalms 78:67 (id: 919078067)

67He rejected the tent of Joseph, and he did not chose the tribe of Ephraim.


## Psalms 78:68 (id: 919078068)

68He chose the tribe of Judah and Mount Zion that he loved.


## Psalms 78:69 (id: 919078069)

69He built his sanctuary like the heavens, like the earth that he has established forever.


## Psalms 78:70 (id: 919078070)

70He chose David, his servant, and took him from the sheepfolds.


## Psalms 78:71 (id: 919078071)

71He took him from following the ewes with their young, and he brought him to be shepherd of Jacob, his people, and of Israel, his heritage.


## Psalms 78:72 (id: 919078072)

72David shepherded them with the integrity of his heart, and he guided them with the skill of his hands.


## Psalms 79:1 (id: 919079001)

1A psalm of Asaph. A Psalm of Asaph God, foreign nations have come into your inheritance; they have defiled your holy temple; they have turned Jerusalem into a heap of ruins.


## Psalms 79:2 (id: 919079002)

2They have given the dead bodies of your servants as food to the birds of the skies, the bodies of your faithful ones to the beasts of the earth.


## Psalms 79:3 (id: 919079003)

3They have shed their blood like water around Jerusalem, and there was none to bury them.


## Psalms 79:4 (id: 919079004)

4We have become a reproach for our neighbors, mocking and derision to those who are around us.


## Psalms 79:5 (id: 919079005)

5How long, Yahweh? Will you stay angry forever? How long will your jealous anger burn like fire?


## Psalms 79:6 (id: 919079006)

6Pour out your wrath on the nations that do not know you and on the kingdoms that do not call upon your name.


## Psalms 79:7 (id: 919079007)

7For they have devoured Jacob and destroyed his villages.


## Psalms 79:8 (id: 919079008)

8Do not hold the sins of our forefathers against us; may your merciful actions come to us, for we are very low.


## Psalms 79:9 (id: 919079009)

9Help us, God of our salvation, for the sake of the glory of your name; save us and forgive our sins for your name’s sake.


## Psalms 79:10 (id: 919079010)

10Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?” May the blood of your servants that was shed be avenged on the nations before our eyes.


## Psalms 79:11 (id: 919079011)

11May the groans of the prisoners come before you; with the greatness of your power keep the children of death alive.


## Psalms 79:12 (id: 919079012)

12Pay back into the laps of our neighboring countries seven times as much as the insults with which they have insulted you, Lord.


## Psalms 79:13 (id: 919079013)

13So we your people and sheep of your pasture will give you thanks forever. We will tell your praises to all generations.


## Psalms 80:1 (id: 919080001)

1For the chief musician, set to the Shoshannim Eduth style. A psalm of Asaph. Pay attention, Shepherd of Israel, you who lead Joseph like a flock; you who sit above the cherubim, shine on us!


## Psalms 80:2 (id: 919080002)

2In the sight of Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh, stir up your power; come and save us.


## Psalms 80:3 (id: 919080003)

3God, restore us; make your face shine on us, and we will be saved.


## Psalms 80:4 (id: 919080004)

4Yahweh God of hosts, how long will you be angry at your people when they pray?


## Psalms 80:5 (id: 919080005)

5You have fed them with the bread of tears and given them tears to drink in great quantities.


## Psalms 80:6 (id: 919080006)

6You make us something for our neighbors to argue over, and our enemies laugh about us among themselves.


## Psalms 80:7 (id: 919080007)

7God of hosts, restore us; make your face shine on us, and we will be saved.


## Psalms 80:8 (id: 919080008)

8You brought a vine out of Egypt; you drove out nations and transplanted it.


## Psalms 80:9 (id: 919080009)

9You cleared the land for it; it took root and filled the land.


## Psalms 80:10 (id: 919080010)

10The mountains were covered with its shade, the cedars of God by its branches.


## Psalms 80:11 (id: 919080011)

11It sent out its branches as far as the sea and its shoots to the Euphrates River.


## Psalms 80:12 (id: 919080012)

12Why have you broken down its walls so that all who pass by along the road pluck its fruit?


## Psalms 80:13 (id: 919080013)

13The boars out of the forest ruin it, and the beasts of the field feed on it.


## Psalms 80:14 (id: 919080014)

14Turn back, God of hosts; look down from heaven and take notice and take care of this vine.


## Psalms 80:15 (id: 919080015)

15This is the root that your right hand planted, the shoot that you made to grow.


## Psalms 80:16 (id: 919080016)

16It has been burned and cut down; they perish because of your rebuke.


## Psalms 80:17 (id: 919080017)

17May your hand be on the man of your right hand, on the son of man whom you made strong for yourself.


## Psalms 80:18 (id: 919080018)

18Then we will not turn away from you; revive us, and we will call on your name.


## Psalms 80:19 (id: 919080019)

19Yahweh God of hosts, restore us; make your face shine on us, and we will be saved.


## Psalms 81:1 (id: 919081001)

1For the chief musician; set to the Gittith style. A psalm of Asaph. Sing aloud to God our strength; shout out for joy to the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 81:2 (id: 919081002)

2Sing a song and play the tambourine, the pleasant lyre with the harp.


## Psalms 81:3 (id: 919081003)

3Blow the trumpet on the day of the new moon, on the day of the full moon, when our feast day begins.


## Psalms 81:4 (id: 919081004)

4For it is a statute for Israel, a decree given by the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 81:5 (id: 919081005)

5He issued it as a regulation in Joseph when he went against the land of Egypt, where I heard a voice that I did not recognize:


## Psalms 81:6 (id: 919081006)

6“I removed the burden from his shoulder; his hands were freed from holding the basket.


## Psalms 81:7 (id: 919081007)

7In your distress you called out, and I helped you; I answered you from a dark thundercloud. I tested you at the waters of Meribah. 


## Psalms 81:8 (id: 919081008)

8Listen, my people, for I will warn you, Israel, if you would only listen to me!


## Psalms 81:9 (id: 919081009)

9There must be no foreign god among you; you must not worship any foreign god.


## Psalms 81:10 (id: 919081010)

10I am Yahweh your God, who brought you out of the land of Egypt. Open your mouth wide, and I will fill it.


## Psalms 81:11 (id: 919081011)

11But my people did not listen to my words; Israel did not obey me.


## Psalms 81:12 (id: 919081012)

12So I gave them over to their own stubborn way so that they might do what seemed right to them.


## Psalms 81:13 (id: 919081013)

13Oh, that my people would listen to me; oh, that my people would walk in my paths.


## Psalms 81:14 (id: 919081014)

14Then I would quickly subdue their enemies and turn my hand against their oppressors.


## Psalms 81:15 (id: 919081015)

15May those who hate Yahweh cringe in fear before him! May they be humiliated forever.


## Psalms 81:16 (id: 919081016)

16I would feed Israel with the finest wheat; I would satisfy you with honey out of the rock.”


## Psalms 82:1 (id: 919082001)

1A psalm of Asaph. A Psalm of Asaph God stands in the divine assembly; in the midst of the gods he renders judgment.


## Psalms 82:2 (id: 919082002)

2How long will you judge unjustly and show favoritism to the wicked? Selah


## Psalms 82:3 (id: 919082003)

3Defend the poor and fatherless; maintain the rights of the afflicted and destitute.


## Psalms 82:4 (id: 919082004)

4Rescue the poor and needy; take them out of the hand of the wicked.


## Psalms 82:5 (id: 919082005)

5They neither know nor understand; they wander around in the darkness; all the foundations of the earth crumble.


## Psalms 82:6 (id: 919082006)

6I said, “You are gods, and all of you sons of the Most High.


## Psalms 82:7 (id: 919082007)

7Nevertheless you will die like men and fall like one of the princes.”


## Psalms 82:8 (id: 919082008)

8Arise, God, judge the earth, for you have an inheritance in all the nations.


## Psalms 83:1 (id: 919083001)

1A song. A psalm of Asaph. God, do not be silent! Do not ignore us and remain unmoved, God.


## Psalms 83:2 (id: 919083002)

2Look, your enemies are making a commotion, and those who hate you have raised their heads.


## Psalms 83:3 (id: 919083003)

3They conspire against your people and plan together against your protected ones.


## Psalms 83:4 (id: 919083004)

4They have said, “Come, and let us destroy them as a nation. Then the name of Israel will no longer be remembered.”


## Psalms 83:5 (id: 919083005)

5They schemed together with one strategy; they made an alliance against you—


## Psalms 83:6 (id: 919083006)

6the tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites, of Moab and the Hagrites,


## Psalms 83:7 (id: 919083007)

7Gebal, Ammon, Amalek; and also Philistia and the inhabitants of Tyre.


## Psalms 83:8 (id: 919083008)

8Assyria also has joined with them; they have become an arm for the descendants of Lot. 


## Psalms 83:9 (id: 919083009)

9Do to them as you did to Midian, as you did to Sisera and to Jabin at the Kishon River.


## Psalms 83:10 (id: 919083010)

10They perished at Endor and became like manure for the earth.


## Psalms 83:11 (id: 919083011)

11Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb, and all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna.


## Psalms 83:12 (id: 919083012)

12They said, “Let us take for ourselves the pastures of God.”


## Psalms 83:13 (id: 919083013)

13My God, make them like the whirling dust, like chaff before the wind,


## Psalms 83:14 (id: 919083014)

14like the fire that burns the forest, and like the flame that sets the mountains on fire.


## Psalms 83:15 (id: 919083015)

15Chase them with your strong wind, and terrify them with your windstorm.


## Psalms 83:16 (id: 919083016)

16Fill their faces with shame so that they might seek your name, Yahweh.


## Psalms 83:17 (id: 919083017)

17May they be put to shame and be terrified forever; may they perish in disgrace.


## Psalms 83:18 (id: 919083018)

18Then they will know that you alone, Yahweh, are honored as the Most High over all the earth.


## Psalms 84:1 (id: 919084001)

1For the chief musician; set to the Gittith style. A psalm of the sons of Korah. How lovely is the place where you live, Yahweh of hosts!


## Psalms 84:2 (id: 919084002)

2I long for the courts of Yahweh, my desire for it has made me exhausted. My heart and all of my being call out to the living God.


## Psalms 84:3 (id: 919084003)

3Even the sparrow has found her a house and the swallow a nest for herself where she may lay her young near your altars, Yahweh of hosts, my King, and my God.


## Psalms 84:4 (id: 919084004)

4Blessed are they who live in your house; they praise you continually. 


## Psalms 84:5 (id: 919084005)

5Blessed is the man whose strength is in you, in whose heart are the highways up to Zion.


## Psalms 84:6 (id: 919084006)

6Passing through the Valley of Tears, they find springs of water to drink. The early rains cover it with blessings.


## Psalms 84:7 (id: 919084007)

7They go from strength to strength; every one of them appears before God in Zion.


## Psalms 84:8 (id: 919084008)

8Yahweh God of hosts, hear my prayer; God of Jacob, listen to what I am saying! 


## Psalms 84:9 (id: 919084009)

9God, watch over our shield; show concern for your anointed.


## Psalms 84:10 (id: 919084010)

10For one day in your courts is better than a thousand elsewhere. I would rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God, than to live within the tents of the wicked.


## Psalms 84:11 (id: 919084011)

11For Yahweh God is our sun and shield; Yahweh will give grace and glory; he does not withhold any good thing from those who walk in integrity.


## Psalms 84:12 (id: 919084012)

12Yahweh of hosts, blessed is the man who trusts in you.


## Psalms 85:1 (id: 919085001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of the sons of Korah. Yahweh, you have showed favor to your land; you have restored the well\-being of Jacob.


## Psalms 85:2 (id: 919085002)

2You have forgiven the sin of your people; you have covered all their sin. Selah


## Psalms 85:3 (id: 919085003)

3You have withdrawn all your wrath; you have turned back from your hot anger.


## Psalms 85:4 (id: 919085004)

4Restore us, God of our salvation, and let go of your displeasure with us.


## Psalms 85:5 (id: 919085005)

5Will you be angry with us forever? Will you remain angry throughout future generations?


## Psalms 85:6 (id: 919085006)

6Will you not revive us again? Then your people will rejoice in you.


## Psalms 85:7 (id: 919085007)

7Show us your covenant faithfulness, Yahweh, grant us your salvation.


## Psalms 85:8 (id: 919085008)

8I will listen to what Yahweh God says, for he will make peace with his people, his faithful ones. Yet they must not turn again to foolish ways.


## Psalms 85:9 (id: 919085009)

9Surely his salvation is near to those who fear him; then glory will remain in our land.


## Psalms 85:10 (id: 919085010)

10Covenant faithfulness and trustworthiness have met together; righteousness and peace have kissed each other.


## Psalms 85:11 (id: 919085011)

11Trustworthiness springs up from the ground, and righteousness looks down from the sky.


## Psalms 85:12 (id: 919085012)

12Yes, Yahweh will give his good blessings, and our land will yield its crops.


## Psalms 85:13 (id: 919085013)

13Righteousness will go before him and make a way for his footsteps.


## Psalms 86:1 (id: 919086001)

1A prayer of David. A Prayer of David. Incline your ear and listen, Yahweh, and answer me, for I am poor and needy.


## Psalms 86:2 (id: 919086002)

2Protect me, for I am faithful; my God, save your servant who trusts in you.


## Psalms 86:3 (id: 919086003)

3Be merciful to me, Lord, for I cry out to you all day long.


## Psalms 86:4 (id: 919086004)

4Make your servant glad, for to you, Lord, I lift up my soul.


## Psalms 86:5 (id: 919086005)

5You, Lord, are good, and ready to forgive, and you show great mercy to all those who cry out to you.


## Psalms 86:6 (id: 919086006)

6Yahweh, listen to my prayer; hear the sound of my pleas.


## Psalms 86:7 (id: 919086007)

7In the day of my trouble I call on you, for you will answer me.


## Psalms 86:8 (id: 919086008)

8There is no one who compares to you among the gods, Lord. There are no deeds like your deeds.


## Psalms 86:9 (id: 919086009)

9All the nations that you have made will come and bow before you, Lord. They will honor your name.


## Psalms 86:10 (id: 919086010)

10For you are great and do wonderful things; you only are God.


## Psalms 86:11 (id: 919086011)

11Teach me your ways, Yahweh. Then I will walk in your truth. Unite my heart to reverence you.


## Psalms 86:12 (id: 919086012)

12Lord my God, I will praise you with my whole heart; I will glorify your name forever.


## Psalms 86:13 (id: 919086013)

13For great is your covenant faithfulness toward me; you have rescued my life from the depths of Sheol.


## Psalms 86:14 (id: 919086014)

14God, the arrogant have risen up against me. A gang of violent men seek my life. They have no regard for you.


## Psalms 86:15 (id: 919086015)

15But you, Lord, are a merciful and gracious God, slow to anger, and abundant in covenant faithfulness and trustworthiness.


## Psalms 86:16 (id: 919086016)

16Turn toward me and have mercy on me; give your strength to your servant; save the son of your servant woman.


## Psalms 86:17 (id: 919086017)

17Show me a sign of your favor. Then those who hate me will see it and be put to shame because you, Yahweh, have helped me and comforted me.


## Psalms 87:1 (id: 919087001)

1A psalm of the sons of Korah; a song. A Psalm of the sons of Korah A Song On the holy mount stands the city he founded;


## Psalms 87:2 (id: 919087002)

2Yahweh loves the gates of Zion more than all the tents of Jacob.


## Psalms 87:3 (id: 919087003)

3Glorious things are said of you, city of God. Selah


## Psalms 87:4 (id: 919087004)

4“I mention Rahab and Babylon to my followers. See, there are Philistia, and Tyre, along with Cush— and will say, ‘This one was born there.’”


## Psalms 87:5 (id: 919087005)

5Of Zion it will be said, “Each of these was born in her; and the Most High himself will establish her.”


## Psalms 87:6 (id: 919087006)

6Yahweh writes in the census book of the nations, “This one was born there.” 


## Psalms 87:7 (id: 919087007)

7So also the singers and the dancers say together, “All my fountains are in you.”


## Psalms 88:1 (id: 919088001)

1A song, a psalm of the sons of Korah; for the chief musician; set to the Mahalath Leannoth style. A maschil of Heman the Ezrahite. Yahweh, God of my salvation, I cry out day and night before you.


## Psalms 88:2 (id: 919088002)

2Let my prayer come before you; pay attention to my cry.


## Psalms 88:3 (id: 919088003)

3For I am filled with troubles, and my life has reached Sheol.


## Psalms 88:4 (id: 919088004)

4People treat me like those who go down into the pit; I am a man with no strength.


## Psalms 88:5 (id: 919088005)

5I am abandoned among the dead; I am like the dead who lie in the grave, about whom you care no more because they are cut off from your power.


## Psalms 88:6 (id: 919088006)

6You place me in the lowest part of the pit, in the dark and deep places.


## Psalms 88:7 (id: 919088007)

7Your wrath lies heavy on me, and all your waves crash over me. 


## Psalms 88:8 (id: 919088008)

8Because of you, my acquaintances avoid me. You have made me a shocking sight to them. I am hemmed in and I cannot escape.


## Psalms 88:9 (id: 919088009)

9My eyes grow weary from trouble; All day long I call out to you, Yahweh; I spread out my hands to you.


## Psalms 88:10 (id: 919088010)

10Will you do wonders for the dead? Will those who have died rise and praise you? 


## Psalms 88:11 (id: 919088011)

11Will your covenant faithfulness be proclaimed in the grave, your loyalty in the place of the dead?


## Psalms 88:12 (id: 919088012)

12Will your wonderful deeds be known in the darkness, or your righteousness in the place of forgetfulness?


## Psalms 88:13 (id: 919088013)

13But I cry to you, Yahweh; in the morning my prayer comes before you.


## Psalms 88:14 (id: 919088014)

14Yahweh, why do you reject me? Why do you hide your face from me?


## Psalms 88:15 (id: 919088015)

15I have always been afflicted and on the verge of death since my youth. I have suffered from your terrors; I am in despair.


## Psalms 88:16 (id: 919088016)

16Your angry actions have passed over me, and your terrifying deeds have annihilated me.


## Psalms 88:17 (id: 919088017)

17They surround me like water all the day long; they have all encircled me.


## Psalms 88:18 (id: 919088018)

18You have removed every friend and acquaintance from me. My only acquaintance is the darkness.


## Psalms 89:1 (id: 919089001)

1A maschil of Ethan the Ezrahite. I will sing of Yahweh’s acts of covenant faithfulness forever. I will proclaim your truthfulness to future generations.


## Psalms 89:2 (id: 919089002)

2For I have said, “Covenant faithfulness has been established forever; your truthfulness you have established in the heavens.”


## Psalms 89:3 (id: 919089003)

3“I have made a covenant with my chosen one, I have made an oath to David my servant.


## Psalms 89:4 (id: 919089004)

4I will establish your descendants forever, and I will establish your throne through all generations.” 


## Psalms 89:5 (id: 919089005)

5The heavens praise your wonders, Yahweh; your truthfulness is praised in the assembly of the holy ones.


## Psalms 89:6 (id: 919089006)

6For who in the skies can be compared to Yahweh? Who among the sons of the gods is like Yahweh?


## Psalms 89:7 (id: 919089007)

7He is a God who is greatly honored in the council of the holy ones and is awesome among all who surround him.


## Psalms 89:8 (id: 919089008)

8Yahweh God of hosts, who is strong like you, Yahweh? Your truthfulness surrounds you.


## Psalms 89:9 (id: 919089009)

9You rule the raging sea; when the waves surge, you calm them.


## Psalms 89:10 (id: 919089010)

10You crushed Rahab as one who is killed. You scattered your enemies with your strong arm.


## Psalms 89:11 (id: 919089011)

11The heavens belong to you, and the earth also. You made the world and all it contains.


## Psalms 89:12 (id: 919089012)

12You created the north and the south. Tabor and Hermon rejoice in your name.


## Psalms 89:13 (id: 919089013)

13You have a mighty arm and a strong hand, and your right hand is high.


## Psalms 89:14 (id: 919089014)

14Righteousness and justice are the foundation of your throne. Covenant faithfulness and trustworthiness come before you.


## Psalms 89:15 (id: 919089015)

15Blessed are the people who know the joyful sound! Yahweh, they walk in the light of your face.


## Psalms 89:16 (id: 919089016)

16They rejoice in your name all day long, and in your righteousness they exalt you.


## Psalms 89:17 (id: 919089017)

17You are their majestic strength, and by your favor our strength is made victorious.


## Psalms 89:18 (id: 919089018)

18For our shield belongs to Yahweh; our king belongs to the Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 89:19 (id: 919089019)

19Long ago you spoke in a vision to your faithful ones; I have raised up one chosen from among the people.


## Psalms 89:20 (id: 919089020)

20I have chosen David my servant; with my holy oil have I anointed him.


## Psalms 89:21 (id: 919089021)

21My hand will support him. Also my arm will be with him to strengthen him.


## Psalms 89:22 (id: 919089022)

22No enemy will deceive him; no son of wickedness will oppress him.


## Psalms 89:23 (id: 919089023)

23I will crush his enemies before him; I will kill those who hate him.


## Psalms 89:24 (id: 919089024)

24My truth and my covenant faithfulness will be with him; by my name he will win victories.


## Psalms 89:25 (id: 919089025)

25I will place his hand over the sea and his right hand over the rivers.


## Psalms 89:26 (id: 919089026)

26He will call out to me, ‘You are my Father, my God, and the rock of my salvation.’


## Psalms 89:27 (id: 919089027)

27I also will place him as my firstborn son, the most exalted of the kings of the earth.


## Psalms 89:28 (id: 919089028)

28I will extend my covenant faithfulness to him forever; and my covenant with him will be secure.


## Psalms 89:29 (id: 919089029)

29I will make his descendants endure forever and his throne as enduring as the skies above.


## Psalms 89:30 (id: 919089030)

30If his children forsake my law and do not walk in my regulations,


## Psalms 89:31 (id: 919089031)

31if they break my rules and do not keep my commands,


## Psalms 89:32 (id: 919089032)

32then will I punish their rebellion with a rod and their iniquity with blows.


## Psalms 89:33 (id: 919089033)

33But I will not remove my steadfast love from him or be unfaithful to my promise.


## Psalms 89:34 (id: 919089034)

34I will not break my covenant or change the words of my lips.


## Psalms 89:35 (id: 919089035)

35Once and for all I have sworn by my holiness— I will not lie to David:


## Psalms 89:36 (id: 919089036)

36his descendants will continue forever and his throne as long as the sun before me.


## Psalms 89:37 (id: 919089037)

37It will be established forever like the moon, the faithful witness in the sky.” 


## Psalms 89:38 (id: 919089038)

38But you have refused and rejected; you have been angry with your anointed king.


## Psalms 89:39 (id: 919089039)

39You have renounced the covenant of your servant. You have desecrated his crown on the ground.


## Psalms 89:40 (id: 919089040)

40You have broken down all his walls. You have ruined his strongholds.


## Psalms 89:41 (id: 919089041)

41All who pass by have robbed him. He has become an object of disgust to his neighbors.


## Psalms 89:42 (id: 919089042)

42You have raised the right hand of his enemies; you have made all his enemies rejoice.


## Psalms 89:43 (id: 919089043)

43You turn back the edge of his sword and have not made him stand when in battle.


## Psalms 89:44 (id: 919089044)

44You have brought his splendor to an end; you have brought down his throne to the ground.


## Psalms 89:45 (id: 919089045)

45You have shortened the days of his youth. You have covered him with shame. 


## Psalms 89:46 (id: 919089046)

46How long, Yahweh? Will you hide yourself, forever? How long will your anger burn like fire?


## Psalms 89:47 (id: 919089047)

47Oh, think about how short my time is, and for what uselessness you have created all the children of mankind!


## Psalms 89:48 (id: 919089048)

48Who can live and not see death, or rescue his own life from the hand of Sheol? 


## Psalms 89:49 (id: 919089049)

49Lord, where are your former acts of covenant faithfulness that you swore to David in your truthfulness?


## Psalms 89:50 (id: 919089050)

50Call to mind, Lord, the mocking directed against your servants and how I bear in my heart so many insults from the nations.


## Psalms 89:51 (id: 919089051)

51Your enemies hurl insults, Yahweh; they mock the footsteps of your anointed one.


## Psalms 89:52 (id: 919089052)

52Blessed be Yahweh forever. Amen and Amen.


## Psalms 90:1 (id: 919090001)

1A prayer of Moses the man of God. A Prayer of Moses a man of God Lord, you have been our refuge throughout all generations.


## Psalms 90:2 (id: 919090002)

2Before the mountains were formed, or you formed the earth and the world, from everlasting to everlasting, you are God.


## Psalms 90:3 (id: 919090003)

3You return man to dust, and you say, “Return, you descendants of mankind.”


## Psalms 90:4 (id: 919090004)

4For a thousand years in your sight are as yesterday when it is past, and as a watch in the night.


## Psalms 90:5 (id: 919090005)

5You sweep them away as with a flood and they sleep; in the morning they are like the grass that sprouts up.


## Psalms 90:6 (id: 919090006)

6In the morning it blooms and grows up; in the evening it withers and dries up.


## Psalms 90:7 (id: 919090007)

7Truly, we are consumed in your anger, and in your wrath we are terrified.


## Psalms 90:8 (id: 919090008)

8You have set our iniquities before you, our hidden sins in the light of your presence.


## Psalms 90:9 (id: 919090009)

9For our life passes away under your wrath; our years quickly pass like a sigh.


## Psalms 90:10 (id: 919090010)

10Our years are seventy, or even eighty if we are healthy; but even our best years are marked by trouble and sorrow. Yes, they pass quickly, and we fly away.


## Psalms 90:11 (id: 919090011)

11Who knows the intensity of your anger, and your wrath that is equal to the fear of you?


## Psalms 90:12 (id: 919090012)

12So teach us to consider our life so that we might live wisely.


## Psalms 90:13 (id: 919090013)

13Turn back, Yahweh! How long will it be? Have pity on your servants.


## Psalms 90:14 (id: 919090014)

14Satisfy us in the morning with your covenant faithfulness so that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.


## Psalms 90:15 (id: 919090015)

15Make us glad in proportion to the days you afflicted us and to the years we have experienced trouble.


## Psalms 90:16 (id: 919090016)

16Let your servants see your work, and let our children see your majesty.


## Psalms 90:17 (id: 919090017)

17May the favor of the Lord our God be ours; prosper the work of our hands; indeed, prosper the work of our hands.


## Psalms 91:1 (id: 919091001)

1He who lives in the shelter of the Most High will stay in the shadow of the Almighty.


## Psalms 91:2 (id: 919091002)

2I will say of Yahweh, “He is my refuge and my fortress, my God, in whom I trust.”


## Psalms 91:3 (id: 919091003)

3For he will rescue you from the snare of the hunter and from the deadly plague.


## Psalms 91:4 (id: 919091004)

4He will cover you with his wings, and under his wings you will find refuge. His trustworthiness is a shield and protection.


## Psalms 91:5 (id: 919091005)

5You will not be afraid of terror in the night, or of the arrow that flies by day,


## Psalms 91:6 (id: 919091006)

6or of the plague that roams around in the darkness, or of the disease that comes at noontime.


## Psalms 91:7 (id: 919091007)

7A thousand may fall at your side and ten thousand at your right hand, but it will not reach you.


## Psalms 91:8 (id: 919091008)

8You will only observe and see the punishment of the wicked.


## Psalms 91:9 (id: 919091009)

9For Yahweh is my refuge! Make the Most High your refuge also.


## Psalms 91:10 (id: 919091010)

10No evil will overtake you; no affliction will come near your home.


## Psalms 91:11 (id: 919091011)

11For he will direct his angels to protect you, to guard you in all your ways.


## Psalms 91:12 (id: 919091012)

12They will lift you up with their hand so that you will not hit your foot on a stone.


## Psalms 91:13 (id: 919091013)

13You will crush lions and adders under your feet; you will trample on young lions and serpents.


## Psalms 91:14 (id: 919091014)

14Because he is devoted to me, I will rescue him. I will protect him because he is loyal to me.


## Psalms 91:15 (id: 919091015)

15When he calls to me, I will answer him. I will be with him in trouble; I will give him victory and will honor him.


## Psalms 91:16 (id: 919091016)

16I will satisfy him with the length of his days, and show him my salvation.


## Psalms 92:1 (id: 919092001)

1A psalm, a song for the Sabbath day. It is a good thing to give thanks to Yahweh and to sing praises to your name, Most High,


## Psalms 92:2 (id: 919092002)

2to proclaim your covenant faithfulness in the morning and your truthfulness every night,


## Psalms 92:3 (id: 919092003)

3with a harp of ten strings and with the melody of the lyre.


## Psalms 92:4 (id: 919092004)

4For you, Yahweh, have made me glad through your deeds. I will sing for joy because of the deeds of your hands.


## Psalms 92:5 (id: 919092005)

5How great are your deeds, Yahweh! Your thoughts are very deep.


## Psalms 92:6 (id: 919092006)

6A brutish person does not know, nor does a fool understand this:


## Psalms 92:7 (id: 919092007)

7When the wicked sprout like the grass, and even when all the evildoers thrive, still they are doomed to eternal destruction.


## Psalms 92:8 (id: 919092008)

8But you, Yahweh, will reign forever.


## Psalms 92:9 (id: 919092009)

9Indeed, look at your enemies, Yahweh! Indeed, look at your enemies. They will perish! All those who do evil will be scattered.


## Psalms 92:10 (id: 919092010)

10You have lifted up my horn like the horn of the wild ox; I am anointed with fresh oil.


## Psalms 92:11 (id: 919092011)

11My eyes have seen the downfall of my enemies; my ears have heard of the doom of my evil foes.


## Psalms 92:12 (id: 919092012)

12The righteous will flourish like the palm tree; they will grow like a cedar in Lebanon.


## Psalms 92:13 (id: 919092013)

13They are planted in the house of Yahweh; they flourish in the courts of our God.


## Psalms 92:14 (id: 919092014)

14They bear fruit even when they are old; they stay fresh and green,


## Psalms 92:15 (id: 919092015)

15to proclaim that Yahweh is just. He is my rock, and there is no unrighteousness in him.


## Psalms 93:1 (id: 919093001)

1Yahweh reigns; he is robed in majesty; Yahweh has clothed and girded himself with strength. The world is firmly established; it cannot be moved.


## Psalms 93:2 (id: 919093002)

2Your throne is established from ancient times; you are from everlasting.


## Psalms 93:3 (id: 919093003)

3The oceans rise, Yahweh; they have lifted up their voice; the oceans’ waves crash and roar.


## Psalms 93:4 (id: 919093004)

4Above the crashing of many waves, the mighty breakers of the sea, Yahweh on high is mighty.


## Psalms 93:5 (id: 919093005)

5Your solemn commands are very trustworthy; holiness adorns your house, Yahweh, for the length of your days.


## Psalms 94:1 (id: 919094001)

1Yahweh, God who avenges, God who avenges, shine over us.


## Psalms 94:2 (id: 919094002)

2Rise up, judge of the earth, give to the proud what they deserve.


## Psalms 94:3 (id: 919094003)

3How long will the wicked, Yahweh, how long will the wicked rejoice?


## Psalms 94:4 (id: 919094004)

4They pour out their arrogant words; all those who do evil boast.


## Psalms 94:5 (id: 919094005)

5They crush your people, Yahweh; they afflict the nation that belongs to you.


## Psalms 94:6 (id: 919094006)

6They kill the widow and foreigner who lives in their country, and they murder the fatherless.


## Psalms 94:7 (id: 919094007)

7They say, “Yahweh will not see, the God of Jacob does not take notice of it.”


## Psalms 94:8 (id: 919094008)

8Understand, you stupid people! You fools, when will you ever learn?


## Psalms 94:9 (id: 919094009)

9He who made the ear, does he not hear? He who formed the eye, does he not see?


## Psalms 94:10 (id: 919094010)

10He who disciplines the nations, does he not correct? He is the one who gives knowledge to man.


## Psalms 94:11 (id: 919094011)

11Yahweh knows the thoughts of men, that they are vapor.


## Psalms 94:12 (id: 919094012)

12Blessed is the one whom you instruct, Yahweh, the one whom you teach from your law.


## Psalms 94:13 (id: 919094013)

13You give him rest in times of trouble until a pit is dug for the wicked.


## Psalms 94:14 (id: 919094014)

14For Yahweh will not forsake his people or abandon his inheritance.


## Psalms 94:15 (id: 919094015)

15For judgment will again be righteous; and all the upright in heart will follow it.


## Psalms 94:16 (id: 919094016)

16Who will rise up to defend me against the evildoers? Who will stand up for me against the wicked?


## Psalms 94:17 (id: 919094017)

17Unless Yahweh had been my help, I would soon be lying down in the place of silence.


## Psalms 94:18 (id: 919094018)

18When I said, “My foot is slipping,” Your covenant faithfulness, Yahweh, held me up.


## Psalms 94:19 (id: 919094019)

19When cares within me are many, your consolations make me happy.


## Psalms 94:20 (id: 919094020)

20Can a throne of destruction be allied with you, one who creates injustice by statute?


## Psalms 94:21 (id: 919094021)

21They conspire together to take the life of the righteous and they condemn the innocent to death.


## Psalms 94:22 (id: 919094022)

22But Yahweh has been my high tower, and my God has been the rock of my refuge.


## Psalms 94:23 (id: 919094023)

23He will bring on them their own iniquity and will cut them off in their own wickedness. Yahweh our God will cut them off.


## Psalms 95:1 (id: 919095001)

1Oh come, let us sing to Yahweh; let us sing joyfully to the rock of our salvation.


## Psalms 95:2 (id: 919095002)

2Let us enter his presence with thanksgiving; let us sing to him with psalms of praise.


## Psalms 95:3 (id: 919095003)

3For Yahweh is a great God and a great King superior to all gods.


## Psalms 95:4 (id: 919095004)

4In his hand are the depths of the earth; the heights of the mountains are his.


## Psalms 95:5 (id: 919095005)

5The sea is his, for he made it, and his hands formed the dry land.


## Psalms 95:6 (id: 919095006)

6Oh come, let us worship and bow down; let us kneel before Yahweh, our Creator:


## Psalms 95:7 (id: 919095007)

7For he is our God, and we are the people of his pasture and the sheep of his hand. Today—oh, that you would hear his voice!


## Psalms 95:8 (id: 919095008)

8“Do not harden your heart, as at Meribah, or as on the day of Massah in the wilderness,


## Psalms 95:9 (id: 919095009)

9where your forefathers tested me and tried me, though they had seen my deeds.


## Psalms 95:10 (id: 919095010)

10For forty years I was angry with that generation and said, ‘This is a people whose hearts wander astray; they have not known my ways.’


## Psalms 95:11 (id: 919095011)

11Therefore I vowed in my anger that they would never enter into my resting place.”


## Psalms 96:1 (id: 919096001)

1Oh, sing to Yahweh a new song; sing to Yahweh, all the earth.


## Psalms 96:2 (id: 919096002)

2Sing to Yahweh, bless his name; announce his salvation day after day.


## Psalms 96:3 (id: 919096003)

3Declare his glory among the nations, his marvelous deeds among all the nations.


## Psalms 96:4 (id: 919096004)

4For Yahweh is great and is to be praised greatly. He is to be feared above all other gods.


## Psalms 96:5 (id: 919096005)

5For all the gods of the nations are idols, but it is Yahweh who made the heavens.


## Psalms 96:6 (id: 919096006)

6Splendor and majesty are in his presence. Strength and beauty are in his sanctuary.


## Psalms 96:7 (id: 919096007)

7Ascribe to Yahweh, you clans of peoples, ascribe praise to Yahweh for his glory and strength.


## Psalms 96:8 (id: 919096008)

8Give to Yahweh the glory that his name deserves. Bring an offering and come into his courts.


## Psalms 96:9 (id: 919096009)

9Bow down to Yahweh in the splendor of holiness; tremble before him, all the earth.


## Psalms 96:10 (id: 919096010)

10Say among the nations, “Yahweh reigns.” The world also is established; it cannot be shaken. He judges the peoples fairly.


## Psalms 96:11 (id: 919096011)

11Let the heavens be glad, and let the earth rejoice; let the sea roar and that which fills it shout with joy.


## Psalms 96:12 (id: 919096012)

12Let the fields rejoice and all that is in them. Then let all the trees in the forest shout for joy


## Psalms 96:13 (id: 919096013)

13before Yahweh, for he is coming. He is coming to judge the earth. He will judge the world with righteousness and the peoples with his faithfulness.


## Psalms 97:1 (id: 919097001)

1Yahweh reigns; let the earth rejoice; let the many coastlands be glad.


## Psalms 97:2 (id: 919097002)

2Clouds and darkness surround him. Righteousness and justice are the foundation of his throne.


## Psalms 97:3 (id: 919097003)

3Fire goes before him and consumes his adversaries on every side.


## Psalms 97:4 (id: 919097004)

4His lightning lights up the world; the earth sees and trembles.


## Psalms 97:5 (id: 919097005)

5The mountains melt like wax before Yahweh, the Lord of the whole earth.


## Psalms 97:6 (id: 919097006)

6The skies declare his justice, and all the nations see his glory.


## Psalms 97:7 (id: 919097007)

7All those who worship carved figures will be shamed, those who boast in worthless idols— bow down to him, all you gods!


## Psalms 97:8 (id: 919097008)

8Zion heard and was glad, and the towns of Judah rejoiced because of your righteous decrees, Yahweh.


## Psalms 97:9 (id: 919097009)

9For you, Yahweh, are most high above all the earth. You are exalted far above all gods.


## Psalms 97:10 (id: 919097010)

10You who love Yahweh, hate evil! He protects the lives of his faithful ones, and he takes them out of the hand of the wicked.


## Psalms 97:11 (id: 919097011)

11Light is sown for the righteous and gladness for those with honest hearts.


## Psalms 97:12 (id: 919097012)

12Be glad in Yahweh, you righteous; and give thanks when you remember his holiness.


## Psalms 98:1 (id: 919098001)

1A psalm. Oh, sing to Yahweh a new song, for he has done marvelous things; his right hand and his holy arm have given him victory.


## Psalms 98:2 (id: 919098002)

2Yahweh has made known his salvation; he has openly showed his justice to all the nations.


## Psalms 98:3 (id: 919098003)

3He calls to mind his covenant loyalty and faithfulness for the house of Israel; all the ends of the earth will see the victory of our God.


## Psalms 98:4 (id: 919098004)

## Psalms 98:5 (id: 919098005)

5Sing praises to Yahweh with the harp, with the harp and melodious song.


## Psalms 98:6 (id: 919098006)

## Psalms 98:7 (id: 919098007)

## Psalms 98:8 (id: 919098008)

8Let the rivers clap their hands, and let the mountains shout for joy.


## Psalms 98:9 (id: 919098009)

9Yahweh is coming to judge the earth; he will judge the world with righteousness and the nations with fairness.

## Psalms 99:2 (id: 919099002)

2Yahweh is great in Zion; he is exalted above all the nations.


## Psalms 99:3 (id: 919099003)

3Let them praise your great and awesome name; he is holy.


## Psalms 99:4 (id: 919099004)

4The king is strong, and he loves justice. You have established fairness; you have done righteousness and justice in Jacob.


## Psalms 99:5 (id: 919099005)

## Psalms 99:6 (id: 919099006)

6Moses and Aaron were among his priests, and Samuel was among those who called on his name. They called to Yahweh, and he answered them.


## Psalms 99:7 (id: 919099007)

7He spoke to them from the pillar of cloud. They kept his solemn commands and the statutes that he gave them.


## Psalms 99:8 (id: 919099008)

## Psalms 99:9 (id: 919099009)

## Psalms 100:1 (id: 919100001)

1A psalm of thanksgiving. Shout joyfully to Yahweh, all the earth.


## Psalms 100:2 (id: 919100002)

2Serve Yahweh with gladness; come before his presence with joyful singing.


## Psalms 100:3 (id: 919100003)

## Psalms 100:4 (id: 919100004)
