## Psalms 100:5 (id: 919100005)

5For Yahweh is good; his covenant faithfulness endures forever and his truthfulness through all generations.


## Psalms 101:1 (id: 919101001)

1A psalm of David. A Psalm of David I will sing of covenant faithfulness and justice; to you, Yahweh, I will sing praises.


## Psalms 101:2 (id: 919101002)

2I will walk in the way of integrity. Oh, when will you come to me? I will walk with integrity within my house.


## Psalms 101:3 (id: 919101003)

3I will not put wrongdoing before my eyes; I hate worthless evil; it will not cling to me.


## Psalms 101:4 (id: 919101004)

4Perverse people will leave me; I am not loyal to evil.


## Psalms 101:5 (id: 919101005)

5I will destroy whoever secretly slanders his neighbor. I will not tolerate anyone who has a proud demeanor and an arrogant attitude.


## Psalms 101:6 (id: 919101006)

6I will look to the faithful of the land to sit at my side. Those who walk in the way of integrity may serve me.


## Psalms 101:7 (id: 919101007)

7Deceitful people will not remain within my house; liars will not be welcome before my eyes.


## Psalms 101:8 (id: 919101008)

8Morning by morning I will destroy all the wicked from the land; I will remove all evildoers from the city of Yahweh.


## Psalms 102:1 (id: 919102001)

1A prayer of the afflicted when he is faint and pours out his lament before Yahweh. Hear my prayer, Yahweh; let my cry come near to you.


## Psalms 102:2 (id: 919102002)

2Do not hide your face from me in my time of trouble. Listen to me. When I call out to you, answer me quickly.


## Psalms 102:3 (id: 919102003)

3For my days pass away like smoke, and my bones burn like fire.


## Psalms 102:4 (id: 919102004)

4My heart is crushed, and I am like grass that has withered. I forget to eat any food.


## Psalms 102:5 (id: 919102005)

5With my continual groaning, I have become very thin.


## Psalms 102:6 (id: 919102006)

6I am like a pelican of the wilderness; I have become like an owl in the ruins.


## Psalms 102:7 (id: 919102007)

7I lie awake like a solitary bird, alone on the housetop.


## Psalms 102:8 (id: 919102008)

8My enemies taunt me all day long; those who mock me use my name in curses.


## Psalms 102:9 (id: 919102009)

9I eat ashes like bread and mix my drink with tears.


## Psalms 102:10 (id: 919102010)

10Because of your raging anger, you have lifted me up to throw me down.


## Psalms 102:11 (id: 919102011)

11My days are like a shadow that fades, and I have withered like grass.


## Psalms 102:12 (id: 919102012)

12But you, Yahweh, live forever, and your fame is for all generations.


## Psalms 102:13 (id: 919102013)

13You will rise up and have mercy on Zion. Now is the time to have mercy upon her; the appointed time has come.


## Psalms 102:14 (id: 919102014)

14For your servants hold her stones dear and feel compassion for the dust of her ruins.


## Psalms 102:15 (id: 919102015)

15The nations will respect your name, Yahweh, and all the kings of the earth will honor your glory.


## Psalms 102:16 (id: 919102016)

16Yahweh will rebuild Zion and will appear in his glory.


## Psalms 102:17 (id: 919102017)

17At that time, he will respond to the prayer of the destitute; he will not reject their prayer.


## Psalms 102:18 (id: 919102018)

18This will be written for future generations, and a people not yet born will praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 102:19 (id: 919102019)

19For he has looked down from the holy heights; from heaven Yahweh has viewed the earth,


## Psalms 102:20 (id: 919102020)

20to hear the groaning of the prisoners, to release those who were condemned to death.


## Psalms 102:21 (id: 919102021)

21Then men will proclaim the name of Yahweh in Zion and his praise in Jerusalem


## Psalms 102:22 (id: 919102022)

22when the peoples and kingdoms gather together to serve Yahweh.


## Psalms 102:23 (id: 919102023)

23He has taken away my strength in the middle of life. He has shortened my days.


## Psalms 102:24 (id: 919102024)

24I said, “My God, do not take me away in the middle of life; you are here throughout all generations.


## Psalms 102:25 (id: 919102025)

25In ancient times you set the earth in place; the heavens are the work of your hands.


## Psalms 102:26 (id: 919102026)

26They will perish, but you will remain; they will all grow old like a garment; like clothing, you will remove them, and they will disappear.


## Psalms 102:27 (id: 919102027)

27But you are the same, and your years will have no end.


## Psalms 102:28 (id: 919102028)

28The children of your servants will live on, and their descendants will live in your presence.”


## Psalms 103:1 (id: 919103001)

1A psalm of David. Of David Bless Yahweh, my inner being! and all that is within me, bless his holy name.


## Psalms 103:2 (id: 919103002)

2Bless Yahweh, my soul! and do not forget all of his rewards.


## Psalms 103:3 (id: 919103003)

3He pardons all your sins; he heals all your diseases.


## Psalms 103:4 (id: 919103004)

4He redeems your life from destruction; he crowns you with steadfastness and mercy.


## Psalms 103:5 (id: 919103005)

5He satisfies you with good things; your youth is renewed like the eagle.


## Psalms 103:6 (id: 919103006)

6Yahweh does what is right and what is just for all the oppressed.


## Psalms 103:7 (id: 919103007)

7He made known his ways to Moses, his deeds to the children of Israel.


## Psalms 103:8 (id: 919103008)

8Yahweh is gracious and merciful, slow to anger, and abounding in steadfast love.


## Psalms 103:9 (id: 919103009)

9He will not always discipline, and he will not keep his anger forever.


## Psalms 103:10 (id: 919103010)

10He does not deal with us according to our sins, and he does not treat us according to our iniquities.


## Psalms 103:11 (id: 919103011)

11For as the skies are high above the earth, so great is his steadfast love toward those who fear him.


## Psalms 103:12 (id: 919103012)

12As far as the east is from the west, this is how far he has removed our transgressions from us.


## Psalms 103:13 (id: 919103013)

13As a father has compassion on his children, so Yahweh has compassion on those who fear him.


## Psalms 103:14 (id: 919103014)

14For he knows our form; remembering that we are dust.


## Psalms 103:15 (id: 919103015)

15As for man, his days are like grass; like the flower of the field he flourishes so.


## Psalms 103:16 (id: 919103016)

16For the wind blows over it, and it is no more, and its place does not acknowledge it again.


## Psalms 103:17 (id: 919103017)

17But the covenant faithfulness of Yahweh is from everlasting to everlasting on those who honor him, and His righteousness is to their children's children.


## Psalms 103:18 (id: 919103018)

18To the ones who keep his covenant, and to the ones who remember his precepts in order to do them.


## Psalms 103:19 (id: 919103019)

19Yahweh has established his throne in the heavens, and his kingdom rules over all.


## Psalms 103:20 (id: 919103020)

20Bless Yahweh, you his angels, you mighty warriors who do his word, obeying the voice of his word.


## Psalms 103:21 (id: 919103021)

21Bless Yahweh, all his hosts, his ministers who do his pleasure.


## Psalms 103:22 (id: 919103022)

22Bless Yahweh, all his works, in all the places where he reigns. Bless Yahweh, my inner being!


## Psalms 104:1 (id: 919104001)

1I give praise to Yahweh with all my life, Yahweh my God, you are very magnificent; you are clothed with splendor and majesty.


## Psalms 104:2 (id: 919104002)

2You cover yourself with light as with a garment; you spread out the heavens like a tent curtain.


## Psalms 104:3 (id: 919104003)

3You lay the beams of your chambers on the clouds; you make the clouds your chariot; you walk on the wings of the wind.


## Psalms 104:4 (id: 919104004)

4He makes the winds his messengers, flames of fire his servants.


## Psalms 104:5 (id: 919104005)

5He laid the foundations of the earth, and it will never be moved.


## Psalms 104:6 (id: 919104006)

6You covered the earth with water like a garment; the water covered the mountains.


## Psalms 104:7 (id: 919104007)

7Your rebuke made the waters recede; at the sound of your thunderous voice they fled.


## Psalms 104:8 (id: 919104008)

8The mountains rose, and the valleys spread out into the places that you had appointed for them.


## Psalms 104:9 (id: 919104009)

9You have set a boundary for them that they will not cross; they will not cover the earth again.


## Psalms 104:10 (id: 919104010)

10He made springs flow into the valleys; the streams flow between the mountains.


## Psalms 104:11 (id: 919104011)

11They supply water for all the animals of the field; the wild donkeys quench their thirst.


## Psalms 104:12 (id: 919104012)

12By the heavens the birds build their nests; they sing among the branches.


## Psalms 104:13 (id: 919104013)

13He waters the mountains from his water chambers in the sky. The earth is filled with the fruit of his labor.


## Psalms 104:14 (id: 919104014)

14He makes the grass grow for the cattle and plants for man to cultivate so that man may produce food from the earth.


## Psalms 104:15 (id: 919104015)

15He makes wine to make man happy, oil to make his face shine, and food to sustain his life.


## Psalms 104:16 (id: 919104016)

16The trees of Yahweh get plenty of rain; the cedars of Lebanon which he planted.


## Psalms 104:17 (id: 919104017)

17There the birds make their nests. The stork makes the cypress tree her home.


## Psalms 104:18 (id: 919104018)

18The wild goats live on the high mountains; the mountain heights are a refuge for the hyraxes.


## Psalms 104:19 (id: 919104019)

19He appointed the moon to mark the seasons; the sun knows its time for setting.


## Psalms 104:20 (id: 919104020)

20You make the darkness of the night when all the beasts of the forest come out.


## Psalms 104:21 (id: 919104021)

21The young lions roar for their prey and seek their food from God.


## Psalms 104:22 (id: 919104022)

22When the sun rises, they retreat and sleep in their dens.


## Psalms 104:23 (id: 919104023)

23Meanwhile, people go out to their work and labor away until the evening.


## Psalms 104:24 (id: 919104024)

24Yahweh, how many and varied are your works! With wisdom you made them all; the earth overflows with your works.


## Psalms 104:25 (id: 919104025)

25Over there is the sea, deep and wide, teeming with innumerable creatures, both small and great.


## Psalms 104:26 (id: 919104026)

26The ships travel there, and Leviathan is also there, which you formed to play in the sea.


## Psalms 104:27 (id: 919104027)

27All these look to you to give them their food on time.


## Psalms 104:28 (id: 919104028)

28When you give to them, they gather; when you open your hand, they are satisfied.


## Psalms 104:29 (id: 919104029)

29When you hide your face, they are troubled; if you take away their breath, they die and return to dust.


## Psalms 104:30 (id: 919104030)

30When you send out your Spirit, they are created, and you renew the countryside.


## Psalms 104:31 (id: 919104031)

31May the glory of Yahweh last forever; may Yahweh enjoy his creation.


## Psalms 104:32 (id: 919104032)

32He looks down on the earth, and it shakes; he touches the mountains, and they smoke.


## Psalms 104:33 (id: 919104033)

33I will sing to Yahweh all my life; I will sing praise to my God as long as I live.


## Psalms 104:34 (id: 919104034)

34May my thoughts be sweet to him; I will rejoice in Yahweh.


## Psalms 104:35 (id: 919104035)

35May sinners vanish from the earth, and let the wicked be no more. I give praise to Yahweh with all my life. Praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 105:1 (id: 919105001)

1Give thanks to Yahweh, call on his name; make known his deeds among the nations.


## Psalms 105:2 (id: 919105002)

2Sing to him, sing praises to him; speak of all his marvelous deeds.


## Psalms 105:3 (id: 919105003)

3Boast in his holy name; let the heart of those who seek Yahweh rejoice.


## Psalms 105:4 (id: 919105004)

4Seek Yahweh and his strength; seek his presence continually.


## Psalms 105:5 (id: 919105005)

5Recall the marvelous things he has done, his miracles and the decrees from his mouth,


## Psalms 105:6 (id: 919105006)

6you descendants of Abraham his servant, you people of Jacob, his chosen ones.


## Psalms 105:7 (id: 919105007)

7He is Yahweh, our God. His decrees are on all the earth.


## Psalms 105:8 (id: 919105008)

8He keeps in mind his covenant forever, the word that he commanded for a thousand generations.


## Psalms 105:9 (id: 919105009)

9He calls to mind the covenant that he made with Abraham and his oath to Isaac.


## Psalms 105:10 (id: 919105010)

10This is what he confirmed to Jacob as a statute and to Israel as an everlasting covenant.


## Psalms 105:11 (id: 919105011)

11He said, “I will give you the land of Canaan as your share of your inheritance.”


## Psalms 105:12 (id: 919105012)

12He said this when they were only few in number, so very few, and were strangers in the land.


## Psalms 105:13 (id: 919105013)

13They went from nation to nation and from one kingdom to another.


## Psalms 105:14 (id: 919105014)

14He did not allow anyone to oppress them; he rebuked kings for their sakes.


## Psalms 105:15 (id: 919105015)

15He said, “Do not touch my anointed ones, and do not harm my prophets.”


## Psalms 105:16 (id: 919105016)

16He called for a famine on the land; he cut off the whole supply of bread.


## Psalms 105:17 (id: 919105017)

17He sent a man ahead of them; Joseph was sold as a servant.


## Psalms 105:18 (id: 919105018)

18His feet were bound by shackles; on his neck was put an iron collar,


## Psalms 105:19 (id: 919105019)

19until what he had said came to pass. The word of Yahweh tested him.


## Psalms 105:20 (id: 919105020)

20The king sent servants to release him; the ruler of the people set him free.


## Psalms 105:21 (id: 919105021)

21He put him in charge of his house as ruler of all his possessions


## Psalms 105:22 (id: 919105022)

22to instruct his princes as he wished and to teach his elders wisdom.


## Psalms 105:23 (id: 919105023)

23Then Israel came into Egypt, and Jacob lived for a time in the land of Ham.


## Psalms 105:24 (id: 919105024)

24Yahweh made his people fruitful, and made them stronger greatly than their enemies.


## Psalms 105:25 (id: 919105025)

25He caused their enemies to hate his people, to mistreat his servants.


## Psalms 105:26 (id: 919105026)

26He sent Moses, his servant, and Aaron, whom he had chosen.


## Psalms 105:27 (id: 919105027)

27They performed his signs among the Egyptians, his wonders in the land of Ham.


## Psalms 105:28 (id: 919105028)

28He sent darkness and made that land dark, but its people did not obey his commands.


## Psalms 105:29 (id: 919105029)

29He turned their water into blood and killed their fish.


## Psalms 105:30 (id: 919105030)

30Their land swarmed with frogs, even in the rooms of their rulers.


## Psalms 105:31 (id: 919105031)

31He spoke, and swarms of flies and gnats came throughout their country.


## Psalms 105:32 (id: 919105032)

32He turned their rain into hail, with fire flaming on their land.


## Psalms 105:33 (id: 919105033)

33He destroyed their vines and fig trees; he broke the trees of their country.


## Psalms 105:34 (id: 919105034)

34He spoke, and the locusts came, young locusts, without number.


## Psalms 105:35 (id: 919105035)

35The locusts ate up all of the vegetation in their land; They ate up all the crops of the ground.


## Psalms 105:36 (id: 919105036)

36He killed every firstborn in their land, the firstfruits of all their strength.


## Psalms 105:37 (id: 919105037)

37He brought the Israelites out with silver and gold; none of his tribes stumbled on the way.


## Psalms 105:38 (id: 919105038)

38Egypt was glad when they went away, for the fear of them had fallen upon them.


## Psalms 105:39 (id: 919105039)

39He spread a cloud for a covering and made a fire to light up the night.


## Psalms 105:40 (id: 919105040)

40The Israelites asked for food, and he brought quail and satisfied them with bread from heaven.


## Psalms 105:41 (id: 919105041)

41He split the rock, and waters gushed from it; they flowed in the wilderness like a river.


## Psalms 105:42 (id: 919105042)

42For he called to mind his holy promise that he made to Abraham his servant.


## Psalms 105:43 (id: 919105043)

43He led his people out with joy, his chosen with shouts of triumph.


## Psalms 105:44 (id: 919105044)

44He gave them the lands of the nations; they took possession of the wealth of the peoples


## Psalms 105:45 (id: 919105045)

45so that they might keep his statutes and obey his laws. Praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 106:1 (id: 919106001)

1Praise Yahweh. Give thanks to Yahweh, for he is good, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.


## Psalms 106:2 (id: 919106002)

2Who can recount the mighty acts of Yahweh or proclaim in full all his praiseworthy deeds?


## Psalms 106:3 (id: 919106003)

3Blessed are those who do what is right, and whose deeds are always just.


## Psalms 106:4 (id: 919106004)

4Call me to mind, Yahweh, when you show favor to your people; help me when you save them.


## Psalms 106:5 (id: 919106005)

5Then I will see the prosperity of your chosen, rejoice in the gladness of your nation, and glory with your inheritance.


## Psalms 106:6 (id: 919106006)

6We have sinned like our ancestors; we have done wrong, and we have done evil.


## Psalms 106:7 (id: 919106007)

7Our fathers did not appreciate your marvelous deeds in Egypt; they ignored your many acts of covenant faithfulness; they were rebellious at the sea, the Sea of Reeds.


## Psalms 106:8 (id: 919106008)

8Nevertheless, he saved them for his name’s sake so that he might reveal his power.


## Psalms 106:9 (id: 919106009)

9He rebuked the Sea of Reeds, and it dried up. Then he led them through the depths, as through a wilderness.


## Psalms 106:10 (id: 919106010)

10He saved them from the hand of those who hated them, and he rescued them from the hand of the enemy.


## Psalms 106:11 (id: 919106011)

11But the waters covered their adversaries; not one of them survived.


## Psalms 106:12 (id: 919106012)

12Then they believed his words, and they sang his praise.


## Psalms 106:13 (id: 919106013)

13But they quickly forgot what he had done; they did not wait for his instructions.


## Psalms 106:14 (id: 919106014)

14They had insatiable cravings in the wilderness, and they challenged God in the desert.


## Psalms 106:15 (id: 919106015)

15So he gave them what they requested, but he sent a horrible disease upon them.


## Psalms 106:16 (id: 919106016)

16In the camp they became jealous of Moses and Aaron, the holy priest of Yahweh.


## Psalms 106:17 (id: 919106017)

17The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan and covered the followers of Abiram.


## Psalms 106:18 (id: 919106018)

18Fire broke out among them; the fire consumed the wicked.


## Psalms 106:19 (id: 919106019)

19They made a calf at Horeb and worshiped a cast metal figure.


## Psalms 106:20 (id: 919106020)

20They traded the glory of God for the image of a bull that eats grass.


## Psalms 106:21 (id: 919106021)

21They forgot God their Savior, who had done great deeds in Egypt.


## Psalms 106:22 (id: 919106022)

22He had done wonderful things in the land of Ham and mighty acts at the Sea of Reeds.


## Psalms 106:23 (id: 919106023)

23So he said he would destroy them— had not Moses, his chosen one, stood in the breach before him, to turn away his anger from destroying them.


## Psalms 106:24 (id: 919106024)

24Then they despised the fruitful land; they did not believe his promise,


## Psalms 106:25 (id: 919106025)

25but grumbled in their tents, and did not obey Yahweh.


## Psalms 106:26 (id: 919106026)

26Therefore he raised his hand and swore to them that he would let them die in the desert,


## Psalms 106:27 (id: 919106027)

27scatter their descendants among the nations, and scatter them in foreign lands.


## Psalms 106:28 (id: 919106028)

28They worshiped the Baal of Peor and ate the sacrifices offered to the dead.


## Psalms 106:29 (id: 919106029)

29They provoked him to anger with their actions, and a plague broke out among them.


## Psalms 106:30 (id: 919106030)

30Then Phinehas rose to intervene, and the plague subsided.


## Psalms 106:31 (id: 919106031)

31It was counted to him as a righteous deed to all generations forever.


## Psalms 106:32 (id: 919106032)

32They also angered Yahweh at the waters of Meribah, and Moses suffered because of them.


## Psalms 106:33 (id: 919106033)

33They made Moses bitter, and he spoke rashly.


## Psalms 106:34 (id: 919106034)

34They did not destroy the nations as Yahweh had commanded them,


## Psalms 106:35 (id: 919106035)

35but they mingled with the nations and learned their ways


## Psalms 106:36 (id: 919106036)

36and worshiped their idols, which became a snare to them.


## Psalms 106:37 (id: 919106037)

37They sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons.


## Psalms 106:38 (id: 919106038)

38They shed innocent blood, the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan, desecrating the land with blood.


## Psalms 106:39 (id: 919106039)

39They were defiled by their deeds; in their actions they were like prostitutes.


## Psalms 106:40 (id: 919106040)

40So Yahweh was angry with his people, and he despised his own people.


## Psalms 106:41 (id: 919106041)

41He gave them into the hand of the nations, and those who hated them ruled over them.


## Psalms 106:42 (id: 919106042)

42Their enemies oppressed them, and they were brought into subjection to their authority.


## Psalms 106:43 (id: 919106043)

43Many times he came to help them, but they kept rebelling and were brought low by their own sin.


## Psalms 106:44 (id: 919106044)

44Nevertheless, he paid attention to their distress when he heard their cry for help.


## Psalms 106:45 (id: 919106045)

45He called to mind his covenant with them and relented because of his steadfast love.


## Psalms 106:46 (id: 919106046)

46He caused all their conquerers to have pity on them.


## Psalms 106:47 (id: 919106047)

47Save us, Yahweh, our God. Gather us from among the nations so that we may give thanks to your holy name and glory in your praises.


## Psalms 106:48 (id: 919106048)

48May Yahweh, the God of Israel, be praised from everlasting to everlasting. All the people said, “Amen.” Praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 107:1 (id: 919107001)

1Give thanks to Yahweh, for he is good, and his covenant faithfulness endures forever.


## Psalms 107:2 (id: 919107002)

2Let the redeemed of Yahweh speak out, those he has rescued from the hand of the enemy.


## Psalms 107:3 (id: 919107003)

3He has gathered them out of foreign lands, from the east and from the west, from the north and from the south.


## Psalms 107:4 (id: 919107004)

4They wandered in the wilderness on a desert road and found no city in which to live.


## Psalms 107:5 (id: 919107005)

5Because they were hungry and thirsty, they fainted from exhaustion.


## Psalms 107:6 (id: 919107006)

6Then they called out to Yahweh in their trouble, and he rescued them out of their distress.


## Psalms 107:7 (id: 919107007)

7He led them by a direct path so that they would go to a city to live in.


## Psalms 107:8 (id: 919107008)

8Oh that people would praise Yahweh for his covenant faithfulness and for the amazing things he has done for humanity!


## Psalms 107:9 (id: 919107009)

9For he satisfies the longings of those who are thirsty, and the desires of those who are hungry he fills up with good things.


## Psalms 107:10 (id: 919107010)

10Some sat in darkness and in gloom, prisoners in affliction and chains.


## Psalms 107:11 (id: 919107011)

11This was because they had rebelled against God’s word and rejected the instruction of the Most High.


## Psalms 107:12 (id: 919107012)

12He humbled their hearts through hardship; they stumbled and there was no one to help them up.


## Psalms 107:13 (id: 919107013)

13Then they called out to Yahweh in their trouble, and he brought them out of their distress.


## Psalms 107:14 (id: 919107014)

14He brought them out of darkness and gloom and broke their bonds.


## Psalms 107:15 (id: 919107015)

15Oh that people would praise Yahweh for his covenant faithfulness and for the amazing things he has done for humanity!


## Psalms 107:16 (id: 919107016)

16For he has broken the gates of bronze and cut through the bars of iron.


## Psalms 107:17 (id: 919107017)

17They were foolish in their rebellious ways and afflicted because of their sins.


## Psalms 107:18 (id: 919107018)

18They lost their desire to eat any food, and they came close to the gates of death.


## Psalms 107:19 (id: 919107019)

19Then they called out to Yahweh in their trouble, and he brought them out of their distress.


## Psalms 107:20 (id: 919107020)

20He sent his word and healed them, and he rescued them from their destruction.


## Psalms 107:21 (id: 919107021)

21Oh that people would praise Yahweh for his covenant faithfulness and for the amazing things he has done for humanity!


## Psalms 107:22 (id: 919107022)

22Let them offer the sacrifices of thanksgiving and proclaim his deeds in singing.


## Psalms 107:23 (id: 919107023)

23Some travel on the sea in ships and do business overseas.


## Psalms 107:24 (id: 919107024)

24These saw the deeds of Yahweh and his wonders on the seas.


## Psalms 107:25 (id: 919107025)

25For he commanded and aroused the windstorm that stirs up the seas.


## Psalms 107:26 (id: 919107026)

26They reached up to the sky; they went down to the depths. Their lives melted away in distress.


## Psalms 107:27 (id: 919107027)

27They swayed and staggered like drunkards and were at their wits’ end.


## Psalms 107:28 (id: 919107028)

28Then they called out to Yahweh in their trouble, and he brought them out of their distress.


## Psalms 107:29 (id: 919107029)

29He calmed the storm, and the waves were stilled.


## Psalms 107:30 (id: 919107030)

30Then they rejoiced because they are quiet, so he brought them to their desired harbor.


## Psalms 107:31 (id: 919107031)

31Oh that people would praise Yahweh for his covenant faithfulness and for the amazing things he has done for humanity!


## Psalms 107:32 (id: 919107032)

32Let them exalt him in the assembly of the people and praise him in the council of the elders.


## Psalms 107:33 (id: 919107033)

33He turns rivers into a wilderness, springs of water into dry land,


## Psalms 107:34 (id: 919107034)

34and a fruitful land into a barren place because of the wickedness of those who dwell in it.


## Psalms 107:35 (id: 919107035)

35He turns the wilderness into a pool of water and dry land into springs of water.


## Psalms 107:36 (id: 919107036)

36He settles the hungry there, and they build a city to live in.


## Psalms 107:37 (id: 919107037)

37They sow fields and plant vineyards, that they may bring in a fruitful harvest.


## Psalms 107:38 (id: 919107038)

38He blesses them so they are very numerous. He does not let their cattle decrease in number.


## Psalms 107:39 (id: 919107039)

39They were diminished and brought low by painful distress and suffering.


## Psalms 107:40 (id: 919107040)

40He pours contempt on the leaders and causes them to wander in the wilderness, where there are no roads.


## Psalms 107:41 (id: 919107041)

41But he protects the needy from affliction and cares for his families like a flock.


## Psalms 107:42 (id: 919107042)

42The upright will see this and rejoice, and all wickedness shuts its mouth.


## Psalms 107:43 (id: 919107043)

43Whoever is wise should take note of these things and meditate on Yahweh’s acts of covenant faithfulness.


## Psalms 108:1 (id: 919108001)

1A song, a psalm of David. My heart is fixed, God; I will sing, yes, I will sing praises also with my honored heart.


## Psalms 108:2 (id: 919108002)

2Wake up, lute and harp; I will wake up the dawn.


## Psalms 108:3 (id: 919108003)

3I will give thanks to you, Yahweh, among the peoples; I will sing praises to you among the nations.


## Psalms 108:4 (id: 919108004)

4For your covenant faithfulness is great above the heavens; and your trustworthiness reaches to the skies.


## Psalms 108:5 (id: 919108005)

5Be exalted, God, above the heavens, and may your glory be exalted over all the earth.


## Psalms 108:6 (id: 919108006)

6So that those you love may be rescued, rescue us with your right hand and answer me.


## Psalms 108:7 (id: 919108007)

7God has spoken in his holiness; “I will rejoice; I will divide Shechem and apportion out the Valley of Succoth.


## Psalms 108:8 (id: 919108008)

8Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is my helmet; Judah is my scepter.


## Psalms 108:9 (id: 919108009)

9Moab is my washbasin; over Edom I will throw my shoe; I will shout in triumph because of Philistia.


## Psalms 108:10 (id: 919108010)

10Who will bring me into the strong city? Who will lead me to Edom?”


## Psalms 108:11 (id: 919108011)

11God, have you not rejected us? You do not go into battle with our army.


## Psalms 108:12 (id: 919108012)

12Give us help against the enemy, for man’s help is futile.


## Psalms 108:13 (id: 919108013)

13We will triumph with God’s help; he will trample down our enemies.


## Psalms 109:1 (id: 919109001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. To the chief musician. A Psalm of David. God whom I praise, do not be silent,


## Psalms 109:2 (id: 919109002)

2For the wicked and deceitful attack me; they speak lies against me.


## Psalms 109:3 (id: 919109003)

3They surround me and say hateful things, and they attack me without cause.


## Psalms 109:4 (id: 919109004)

4In return for my love they accuse me, but I pray for them.


## Psalms 109:5 (id: 919109005)

5They repay me evil for good, and they hate my love.


## Psalms 109:6 (id: 919109006)

6Appoint a wicked man over such an enemy as these people; appoint an accuser to stand at his right hand.


## Psalms 109:7 (id: 919109007)

7When he is judged, may he be found guilty; may his prayer be considered sinful.


## Psalms 109:8 (id: 919109008)

8May his days be few; may another take his office.


## Psalms 109:9 (id: 919109009)

9May his children be fatherless, and may his wife be a widow.


## Psalms 109:10 (id: 919109010)

10May his children wander about and beg, asking for handouts as they leave their ruined home.


## Psalms 109:11 (id: 919109011)

11May the creditor take all he owns; may strangers plunder what he earns.


## Psalms 109:12 (id: 919109012)

12May no one extend any kindness to him; may no one have pity on his fatherless children.


## Psalms 109:13 (id: 919109013)

13May his children be cut off; may their name be blotted out in the next generation.


## Psalms 109:14 (id: 919109014)

14May his ancestors’ sins be mentioned to Yahweh; and may the sin of his mother not be forgotten.


## Psalms 109:15 (id: 919109015)

15May their guilt always be before Yahweh; may Yahweh cut off their memory from the earth.


## Psalms 109:16 (id: 919109016)

16May Yahweh do this because this man never bothered to show any covenant faithfulness, but instead harassed the oppressed, the needy, and the disheartened to death.


## Psalms 109:17 (id: 919109017)

17He loved cursing; may it come back upon him. He had no desire for blessing; may no blessing come to him.


## Psalms 109:18 (id: 919109018)

18He clothed himself with cursing as his garment, and his curse came into his inner being like water, like oil into his bones.


## Psalms 109:19 (id: 919109019)

19May his curses be to him like the clothes he wears to cover himself, like the belt he always wears.


## Psalms 109:20 (id: 919109020)

20May this be the reward of my accusers from Yahweh, of those who say evil things about me.


## Psalms 109:21 (id: 919109021)

21Yahweh my Lord, deal kindly with me for your name’s sake. Because your covenant faithfulness is good, save me.


## Psalms 109:22 (id: 919109022)

22For I am oppressed and needy, and my heart is wounded within me.


## Psalms 109:23 (id: 919109023)

23I am fading away like the shadow of the evening; I am shaken off like a locust.


## Psalms 109:24 (id: 919109024)

24My knees are weak from fasting; My flesh is feeble from lack of fatness.


## Psalms 109:25 (id: 919109025)

25I am disdained by my accusers; when they see me, they shake their heads.


## Psalms 109:26 (id: 919109026)

26Help me, Yahweh my God; save me by your covenant faithfulness.


## Psalms 109:27 (id: 919109027)

27May they know that this is your hand, that you, Yahweh, have done this.


## Psalms 109:28 (id: 919109028)

28Though they curse me, please bless me; when they attack, may they be put to shame, but may your servant rejoice.


## Psalms 109:29 (id: 919109029)

29May my adversaries be clothed with shame; may they wear their shame like a robe.


## Psalms 109:30 (id: 919109030)

30With my mouth I give great thanks to Yahweh; I will praise him in the midst of a crowd.


## Psalms 109:31 (id: 919109031)

31For he will stand at the right hand of the one who is needy, to save him from those who judge him.


## Psalms 110:1 (id: 919110001)

1A psalm of David. Of David, a song. The declaration of Yahweh to my lord, “Sit at my right hand until I make your enemies a footstool for your feet.”


## Psalms 110:2 (id: 919110002)

2Yahweh will stretch out the scepter of your strength from Zion; rule in the midst of your enemies.


## Psalms 110:3 (id: 919110003)

3Your people voluntarily follow in holy splendor in the day of your strength; from the womb of the dawn your youth will be to you as dew.


## Psalms 110:4 (id: 919110004)

4Yahweh has sworn, and will not change his mind: “You are a priest forever, after the manner of Melchizedek.”


## Psalms 110:5 (id: 919110005)

5The Lord is at your right hand. He will crush kings on the day of his anger.


## Psalms 110:6 (id: 919110006)

6He will judge the nations; he will fill corpses; he will crush the heads of many lands.


## Psalms 110:7 (id: 919110007)

7He will drink from the stream along the path, Therefore, he will lift up the head.


## Psalms 111:1 (id: 919111001)

1Praise Yahweh. I will give thanks to Yahweh with my whole heart in the assembly of the upright, in their gathering.


## Psalms 111:2 (id: 919111002)

2The works of Yahweh are great, eagerly awaited by all those who desire them.


## Psalms 111:3 (id: 919111003)

3His work is majestic and glorious, and his righteousness endures forever.


## Psalms 111:4 (id: 919111004)

4He does wonderful things that will be remembered; Yahweh is gracious and merciful.


## Psalms 111:5 (id: 919111005)

5He gives food to his faithful followers. He will always call to mind his covenant.


## Psalms 111:6 (id: 919111006)

6He showed his powerful works to his people in giving them the inheritance of the nations.


## Psalms 111:7 (id: 919111007)

7The works of his hands are trustworthy and just; all his instructions are reliable.


## Psalms 111:8 (id: 919111008)

8They are established forever, to be observed faithfully and properly.


## Psalms 111:9 (id: 919111009)

9He has sent redemption to his people; he ordained his covenant forever; holy and awesome is his name.


## Psalms 111:10 (id: 919111010)

10To honor Yahweh is the beginning of wisdom; those who carry out his instructions have good understanding. His praise endures forever.


## Psalms 112:1 (id: 919112001)

1Praise Yahweh. Blessed is the man who fears Yahweh, who greatly delights in his commandments.


## Psalms 112:2 (id: 919112002)

2His descendants will be powerful on earth; the descendants of the godly man will be blessed.


## Psalms 112:3 (id: 919112003)

3Wealth and riches are in his house; his righteousness will endure forever.


## Psalms 112:4 (id: 919112004)

4Light shines in the darkness for the godly person; he is gracious, merciful, and just.


## Psalms 112:5 (id: 919112005)

5It goes well for the man who deals graciously and lends money, who conducts his affairs with honesty.


## Psalms 112:6 (id: 919112006)

6For he will never be moved; the righteous person will be remembered forever.


## Psalms 112:7 (id: 919112007)

7He does not fear bad news; his heart is sure, trusting in Yahweh.


## Psalms 112:8 (id: 919112008)

8His heart is tranquil, without fear, until he looks in triumph over his adversaries.


## Psalms 112:9 (id: 919112009)

9He generously gives to the poor; his righteousness endures forever; he will be exalted with honor.


## Psalms 112:10 (id: 919112010)

10The wicked person will see this and be angry; he will grind his teeth in rage and he will melt away; the desire of the wicked people will perish.


## Psalms 113:1 (id: 919113001)

1Praise Yahweh. Praise him, you servants of Yahweh; praise the name of Yahweh.


## Psalms 113:2 (id: 919113002)

2Blessed be the name of Yahweh, both now and forevermore.


## Psalms 113:3 (id: 919113003)

3From the rising of the sun to its setting, Yahweh’s name should be praised.


## Psalms 113:4 (id: 919113004)

4Yahweh is exalted above all nations, and his glory reaches above the skies.


## Psalms 113:5 (id: 919113005)

5Who is like Yahweh our God, who has his seat on high,


## Psalms 113:6 (id: 919113006)

6who looks down at the sky and at the earth?


## Psalms 113:7 (id: 919113007)

7He raises up the poor out of the dirt and lifts up the needy from the ash heap,


## Psalms 113:8 (id: 919113008)

8so that he may seat him with princes, with the princes of his people.


## Psalms 113:9 (id: 919113009)

9He gives a home to the barren woman of the house, he makes her a joyful mother of children. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 114:1 (id: 919114001)

1When Israel left Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people who spoke a foreign language,


## Psalms 114:2 (id: 919114002)

2Judah became his holy place, Israel his kingdom.


## Psalms 114:3 (id: 919114003)

3The sea looked and fled; the Jordan turned back.


## Psalms 114:4 (id: 919114004)

4The mountains skipped like rams, the little hills like lambs.


## Psalms 114:5 (id: 919114005)

5Why did you flee, sea? Jordan, why did you turn back?


## Psalms 114:6 (id: 919114006)

6Mountains, why did you skip like rams? You little hills, why did you skip like lambs?


## Psalms 114:7 (id: 919114007)

7Tremble, earth, before the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 114:8 (id: 919114008)

8He turned the rock into a pool of water, the hard rock into a spring of water.


## Psalms 115:1 (id: 919115001)

1Not to us, Yahweh, not to us, but to your name bring honor, for your covenant faithfulness and for your trustworthiness.


## Psalms 115:2 (id: 919115002)

2Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?”


## Psalms 115:3 (id: 919115003)

3Our God is in heaven; he does whatever he pleases.


## Psalms 115:4 (id: 919115004)

4The nations’ idols are silver and gold, the work of men’s hands.


## Psalms 115:5 (id: 919115005)

5Those idols have mouths, but they do not speak; they have eyes, but they do not see;


## Psalms 115:6 (id: 919115006)

6they have ears, but they do not hear; they have noses, but they do not smell.


## Psalms 115:7 (id: 919115007)

7Those idols have hands, but do not feel; they have feet, but they cannot walk; nor do they speak from their mouths.


## Psalms 115:8 (id: 919115008)

8Those who make them are like them, as is everyone who trusts in them.


## Psalms 115:9 (id: 919115009)

9Israel, trust in Yahweh; he is your help and shield.


## Psalms 115:10 (id: 919115010)

10House of Aaron, trust in Yahweh; he is your help and shield.


## Psalms 115:11 (id: 919115011)

11You who honor Yahweh, trust in him; he is your help and shield.


## Psalms 115:12 (id: 919115012)

12Yahweh takes notice of us and will bless us; he will bless the family of Israel; he will bless the family of Aaron.


## Psalms 115:13 (id: 919115013)

13He will bless those who honor him, both young and old.


## Psalms 115:14 (id: 919115014)

14May Yahweh increase your numbers more and more, yours and your descendants’.


## Psalms 115:15 (id: 919115015)

15May you be blessed by Yahweh, who made heaven and earth.


## Psalms 115:16 (id: 919115016)

16The heavens, even the heavens belong to Yahweh; but the earth he has given to the sons of men.


## Psalms 115:17 (id: 919115017)

17The dead do not praise Yahweh, nor do any who go down into silence;


## Psalms 115:18 (id: 919115018)

18But we will bless Yahweh now and forevermore. Praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 116:1 (id: 919116001)

1I love Yahweh because he hears my voice and my pleas for mercy.


## Psalms 116:2 (id: 919116002)

2Because he listened to me, I will call on him as long as I live.


## Psalms 116:3 (id: 919116003)

3The cords of death surrounded me, and the snares of Sheol confronted me; I felt anguish and sorrow.


## Psalms 116:4 (id: 919116004)

4Then I called on the name of Yahweh: “Please Yahweh, rescue my life.”


## Psalms 116:5 (id: 919116005)

5Yahweh is merciful and fair; our God is compassionate.


## Psalms 116:6 (id: 919116006)

6Yahweh protects the naive; I was brought low, and he saved me.


## Psalms 116:7 (id: 919116007)

7My soul can return to its resting place, for Yahweh has been good to me.


## Psalms 116:8 (id: 919116008)

8For you rescued my life from death, my eyes from tears, and my feet from stumbling.


## Psalms 116:9 (id: 919116009)

9I will walk before Yahweh in the land of the living.


## Psalms 116:10 (id: 919116010)

10I believed in him, even when I said, “I am greatly afflicted.”


## Psalms 116:11 (id: 919116011)

11In my confusion I said, “All men are liars.”


## Psalms 116:12 (id: 919116012)

12How can I repay Yahweh for all his kindnesses to me?


## Psalms 116:13 (id: 919116013)

13I will raise the cup of salvation, and call on the name of Yahweh.


## Psalms 116:14 (id: 919116014)

14I will fulfill my vows to Yahweh now in the presence of all his people.


## Psalms 116:15 (id: 919116015)

15Precious in the sight of Yahweh is the death of his faithful ones.


## Psalms 116:16 (id: 919116016)

16Yahweh, indeed, I am your servant; I am your servant, the son of your servant woman; you have taken away my bonds.


## Psalms 116:17 (id: 919116017)

17I will offer to you the sacrifice of thanksgiving and will call on the name of Yahweh.


## Psalms 116:18 (id: 919116018)

18I will fulfill my vows to Yahweh now in the presence of all his people,


## Psalms 116:19 (id: 919116019)

19in the courts of Yahweh’s house, in your midst, Jerusalem. Praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 117:1 (id: 919117001)

1Praise Yahweh, all you nations; exalt him, all you peoples.


## Psalms 117:2 (id: 919117002)

2For his covenant faithfulness is great toward us, and the trustworthiness of Yahweh endures forever. Praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 118:1 (id: 919118001)

1Give thanks to Yahweh, for he is good, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.


## Psalms 118:2 (id: 919118002)

2Let Israel now say, “His covenant faithfulness endures forever.”


## Psalms 118:3 (id: 919118003)

3Let the house of Aaron now say, “His covenant faithfulness endures forever.”


## Psalms 118:4 (id: 919118004)

4Let the loyal followers of Yahweh say, “His covenant faithfulness endures for ever.”


## Psalms 118:5 (id: 919118005)

5In my distress I called out to Yahweh; Yahweh answered me and set me free.


## Psalms 118:6 (id: 919118006)

6Yahweh is with me; I will not be afraid; what can man do to me?


## Psalms 118:7 (id: 919118007)

7Yahweh is on my side as my helper; I will look in triumph on those who hate me.


## Psalms 118:8 (id: 919118008)

8It is better to take shelter in Yahweh than to put confidence in man.


## Psalms 118:9 (id: 919118009)

9It is better to take refuge in Yahweh than to put one’s trust in a princes.


## Psalms 118:10 (id: 919118010)

10All the nations surrounded me; in Yahweh’s name I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:11 (id: 919118011)

11They surrounded me; yes, they surrounded me; in Yahweh’s name I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:12 (id: 919118012)

12They surrounded me like bees; they disappeared as quickly as fire among thorns; in Yahweh’s name I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:13 (id: 919118013)

13They attacked me to knock me down, but Yahweh helped me.


## Psalms 118:14 (id: 919118014)

14Yahweh is my strength and song, and he is the one who rescues me.


## Psalms 118:15 (id: 919118015)

15The joyful shout of victory is heard in the tents of the righteous; the right hand of Yahweh does valiantly.


## Psalms 118:16 (id: 919118016)

16The right hand of Yahweh is exalted; the right hand of Yahweh does valiantly.


## Psalms 118:17 (id: 919118017)

17I will not die, but live and declare the deeds of Yahweh.


## Psalms 118:18 (id: 919118018)

18Yahweh has punished me harshly; but he has not handed me over to death.


## Psalms 118:19 (id: 919118019)

19Open to me the gates of righteousness; I will enter them and I will give thanks to Yahweh.


## Psalms 118:20 (id: 919118020)

20This is the gate of Yahweh; the righteous enter through it.


## Psalms 118:21 (id: 919118021)

21I will give thanks to you, for you answered me, and you have become my salvation.


## Psalms 118:22 (id: 919118022)

22The stone that the builders rejected has become the chief cornerstone.


## Psalms 118:23 (id: 919118023)

23This is Yahweh’s doing; it is marvelous in our eyes.


## Psalms 118:24 (id: 919118024)

24This is the day on which Yahweh has acted; we will rejoice and be glad in it.


## Psalms 118:25 (id: 919118025)

25Please, Yahweh, give us victory! Please, Yahweh, send now success!


## Psalms 118:26 (id: 919118026)

26Blessed is he who comes in the name of Yahweh; we bless you from the house of Yahweh.


## Psalms 118:27 (id: 919118027)

27Yahweh is God, and he has given us light; bind the sacrifice with cords to the horns of the altar.


## Psalms 118:28 (id: 919118028)

28You are my God, and I will give thanks to you; you are my God; I will exalt you.


## Psalms 118:29 (id: 919118029)

29Oh, give thanks to Yahweh; for he is good; for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.


## Psalms 119:1 (id: 919119001)

1Blessed are those whose ways are blameless, who walk in the teaching of Yahweh.


## Psalms 119:2 (id: 919119002)

2Blessed are they who keep his testimonies, who seek him with all their heart.


## Psalms 119:3 (id: 919119003)

3Surely they do not practice injustice; they walk in his ways.


## Psalms 119:4 (id: 919119004)

4You have commanded your instructions so that we should carefully observe them.


## Psalms 119:5 (id: 919119005)

5Oh, that my path would be firmly established, keeping your statutes!


## Psalms 119:6 (id: 919119006)

6Then I would not be ashamed when I look to all of your commandments.


## Psalms 119:7 (id: 919119007)

7I will give thanks to you with an upright heart when I learn the judgments of your righteousness.


## Psalms 119:8 (id: 919119008)

8I will keep your statutes; do not utterly leave me.


## Psalms 119:9 (id: 919119009)

9How can a young man keep his path pure? By keeping your word.


## Psalms 119:10 (id: 919119010)

10With my whole heart I seek you; Do not let me stray from your commandments.


## Psalms 119:11 (id: 919119011)

11I have hidden your word in my heart so that I might not sin against you.


## Psalms 119:12 (id: 919119012)

12Blessed you are, Yahweh; teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:13 (id: 919119013)

13With my lips I have announced all the judgments of your mouth.


## Psalms 119:14 (id: 919119014)

14I rejoice in the way of your testimonies more than in all riches.


## Psalms 119:15 (id: 919119015)

15I will meditate on your instructions and I will consider your paths.


## Psalms 119:16 (id: 919119016)

16I delight in your statutes; I will not forget your word.


## Psalms 119:17 (id: 919119017)

17Deal kindly with your servant so that I may live and keep your word.


## Psalms 119:18 (id: 919119018)

18Uncover my eyes so that I may gaze on the marvelous works from your teaching.


## Psalms 119:19 (id: 919119019)

19I am a foreigner in the land; do not hide your commandments from me.


## Psalms 119:20 (id: 919119020)

20My inner being is crushed with longing for your judgments at all times.


## Psalms 119:21 (id: 919119021)

21You rebuke the proud, who are cursed, who wander from your commandments.


## Psalms 119:22 (id: 919119022)

22Spare me from disgrace and humiliation, for I have kept your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:23 (id: 919119023)

23Even though rulers sit against me and slander, your servant meditates on your statutes.


## Psalms 119:24 (id: 919119024)

24Also, your testimonies are my pleasure. They are my counselors.


## Psalms 119:25 (id: 919119025)

25My inner being clings to the dust! Give me life according to your word.


## Psalms 119:26 (id: 919119026)

26I recounted my ways, and you answered me. Teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:27 (id: 919119027)

27Make me understand the way of your instructions, so that I can meditate on your wondrous works.


## Psalms 119:28 (id: 919119028)

28My inner being melts away from grief Lift me up by your word.


## Psalms 119:29 (id: 919119029)

29Turn from me the path of deceit; graciously give me your teaching.


## Psalms 119:30 (id: 919119030)

30I have chosen the way of faithfulness; I have desired your judgments.


## Psalms 119:31 (id: 919119031)

31I cling to your testimonies; Yahweh, do not let me be shamed.


## Psalms 119:32 (id: 919119032)

32I run in the way of your commandments, for you enlarge my heart.


## Psalms 119:33 (id: 919119033)

33Teach me, Yahweh, the way of your statutes, and I will keep it to the end.


## Psalms 119:34 (id: 919119034)

34Give me understanding, and I will keep your teaching; I will observe it with all my heart.


## Psalms 119:35 (id: 919119035)

35Guide me in the way of your commandments, for I delight in it.


## Psalms 119:36 (id: 919119036)

36Incline my heart toward your testimonies and not toward unrighteous gain.


## Psalms 119:37 (id: 919119037)

37Turn away my eyes from looking at worthless things; in your ways, revive me.


## Psalms 119:38 (id: 919119038)

38Fulfill for your servant your promises. that he may fear you.


## Psalms 119:39 (id: 919119039)

39Turn away the reproach that I dread, for your judgments are good.


## Psalms 119:40 (id: 919119040)

40Look, I long for your precepts; in your righteousness, revive me.


## Psalms 119:41 (id: 919119041)

41May your steadfast love come, oh Yahweh— your salvation, according to your promise;


## Psalms 119:42 (id: 919119042)

42then I will answer the one who mocks me with a word, for I trust in your word.


## Psalms 119:43 (id: 919119043)

43Do not utterly take the word of truth from my mouth, for I hope in your judgments.


## Psalms 119:44 (id: 919119044)

44I will observe your teaching continually, forever and ever.


## Psalms 119:45 (id: 919119045)

45I will walk in a broad path, for I seek your precepts.


## Psalms 119:46 (id: 919119046)

46I will speak of your testimonies before kings, and I will not be ashamed.


## Psalms 119:47 (id: 919119047)

47I delight in your commandments, which I love.


## Psalms 119:48 (id: 919119048)

48I will lift up my hands to your commandments, which I love; I will meditate on your statutes.


## Psalms 119:49 (id: 919119049)

49Remember your word to your servant because you have given me hope.


## Psalms 119:50 (id: 919119050)

50This is my comfort in my affliction: that your promise keeps me alive.


## Psalms 119:51 (id: 919119051)

51The proud utterly scoff at me, from your teaching I do not turned aside.


## Psalms 119:52 (id: 919119052)

52I remember your judgments from ancient times, Yahweh, and I comfort myself.


## Psalms 119:53 (id: 919119053)

53Hot anger has seized me because of the wicked who reject your teaching.


## Psalms 119:54 (id: 919119054)

54Your statutes are songs for me in the house where I temporarily live.


## Psalms 119:55 (id: 919119055)

55I remember your name during the night, Yahweh, and I observe your teaching.


## Psalms 119:56 (id: 919119056)

56This is for me because I keep your precepts.


## Psalms 119:57 (id: 919119057)

57Yahweh is my portion; I promise to observe your words.


## Psalms 119:58 (id: 919119058)

58I entreat your favor with my whole heart; be merciful to me according to your promises.


## Psalms 119:59 (id: 919119059)

59I examine my ways and turn my feet to your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:60 (id: 919119060)

60I hurry and do not delay to observe your commandments.


## Psalms 119:61 (id: 919119061)

61The cords of the wicked ensnare me; I do not forget your teaching.


## Psalms 119:62 (id: 919119062)

62In the middle of the night I rise to bring praise to you because of the judgments of your righteousness.


## Psalms 119:63 (id: 919119063)

63I am a companion to all who fear you, and observe your precepts.


## Psalms 119:64 (id: 919119064)

64The earth is full of your steadfast love, Yahweh; teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:65 (id: 919119065)

65You do good to your servant, Yahweh, according to your word.


## Psalms 119:66 (id: 919119066)

66Teach me good discernment and understanding, for I trust in your commandments.


## Psalms 119:67 (id: 919119067)

67Before I was afflicted I went astray, but now I observe your promises.


## Psalms 119:68 (id: 919119068)

68You are good, and you do good. Teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:69 (id: 919119069)

69The arrogant smear me with lies, but I myself keep your precepts with my whole heart.


## Psalms 119:70 (id: 919119070)

70Their hearts are unfeeling like fat, but I myself delight in your teaching.


## Psalms 119:71 (id: 919119071)

71It is good for me that I have suffered so that I would learn your statutes.


## Psalms 119:72 (id: 919119072)

72The teaching of your mouth is good to me, more than thousands of pieces of gold and silver.


## Psalms 119:73 (id: 919119073)

73Your hands have made me and fashioned me; give me understanding so that I may learn your commandments.


## Psalms 119:74 (id: 919119074)

74May those who fear you see me and rejoice because I hope in your word.


## Psalms 119:75 (id: 919119075)

75Yahweh, I know that your judgments are just, and in faithfulness you humble me.


## Psalms 119:76 (id: 919119076)

76Let your steadfast love be my comfort, just as your promises to your servant.


## Psalms 119:77 (id: 919119077)

77May your grace come to me so that I may live, for your teaching is my delight.


## Psalms 119:78 (id: 919119078)

78Let the proud be put to shame, for they have accused me falsely; but as for me, I will meditate on your precepts.


## Psalms 119:79 (id: 919119079)

79May those who fear you turn to me, also those who know your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:80 (id: 919119080)

80May my heart be blameless with respect to your statutes, so that I may not be put to shame.


## Psalms 119:81 (id: 919119081)

81My inner being faints with longing for your salvation! I hope for your word.


## Psalms 119:82 (id: 919119082)

82My eyes faint with longing for your promise; saying, "When will you comfort me?"


## Psalms 119:83 (id: 919119083)

83For I have become like a wineskin in the smoke; I do not forget your statutes.


## Psalms 119:84 (id: 919119084)

84How long must your servant endure this; when will you act in pursuit of justice for me?


## Psalms 119:85 (id: 919119085)

85The proud have dug pits for me, which is not according to your teaching.


## Psalms 119:86 (id: 919119086)

86All your commandments are true; they pursue me deceifully; help me.


## Psalms 119:87 (id: 919119087)

87They have almost made an end to me in the land, but as for me, I do not reject your instructions.


## Psalms 119:88 (id: 919119088)

88According to your steadfast love, keep me alive, so that I may observe the testimonies of your mouth.


## Psalms 119:89 (id: 919119089)

89Forever, Yahweh, your word stands in the heavens.


## Psalms 119:90 (id: 919119090)

90Your faithfulness lasts from generation to generation; you have established the earth, and it stands.


## Psalms 119:91 (id: 919119091)

91They stand for your judgments today, for all things are your servants.


## Psalms 119:92 (id: 919119092)

92If your teaching had not been my delight, then I would have perished in my affliction.


## Psalms 119:93 (id: 919119093)

93I will not forget your precepts forever, for through them you have preserved me alive.


## Psalms 119:94 (id: 919119094)

94I am yours; save me, for I seek your precepts.


## Psalms 119:95 (id: 919119095)

95The wicked wait for me in order to destroy me, but I seek to understand your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:96 (id: 919119096)

96I have seen an end for all perfection; your commandments are very broad.


## Psalms 119:97 (id: 919119097)

97Oh how I love your teaching! It is my meditation all day long.


## Psalms 119:98 (id: 919119098)

98Your commandments make me wiser than my enemies, for it is with me forever.


## Psalms 119:99 (id: 919119099)

99I have more understanding than all my teachers, for your testimonies are my meditation.


## Psalms 119:100 (id: 919119100)

100I understand more than the elders; for I have kept your precepts.


## Psalms 119:101 (id: 919119101)

101I have restrained my feet from every path of evil so that I might observe your word.


## Psalms 119:102 (id: 919119102)

102I have not turned aside from your judgments, for you alone have instructed me.


## Psalms 119:103 (id: 919119103)

103How sweet are your promises to my taste, yes, sweeter than honey to my mouth!


## Psalms 119:104 (id: 919119104)

104Through your precepts I gain understanding; therefore I hate every path of falsehood.


## Psalms 119:105 (id: 919119105)

105Your word is a lamp to my feet and a light for my path.


## Psalms 119:106 (id: 919119106)

106I have sworn and have confirmed it, that I will observe your righteous judgments.


## Psalms 119:107 (id: 919119107)

107I am very afflicted; keep me alive, Yahweh, according to your word.


## Psalms 119:108 (id: 919119108)

108Yahweh, please accept the freewill offerings of my mouth, and teach me your judgments.


## Psalms 119:109 (id: 919119109)

109My life is in my palm continually, yet I do not forget your teaching.


## Psalms 119:110 (id: 919119110)

110The wicked have set a snare for me, but I have not strayed from your precepts.


## Psalms 119:111 (id: 919119111)

111I claim your testimonies as my heritage forever, for they are the joy of my heart.


## Psalms 119:112 (id: 919119112)

112I incline my heart to do your statutes forever, to the end!


## Psalms 119:113 (id: 919119113)

113I hate double\-minded people, but I love your teaching.


## Psalms 119:114 (id: 919119114)

114You are my hiding place and my shield; I hope in your word.


## Psalms 119:115 (id: 919119115)

115Get away from me, you evil doers, so that I may observe the commandments of my God.


## Psalms 119:116 (id: 919119116)

116Sustain me by your word so that I may live and do not make me ashamed of my expectation.


## Psalms 119:117 (id: 919119117)

117Sustain me, and I will be saved; And, I will gaze on your statutes continually.


## Psalms 119:118 (id: 919119118)

118You reject all those who stray from your statutes, for their deception is in vain.


## Psalms 119:119 (id: 919119119)

119You remove all the wicked of the earth like dross; therefore I love your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:120 (id: 919119120)

120My body trembles in fear of you, and I fear of your judgments.


## Psalms 119:121 (id: 919119121)

121I do justice and righteousness; do not abandon me to my oppressors.


## Psalms 119:122 (id: 919119122)

122Ensure goodness for your servant; do not let the proud oppress me.


## Psalms 119:123 (id: 919119123)

123My eyes faint for your salvation and for the promise of your righteousness.


## Psalms 119:124 (id: 919119124)

124Deal with your servant according to your steadfast love, and teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:125 (id: 919119125)

125I am your servant; give me understanding so that I may know your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:126 (id: 919119126)

126It is time for Yahweh to act, they break your teaching.


## Psalms 119:127 (id: 919119127)

127Therefore, I love your commandments more than gold, more than fine gold.


## Psalms 119:128 (id: 919119128)

128Therefore I consider all your precepts to be right in everything. I hate every path of falsehood.


## Psalms 119:129 (id: 919119129)

129Your testimonies are wonderful. Therefore, I obey them.


## Psalms 119:130 (id: 919119130)

130The unfolding of your words gives light; it gives understanding to the untrained.


## Psalms 119:131 (id: 919119131)

131I open my mouth and pant, for I long for your commandments.


## Psalms 119:132 (id: 919119132)

132Turn to me and be gracious to me according to justice, to those who love your name.


## Psalms 119:133 (id: 919119133)

133Establish my footsteps in your promises; and do not let any iniquity rule over me.


## Psalms 119:134 (id: 919119134)

134Ransom me from the oppression of man so that I may observe your precepts.


## Psalms 119:135 (id: 919119135)

135Let your face shine on your servant, and teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:136 (id: 919119136)

136Channels of water run down from my eyes because they do not observe your teaching.


## Psalms 119:137 (id: 919119137)

137You are righteous, Yahweh, and your judgments are upright.


## Psalms 119:138 (id: 919119138)

138You command your testimonies righteously and very faithfully.


## Psalms 119:139 (id: 919119139)

139My jealousy has destroyed me because my adversaries forget your words.


## Psalms 119:140 (id: 919119140)

140Your promise is well refined, and your servant loves it.


## Psalms 119:141 (id: 919119141)

141I am little and despised. I do not forget your instructions.


## Psalms 119:142 (id: 919119142)

142Your righteousness is right forever, and your instruction is true.


## Psalms 119:143 (id: 919119143)

143Distress and anguish have found me. your commandments are my delight.


## Psalms 119:144 (id: 919119144)

144Your testimonies are righteous forever; give me understanding that I may live.


## Psalms 119:145 (id: 919119145)

145I cried out with my whole heart, “Answer me, Yahweh, I will keep your statutes.


## Psalms 119:146 (id: 919119146)

146I call to you; save me, so that I may observe your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:147 (id: 919119147)

147I rise before the dawn and cry for help. I hope in your words.


## Psalms 119:148 (id: 919119148)

148My eyes are open during the night watches in order to meditate on your promise.


## Psalms 119:149 (id: 919119149)

149Hear my voice according to your steadfast love; Yahweh, according to your judgment preserve my life.


## Psalms 119:150 (id: 919119150)

150Those pursuing wickedness are coming near. They wander far from your teaching.


## Psalms 119:151 (id: 919119151)

151You are near, Yahweh, and all your commandments are true.


## Psalms 119:152 (id: 919119152)

152Long ago I learned from your testimonies that you had established them forever.


## Psalms 119:153 (id: 919119153)

153Look on my affliction and rescue me, for I do not forget your teaching.


## Psalms 119:154 (id: 919119154)

154Plead my cause and redeem me; preserve me for your promise.


## Psalms 119:155 (id: 919119155)

155Salvation is far from the wicked, for they do not pursue your statutes.


## Psalms 119:156 (id: 919119156)

156Your mercies are many, Yahweh; according to your judgments, preserve me.


## Psalms 119:157 (id: 919119157)

157My pursuers and my adversaries are many; from your testimonies I have not turned.


## Psalms 119:158 (id: 919119158)

158I see the treacherous and I despise it because they do not observe your promise.


## Psalms 119:159 (id: 919119159)

159See that I love your precepts; Yahweh, according to your steadfast love, preserve me.


## Psalms 119:160 (id: 919119160)

160The head of your word is truth, and all of your righteous judgments lasts forever.


## Psalms 119:161 (id: 919119161)

161Commanders pursue me without cause, but from your word my heart trembles


## Psalms 119:162 (id: 919119162)

162I rejoice on account of your promise, like one who finds great plunder.


## Psalms 119:163 (id: 919119163)

163I hate falsehood, and I loathe it. I love your instruction.


## Psalms 119:164 (id: 919119164)

164Seven times in a day I praise you on account of your righteous judgments.


## Psalms 119:165 (id: 919119165)

165Great peace is for those who love your instruction; there is no stumbling for them.


## Psalms 119:166 (id: 919119166)

166I wait for your salvation, Yahweh, and I do your commandments.


## Psalms 119:167 (id: 919119167)

167My life keeps your testimonies, and I love them greatly.


## Psalms 119:168 (id: 919119168)

168I keep your precepts and your testimonies, for all my ways are before you.


## Psalms 119:169 (id: 919119169)

169My plea comes near to your face, Yahweh; give me understanding into your word.


## Psalms 119:170 (id: 919119170)

170May my supplication come before your face; according to your promise, rescue me.


## Psalms 119:171 (id: 919119171)

171May my lips pour out praise, for you teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:172 (id: 919119172)

172Let my tongue sing about your promise, for all your commandments are right.


## Psalms 119:173 (id: 919119173)

173Let your hand be for my help, for I have chosen your precepts.


## Psalms 119:174 (id: 919119174)

174I long for your salvation, Yahweh, and your teaching is my delight.


## Psalms 119:175 (id: 919119175)

175May I live and praise you, and may your judgments help me.


## Psalms 119:176 (id: 919119176)

176I have wandered off like a lost sheep; seek your servant, for I have not forgotten your commandments.”

## Psalms 135:5 (id: 919135005)

5For I myself know that Yahweh is great, and our Lord is greater than all other gods.


## Psalms 135:6 (id: 919135006)

## Psalms 135:7 (id: 919135007)

7Causing the clouds to rise from the end of the earth, he makes lightning accompany the rain and bringing the wind out of his storehouse.

8He struck the firstborn of Egypt, from man to beast.


## Psalms 135:9 (id: 919135009)

## Psalms 135:10 (id: 919135010)

10He struck many nations and killed mighty kings,


## Psalms 135:11 (id: 919135011)

## Psalms 135:12 (id: 919135012)

## Psalms 135:13 (id: 919135013)

## Psalms 135:14 (id: 919135014)

14For Yahweh judges his people, and he shows compassion on his servants.

## Psalms 135:16 (id: 919135016)

## Psalms 135:17 (id: 919135017)

## Psalms 135:18 (id: 919135018)

## Psalms 136:5 (id: 919136005)

## Psalms 136:7 (id: 919136007)

8the sun to rule by day, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever—


## Psalms 136:9 (id: 919136009)

## Psalms 136:10 (id: 919136010)

## Psalms 136:11 (id: 919136011)

11and brought out Israel from among them, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever—


## Psalms 136:12 (id: 919136012)

12with a strong hand and a raised arm, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.

## Psalms 136:14 (id: 919136014)

14and made Israel to pass through the middle of it, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever—


## Psalms 136:15 (id: 919136015)

15and threw down Pharaoh and his army in the Sea of Reeds, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.


## Psalms 136:16 (id: 919136016)

16to him who led his people through the wilderness, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever—


## Psalms 136:17 (id: 919136017)

17to him who struck down great kings, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.


## Psalms 136:18 (id: 919136018)

18to him who killed powerful kings, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever—


## Psalms 136:19 (id: 919136019)

19Sihon king of the Amorites, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever—


## Psalms 136:20 (id: 919136020)

20and Og king of Bashan, for his covenant faithfulness endures forever.

## Psalms 136:22 (id: 919136022)

## Psalms 136:23 (id: 919136023)

## Psalms 137:1 (id: 919137001)

1Beside the rivers of Babylon there we sat and wept when we remembered Zion.


## Psalms 137:2 (id: 919137002)

2On the poplars there we hung our harps.


## Psalms 137:3 (id: 919137003)

3For there our captors demanded that we sing songs, and those who relentlessly mocked us said, “Sing to us from the songs of Zion.”


## Psalms 137:4 (id: 919137004)

4How could we sing a song about Yahweh in a foreign land?


## Psalms 137:5 (id: 919137005)

5If I forget you, Jerusalem, let my right hand forget


## Psalms 137:6 (id: 919137006)

## Psalms 137:7 (id: 919137007)

7Remember, Yahweh, the sons of Edom, on the day of Jerusalem, saying, “Tear it down, tear it down to its foundations.”


## Psalms 137:8 (id: 919137008)
