## Psalms 137:9 (id: 919137009)

9Blessed be the one who seizes and dashes your little ones against the rocks.


## Psalms 138:1 (id: 919138001)

1A psalm of David. Of David I will give you thanks with my whole heart; before the gods I will sing praises to you.


## Psalms 138:2 (id: 919138002)

2I will bow down toward the temple of your holiness, and I will give thanks to your name for your covenant faithfulness and for your trustworthiness. For you have exalted above all things your name and your word.


## Psalms 138:3 (id: 919138003)

3On the day that I called and you answered me; you emboldened my life with power.


## Psalms 138:4 (id: 919138004)

4All the kings of the earth will give you thanks, Yahweh, for they will hear the words from your mouth.


## Psalms 138:5 (id: 919138005)

5Indeed, they will sing of the ways of Yahweh, for great is the glory of Yahweh.


## Psalms 138:6 (id: 919138006)

6For though Yahweh is high, yet he sees the lowly, but the proud he knows from far off.


## Psalms 138:7 (id: 919138007)

7Though I walk in the middle of danger, you will preserve my life; you will reach out with your hand against the anger of my enemies, and your right hand will save me.


## Psalms 138:8 (id: 919138008)

8Yahweh is with me to the end; your covenant faithfulness, Yahweh, endures forever. Do not forsake the ones whom your hands have made.


## Psalms 139:1 (id: 919139001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. For the choir director, a psalm of David. Yahweh, you have examined me, and you know.


## Psalms 139:2 (id: 919139002)

2You know when I sit and when I rise; you understand my thoughts from far away.


## Psalms 139:3 (id: 919139003)

3You have measured my path and my resting places; and you are familiar with all my ways.


## Psalms 139:4 (id: 919139004)

4For there is not a word on my tongue ..., See, you know it completely, Yahweh.


## Psalms 139:5 (id: 919139005)

5Behind and before you encircle me and you place your hand upon me.


## Psalms 139:6 (id: 919139006)

6Such knowledge is too wonderful for me! it is high; I cannot reach it.


## Psalms 139:7 (id: 919139007)

7Where can I go from your Spirit? Where can I flee from your presence?


## Psalms 139:8 (id: 919139008)

8If I ascend up to the heavens, you are there; if I make my bed in Sheol, behold, you are there.


## Psalms 139:9 (id: 919139009)

9If I rise on the wings of the morning or dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea,


## Psalms 139:10 (id: 919139010)

10even there your hand will lead me, your right hand will hold on to me.


## Psalms 139:11 (id: 919139011)

11If I said, “Surely the darkness will cover me, and the light will become night around me,”


## Psalms 139:12 (id: 919139012)

12even the darkness would not be dark to you, and night would shine like the day. The darkness is like the light to you!


## Psalms 139:13 (id: 919139013)

13For You created my inner parts; you wove me together in my mother’s womb.


## Psalms 139:14 (id: 919139014)

14I will praise you because I am fearfully and wonderfully made. Your works are wonderful. My inner being knows this very well.


## Psalms 139:15 (id: 919139015)

15My bones were not hidden from you when I was made in private, when I was woven together in the depths of the earth.


## Psalms 139:16 (id: 919139016)

16Your eyes saw my unformed body; all the days formed for me were recorded in your book even before the first of them was.


## Psalms 139:17 (id: 919139017)

17How precious are your thoughts to me, God! How vast is their sum!


## Psalms 139:18 (id: 919139018)

18If I counted them, they would be more numberous than the sand. When I awake, I am still with you.


## Psalms 139:19 (id: 919139019)

19If only you would kill the wicked, God; and you men of bloodshed, get away from me.


## Psalms 139:20 (id: 919139020)

20For they speak against you with evil intent; your enemies abuse your character


## Psalms 139:21 (id: 919139021)

21Do I not hate those, Yahweh, who hate you? Do I not despise those who rise up against you?


## Psalms 139:22 (id: 919139022)

22I hate them completely; they have become my enemies.


## Psalms 139:23 (id: 919139023)

23Examine me, God, and know my heart; test me and know my thoughts.


## Psalms 139:24 (id: 919139024)

24See if there is any wicked way in me, and lead me in the path of forever.


## Psalms 140:1 (id: 919140001)

1For the chief musician. A psalm of David. Yahweh, rescue me from men of wickedness; preserve me from men of violence.


## Psalms 140:2 (id: 919140002)

2For they plan evil in their hearts; they assemble for battles every day.


## Psalms 140:3 (id: 919140003)

3Their tongues pierce like a serpent; vipers’ poison is on their lips. Selah


## Psalms 140:4 (id: 919140004)

4Keep me from the hands of the wicked, Yahweh; preserve me from men of violence who plan to push down my step.


## Psalms 140:5 (id: 919140005)

5The proud have set a trap for me; and with ropes they have spread a net by hand along the path; they have set snares for me. 


## Psalms 140:6 (id: 919140006)

6I said to Yahweh, “You are my God; Yahweh, give ear to my cries for mercy.”


## Psalms 140:7 (id: 919140007)

7Yahweh, my Lord, you are the strength of my salvation; you shield my head in the day of battle.


## Psalms 140:8 (id: 919140008)

8Yahweh, do not grant the desires of the wicked; do not promote their plots, they rise up 


## Psalms 140:9 (id: 919140009)

9Those who surround me raise their heads; let the mischief of their own lips cover them.


## Psalms 140:10 (id: 919140010)

10Let burning coals fall on them; throw them into the fire, into bottomless pits, never again will they rise.


## Psalms 140:11 (id: 919140011)

11May men of tongues not be established in the land; may evil hunt down the man of violence speedily.


## Psalms 140:12 (id: 919140012)

12I know that Yahweh will act with favor for the poor, justice to the needy.


## Psalms 140:13 (id: 919140013)

13Surely the righteous will praise your name; the upright will dwell before your face.


## Psalms 141:1 (id: 919141001)

1A psalm of David. A song of David Yahweh, I called out to you, "Come quickly to me. Give ear to my voice when I call to you."


## Psalms 141:2 (id: 919141002)

2May my prayer rise like incense to your face; may my lifted hands be like the evening sacrifice.


## Psalms 141:3 (id: 919141003)

3Yahweh, place a guard over my mouth; guard the door of my lips.


## Psalms 141:4 (id: 919141004)

4Do not let my heart bend toward any evil thing or participate in sinful activities with men who behave wickedly. May I not eat any of their delicacies.


## Psalms 141:5 (id: 919141005)

5Let a righteous person hit me; it will be a kindness. Let him correct me; it will be like oil on my head. May my head not refuse. For my prayer is always against their wicked deeds.


## Psalms 141:6 (id: 919141006)

6Their judges will stumble into the hands of craggy rocks; they will hear that my own words are pleasant.


## Psalms 141:7 (id: 919141007)

7“As when one plows and breaks up the ground, so our bones have been scattered at the mouth of Sheol.”


## Psalms 141:8 (id: 919141008)

8For my eyes are on you, Yahweh, Lord; in you I take refuge; do not abandon my life.


## Psalms 141:9 (id: 919141009)

9Keep me from the hands of the snare that they have laid for me, from the traps of evildoers.


## Psalms 141:10 (id: 919141010)

10Let the wicked fall into their own nets while I escape.


## Psalms 142:1 (id: 919142001)

1A maschil of David, when he was in the cave; a prayer. With my voice I cry out to Yahweh; with my voice I plead to Yahweh for favor.


## Psalms 142:2 (id: 919142002)

2I pour out my lament before him; I declare my troubles before him.


## Psalms 142:3 (id: 919142003)

3When my spirit is weak within me, you yourself know my path. Along this path I walk they have hidden a trap for me.


## Psalms 142:4 (id: 919142004)

4I look to my right and see that there is no one who cares for me. there is no refuge for me; no one looks after my life.


## Psalms 142:5 (id: 919142005)

5I called out to you, Yahweh; I said, “You are my refuge, my portion in the land of the living.


## Psalms 142:6 (id: 919142006)

6Listen to my cries, for I have been brought very low; rescue me from my pursuers, for they are stronger than I.


## Psalms 142:7 (id: 919142007)

7Bring my life out of prison in order to praise your name. The righteous will gather around me because you have been good to me.”


## Psalms 143:1 (id: 919143001)

1A psalm of David. A song of David Hear my prayer, Yahweh; listen to my pleas. On account of your faithfulness answer me in your righteousness!


## Psalms 143:2 (id: 919143002)

2Do not enter into judgment with your servant, for no one living is righteous before you.


## Psalms 143:3 (id: 919143003)

3For the enemy has pursued my being; he has crushed my life to the ground; he has made me to live in dark places like those dead a long time.


## Psalms 143:4 (id: 919143004)

4My breath is faint in me; my heart despairs within me.


## Psalms 143:5 (id: 919143005)

5I remember days from old; I meditate on all your works; I reflect on the works of your hands.


## Psalms 143:6 (id: 919143006)

6I spread my hands out to you; my soul thirsts for you as in a parched land. 


## Psalms 143:7 (id: 919143007)

7Answer me quickly, Yahweh, because my spirit faints. Do not hide your face from me, or I will become like those who go down into the pit.


## Psalms 143:8 (id: 919143008)

8Let me hear your covenant faithfulness in the morning, for I trust in you. Make known to me the way where I should walk, for I lift up my soul to you.


## Psalms 143:9 (id: 919143009)

9Rescue me from my enemies, Yahweh; I hide in you.


## Psalms 143:10 (id: 919143010)

10Teach me to do your good pleasures, for you are my God. May your spirit of goodness lead me in the land of uprightness.


## Psalms 143:11 (id: 919143011)

11Yahweh, for the sake of your name, keep me alive; in your righteousness bring my life out of trouble.


## Psalms 143:12 (id: 919143012)

12In your covenant faithfulness cut off my enemies and destroy all the enemies of my life, for I am your servant.


## Psalms 144:1 (id: 919144001)

1A psalm of David. Of David. Blessed be Yahweh, my rock, who trains my hands for war and my fingers for battle.


## Psalms 144:2 (id: 919144002)

2You are my steadfast love and my fortress, my high tower and the one who rescues me, my shield and the one in whom I take refuge, the one who subdues nations under me.


## Psalms 144:3 (id: 919144003)

3Yahweh, what is man that you take notice of him, the son of man that you think about him?


## Psalms 144:4 (id: 919144004)

4Man is like a breath; his days are like a passing shadow.


## Psalms 144:5 (id: 919144005)

5Yahweh, cause your sky to spread wide and come down; touch the mountains and make them smoke.


## Psalms 144:6 (id: 919144006)

6Shoot lightning and scatter them; send your bolts and disturb them.


## Psalms 144:7 (id: 919144007)

7Reach out your hand from above, deliver me and rescue me out of many waters, from the hand of sons of foreigners.


## Psalms 144:8 (id: 919144008)

8For their mouths speak lies, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood.


## Psalms 144:9 (id: 919144009)

9I will sing a new song to you, God; on a lute of ten strings I will play for you,


## Psalms 144:10 (id: 919144010)

10who gives salvation to kings, who rescues David your servant from an evil sword.


## Psalms 144:11 (id: 919144011)

11Rescue me and deliver me from the hand of sons of foreigners. For their mouths speak lies, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood.


## Psalms 144:12 (id: 919144012)

12May our sons be like plants who grow large in their youth and our daughters like carved corner pillars, resembling a palace.


## Psalms 144:13 (id: 919144013)

13May our storehouses be full with every kind of produce, and may our sheep produce thousands and ten thousands in our fields.


## Psalms 144:14 (id: 919144014)

14May our oxen have many young. No one will break through, no one will go out, and no one will cry in our streets.


## Psalms 144:15 (id: 919144015)

15Blessed is the people for whom this is so; blessed is the people for whom Yahweh is his God.


## Psalms 145:1 (id: 919145001)

1A psalm of praise. Of David. A song of David I will extol you, my God, the King; I will bless your name forever and ever.


## Psalms 145:2 (id: 919145002)

2Every day will I bless you; I will praise your name forever and ever.


## Psalms 145:3 (id: 919145003)

3Great is Yahweh and greatly to be praised; and his greatness cannot be measured.


## Psalms 145:4 (id: 919145004)

4Generation to generation will rejoice because of your deeds and they will proclaim your mighty actions.


## Psalms 145:5 (id: 919145005)

5On the glorious splendor of your majesty and on your marvelous deeds, I will meditate.


## Psalms 145:6 (id: 919145006)

6They will speak of the power of your awesome works, and I will declare your greatness.


## Psalms 145:7 (id: 919145007)

7They will celebrate the fame of your abounding goodness, and they will sing about your righteousness.


## Psalms 145:8 (id: 919145008)

8Yahweh is gracious and merciful, slow to anger and great in steadfast love.


## Psalms 145:9 (id: 919145009)

9Yahweh is good to all; and his abundant mercies are over all his works.


## Psalms 145:10 (id: 919145010)

10All you have made will give thanks to you, Yahweh; your faithful ones will bless you.


## Psalms 145:11 (id: 919145011)

11They will speak of the glory of your kingdom, and they will tell of your power.


## Psalms 145:12 (id: 919145012)

12Making known to the children of mankind his mighty deeds and the glorious splendor of his kingdom.


## Psalms 145:13 (id: 919145013)

13Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and your dominion endures throughout all generations.


## Psalms 145:14 (id: 919145014)

14Yahweh supports all who are falling and raises up all who are bent over.


## Psalms 145:15 (id: 919145015)

15The eyes of all wait for you; you give them their food in its time.


## Psalms 145:16 (id: 919145016)

16You open your hand and satisfy the desire of every living thing.


## Psalms 145:17 (id: 919145017)

17Yahweh is righteous in all his ways and faithful in all he does.


## Psalms 145:18 (id: 919145018)

18Yahweh is near to all who call to him, to all who call to him in truth.


## Psalms 145:19 (id: 919145019)

19He does the desire of those who fear him, and he hears their cry and saves them.


## Psalms 145:20 (id: 919145020)

20Yahweh keeps all those who love him, but he will destroy all the wicked.


## Psalms 145:21 (id: 919145021)

21My mouth speaks the praise of Yahweh; let all flesh bless his holy name forever and ever.

## Psalms 146:4 (id: 919146004)

## Psalms 146:5 (id: 919146005)

## Psalms 146:6 (id: 919146006)

## Psalms 146:8 (id: 919146008)

## Psalms 146:9 (id: 919146009)

## Psalms 147:1 (id: 919147001)

1Praise Yahweh! How good it is to sing praises to our God, how pleasant and suitable is a song of praise.


## Psalms 147:2 (id: 919147002)

2Yahweh builds up Jerusalem, he gathers the scattered people of Israel.


## Psalms 147:3 (id: 919147003)

3He heals the brokenhearted and binds up their wounds.


## Psalms 147:4 (id: 919147004)

4He counts the number of the stars; he gives names to all of them.


## Psalms 147:5 (id: 919147005)

5Great is our Lord and abounding in power, his understanding is without measure.


## Psalms 147:6 (id: 919147006)

6Yahweh lifts up the oppressed, he brings the wicked down to the ground.


## Psalms 147:7 (id: 919147007)

7Sing to Yahweh with thanksgiving, sing praises to our God with a harp.


## Psalms 147:8 (id: 919147008)

8He is the one who covers the heavens with clouds; he is the one who prepares rain for the earth; he is the one who causes the mountains to sprout with grass.


## Psalms 147:9 (id: 919147009)

9He gives food to the animals and to the children of the ravens when they call.


## Psalms 147:10 (id: 919147010)

10He does not delight in the strength of a horse, he does not enjoy the strong legs of a man.


## Psalms 147:11 (id: 919147011)

11Yahweh enjoys those who fear him, those who hope for his steadfast love.


## Psalms 147:12 (id: 919147012)

12Extol Yahweh, Jerusalem, praise your God, Zion.


## Psalms 147:13 (id: 919147013)

13For he strengthens the bars of your gates, he blesses your children in your midst.


## Psalms 147:14 (id: 919147014)

14He sets your borders with peace, he satisfies you with the finest of wheat.


## Psalms 147:15 (id: 919147015)

15He sends out his word to the land, his command runs with swiftness.


## Psalms 147:16 (id: 919147016)

16He makes the snow like wool, he scatters the frost like ashes.


## Psalms 147:17 (id: 919147017)

17He sends out his hail like crumbs, who can stand before his cold?


## Psalms 147:18 (id: 919147018)

18He sends out his command and melts them; he makes his wind blow, and the waters flow.


## Psalms 147:19 (id: 919147019)

19He proclaimed his word to Jacob, his statutes and his righteous decrees to Israel.


## Psalms 147:20 (id: 919147020)

20He has not done so with any other nation, and as for his judgments, they do not know them. Praise Yahweh.

## Psalms 148:6 (id: 919148006)

## Psalms 149:3 (id: 919149003)

## Psalms 149:4 (id: 919149004)

4For Yahweh takes pleasure in his people; he glorifies the humble with salvation.


## Psalms 149:5 (id: 919149005)

## Psalms 149:6 (id: 919149006)

6May the exaltation of God be in their throats and two\-edged swords in their hands


## Psalms 149:7 (id: 919149007)

## Psalms 149:8 (id: 919149008)

8to bind their kings with chains and their honored ones with iron shackles.


## Psalms 149:9 (id: 919149009)

1Praise Yahweh. Praise God in his holy place; praise him in the mighty heavens.


## Psalms 150:2 (id: 919150002)

2Praise him for his mighty acts; praise him for his surpassing greatness.


## Psalms 150:3 (id: 919150003)

3Praise him with the blast of the horn; praise him with lute and harp.


## Psalms 150:4 (id: 919150004)

## Psalms 150:5 (id: 919150005)

## Psalms 150:6 (id: 919150006)
